<br /><br />
3<br /><br />
PRODUCTION SHARING CONTRACT<br /><br />
<br /><br />
This Contract is made and entered into as of<br /><br />
<br /><br />
2001 by and between<br /><br />
<br /><br />
(1)<br /><br />
<br /><br />
The State of Georgia ("the State") represented by the State Agency for<br /><br />
Regulation of Oil and Gas Resources ("State Agency");<br /><br />
<br /><br />
(2)<br /><br />
<br /><br />
The Joint Stock National Oil Company Saknavtobi, a legal entity under<br /><br />
the laws of Georgia pursuant to the Charter of Saknavtobi and the Law<br /><br />
on Oil and Gas ("Georgian Oil");<br /><br />
<br /><br />
(3)<br /><br />
<br /><br />
National Petroleum Limited, a company organised and existing under the<br /><br />
laws of Bermuda ("Contractor");<br /><br />
<br /><br />
The State, Georgian Oil, and Contractor may individually be referred to as a<br /><br />
"Party" and collectively as the "Parties".<br /><br />
WITNESSETH:<br /><br />
<br /><br />
WHEREAS, Georgian Oil and Contractor have entered into a Production Sharing<br /><br />
Agreement dated June 9 1995, as amended by Addendum No 1 of June 20 1997 and<br /><br />
Addendum No 2 of August 21 1998 (the "Original Agreements"); and<br /><br />
WHEREAS, a certain licence, series 33, 34, 46,47, number 7, was issued<br /><br />
provisionally on behalf of the State by the Georgian Oil Department of the<br /><br />
Republic of Georgia on July 10 1995 in respect of the Contract Area; and<br /><br />
subsequently reissued by licence, series 33, 34, 46,47, number 0058, by the<br /><br />
Department for the Protection of Mineral Resources and Mining of the Ministry of<br /><br />
Environmental Protection on October 13 1995; and subsequently extended by the<br /><br />
State Agency for the Regulation of Oil and Gas Resources and subsequently<br /><br />
re-issued temporary licence Series OGA Number 002 Code 01-11B by them on October<br /><br />
2 2000; and<br /><br />
WHEREAS, on April 16, 1999 the Law on Oil and Gas in Georgia ("the Petroleum<br /><br />
Law")<br /><br />
4<br /><br />
<br /><br />
<PAGE><br /><br />
came into effect;<br /><br />
<br /><br />
WHEREAS, the Petroleum Law, among other things, provided for the creation of the<br /><br />
State Agency and vested in it the power to represent the State in management of<br /><br />
oil and gas operations to include entering into production sharing contracts on<br /><br />
behalf of the State, to issue and to reissue licenses to investors for<br /><br />
performance of oil and gas operations, and to delegate all operational and<br /><br />
commercial functions of the State under production sharing contracts to Georgian<br /><br />
Oil until the State ceases to own more than 75% of its shares;<br /><br />
WHEREAS, the Petroleum Law, among other things, designated Georgian Oil to<br /><br />
perform the functions of the National Oil Company (as that term is defined in<br /><br />
Article 1.39 of the Petroleum Law) so long as the State owns more than 75% of<br /><br />
its shares;<br /><br />
WHEREAS, the Parties wish to amend and restate the terms of the Original<br /><br />
Agreements to take account of changed economic circumstances and the<br /><br />
introduction of the Georgian Law on Oil and Gas;<br /><br />
NOW, THEREFORE, in consideration of the promises and the mutual covenants and<br /><br />
conditions herein contained, it is hereby agreed as follows:<br /><br />
5<br /><br />
<br /><br />
<PAGE><br /><br />
<br /><br />
ARTICLE 1<br /><br />
DEFINITIONS<br /><br />
The following words and terms used in this Contract shall unless otherwise<br /><br />
expressly specified in this Contract have the following respective meanings:<br /><br />
1.1<br /><br />
<br /><br />
"Accounting Procedure" means the accounting procedure set out in Annex<br /><br />
"C" hereto.<br /><br />
<br /><br />
1.2<br /><br />
<br /><br />
"Administrative Fees" shall mean any fees, fees, charges, or other<br /><br />
imposts which are generally applicable or which are imposed for<br /><br />
specific services or materials provided by the Government or any local<br /><br />
authority, provided they are imposed by laws, rules and regulations of<br /><br />
general application and do not discriminate or have the effect of<br /><br />
discriminating against the Contractor.<br /><br />
<br /><br />
1.3<br /><br />
<br /><br />
An "Affiliated Company" or "Affiliate" means:<br /><br />
1.3.1<br /><br />
<br /><br />
with respect to Contractor or, as indicated, the Parent<br /><br />
Company, a company, corporation, partnership or other legal<br /><br />
entity:<br /><br />
i)<br /><br />
<br /><br />
in which Contractor or the Parent Company, as the case<br /><br />
may be, owns, directly or indirectly, more than fifty<br /><br />
percent (50%) of the shares or voting interests as well<br /><br />
as the unrestricted right to exercise management control<br /><br />
on all matters and otherwise has the right to establish<br /><br />
management policy and exercise such management control;<br /><br />
or<br /><br />
<br /><br />
ii) in which at least fifty percent (50%) of the shares or<br /><br />
voting interests are owned directly or indirectly by a<br /><br />
company, corporation, partnership or other legal entity,<br /><br />
which owns directly or indirectly more than fifty percent<br /><br />
(50%) of the shares or voting interest as well as the<br /><br />
unrestricted right to exercise management control on all<br /><br />
matters, and otherwise has the right to establish<br /><br />
management policy and exercise such management control,<br /><br />
of Contractor or Parent Company;<br /><br />
6<br /><br />
<br /><br />
<PAGE><br /><br />
1.3.2<br /><br />
<br /><br />
with respect to Georgian Oil, any legal entity directly or<br /><br />
indirectly controlled by Georgian Oil, or any legal entity<br /><br />
that directly or indirectly controls Georgian Oil. For the<br /><br />
purposes of this part of the definition, the term to "control"<br /><br />
shall mean with respect to any such entity, having the right<br /><br />
to carry out direct or indirect supervision of such entity or<br /><br />
to define a general scope of its activity based on holding the<br /><br />
shares entitled to vote, any other form of ownership, or on<br /><br />
any other grounds.<br /><br />
<br /><br />
1.4<br /><br />
<br /><br />
"Annex" or "Annexes" means each or all of the Annexes "A" through "G"<br /><br />
attached to this Contract and made a part hereof. In the event of a<br /><br />
conflict between the provisions of an Annex and a term in the main body<br /><br />
of this Contract, the provisions of the latter shall prevail.<br /><br />
<br /><br />
1.5<br /><br />
<br /><br />
"Annual Work Programme" means a work plan and schedule, prepared and<br /><br />
submitted by the Contractor to the Co-ordination Committee and<br /><br />
approved, or deemed approved, by the Co-ordination Committee, all as<br /><br />
more fully herein provided, setting forth the Petroleum Operations to<br /><br />
be carried out during a Calendar Year by the Contractor.<br /><br />
<br /><br />
1.6<br /><br />
<br /><br />
"Appraisal" means all works carried out by the Contractor to evaluate<br /><br />
and delineate a discovery of Petroleum in the Contract Area.<br /><br />
<br /><br />
1.7<br /><br />
<br /><br />
"Appraisal Area" means a part of the Contract Area in which an<br /><br />
Appraisal Programme is to be conducted by the Contractor.<br /><br />
<br /><br />
1.8<br /><br />
<br /><br />
"Appraisal Programme" means a Work Programme submitted by the<br /><br />
Contractor to the Coordination Committee for approval, under which the<br /><br />
Contractor will evaluate and delineate a discovery of Petroleum, and<br /><br />
which has been approved, or deemed approved, by the Coordination<br /><br />
Committee as herein provided. Any Appraisal Programme which has not yet<br /><br />
been so approved shall herein be referred to as a Draft Appraisal<br /><br />
Programme.<br /><br />
<br /><br />
1.9<br /><br />
<br /><br />
"Associated Natural Gas" means all gaseous hydrocarbons produced in<br /><br />
association with Crude Oil, which Crude Oil itself can be commercially<br /><br />
produced and separated<br /><br />
7<br /><br />
<br /><br />
<PAGE><br /><br />
therefrom.<br /><br />
1.10<br /><br />
<br /><br />
"Available Crude Oil" means Crude Oil produced and Saved from the<br /><br />
Contract Area and not used in Petroleum Operations in accordance with<br /><br />
Article 11.3.<br /><br />
<br /><br />
1.11<br /><br />
<br /><br />
"Available Natural Gas" means Associated or non-Associated Natural Gas<br /><br />
produced and Saved from the Contract Area and not used in Petroleum<br /><br />
Operations in accordance with Article 11.3.<br /><br />
<br /><br />
1.12<br /><br />
<br /><br />
"Available Petroleum" means Available Crude Oil and Available Natural<br /><br />
Gas.<br /><br />
<br /><br />
1.13<br /><br />
<br /><br />
"Barrel" means a quantity consisting of forty-two (42) United States<br /><br />
gallons liquid measure, corrected to a temperature of sixty (60)<br /><br />
degrees Fahrenheit with pressure at sea level.<br /><br />
<br /><br />
1.14<br /><br />
<br /><br />
"Base Level Oil" is the amount of oil that Georgian Oil expect they<br /><br />
would have produced from the Contract Area had there been no other<br /><br />
<br /><br />
arrangements over the period 1996 to 2000. The Parties agree that this<br /><br />
Base Level Oil amounts to 250,000 tons.<br /><br />
1.15<br /><br />
<br /><br />
"Budget" means the estimate of the expenditures, listed category by<br /><br />
category, relating to Petroleum Operations and contained in any Work<br /><br />
Programme.<br /><br />
<br /><br />
1.16<br /><br />
<br /><br />
"Calendar Quarter" or "Quarter" is a period of three consecutive months<br /><br />
beginning on January 1st, April 1st, July 1st and October 1st of each<br /><br />
Calendar Year.<br /><br />
<br /><br />
1.17<br /><br />
<br /><br />
"Calendar Year" or "Year" means a period of twelve (12) consecutive<br /><br />
months beginning on January 1st and ending on December 31st in the same<br /><br />
year, according to the Gregorian Calendar.<br /><br />
<br /><br />
1.18<br /><br />
<br /><br />
"Commercial Discovery" means a discovery of Petroleum in respect of<br /><br />
which the Contractor has given a notice pursuant to Article 9.3.1.<br /><br />
<br /><br />
1.19<br /><br />
<br /><br />
"Commencement of Commercial Production" means the date on which the<br /><br />
first lifting, shipment or delivery of Petroleum is made under<br /><br />
Commercial Production.<br /><br />
8<br /><br />
<br /><br />
<PAGE><br /><br />
1.20<br /><br />
<br /><br />
"Commercial Production" means production of Petroleum and delivery<br /><br />
under a lifting agreement or contract for sale as provided for in a<br /><br />
Development Plan as amended from time to time.<br /><br />
<br /><br />
1.21<br /><br />
<br /><br />
"Contract" or "PSC" means the Original Agreements as amended, restated<br /><br />
and superseded by this Production Sharing Contract together with all<br /><br />
attached Annexes and any variation, extension or modification hereto,<br /><br />
which may be agreed in writing by all the Parties.<br /><br />
<br /><br />
1.22<br /><br />
<br /><br />
"Contract Area" means the area (from the surface to all depths<br /><br />
accessible to drilling technology) specified in Article 3 hereof and<br /><br />
delineated in Annex A as reduced or enlarged from time to time in<br /><br />
accordance with the provisions of this Contract.<br /><br />
<br /><br />
1.23<br /><br />
<br /><br />
"Contractor" means the Contractor and his permitted assignees and<br /><br />
successors, as provided herein.<br /><br />
<br /><br />
1.24<br /><br />
<br /><br />
"Co-ordination Committee" means the committee constituted in accordance<br /><br />
with Article 6.<br /><br />
<br /><br />
1.25<br /><br />
<br /><br />
"Cost Recovery" means the method by which Costs and Expenses are<br /><br />
recovered in accordance with Article 11.5.<br /><br />
<br /><br />
1.26<br /><br />
<br /><br />
"Cost Recovery Petroleum" means Petroleum available for Cost Recovery<br /><br />
pursuant to Article 11.5.<br /><br />
<br /><br />
1.27<br /><br />
<br /><br />
"Costs and Expenses" means all incurred costs and expenses necessary to<br /><br />
conduct Petroleum Operations and chargeable to the Petroleum Operations<br /><br />
Account, all as more fully set forth and in accordance with the<br /><br />
Accounting Procedure, including such amounts so chargeable as are set<br /><br />
forth in Annex F in respect of costs and expenses incurred prior to the<br /><br />
date of this Contract or hereinafter stated to be approved by the<br /><br />
Co-ordination Committee, subject to the audit provisions of this<br /><br />
Contract.<br /><br />
<br /><br />
1.28<br /><br />
<br /><br />
"Crude Oil" means crude mineral oil, asphalt, ozokerite and all kinds<br /><br />
of hydrocarbons whether in a solid, liquid or mixed state at the<br /><br />
wellhead or separator or which is obtained from Natural Gas through<br /><br />
condensation or extraction, excluding methane gas.<br /><br />
9<br /><br />
<br /><br />
<PAGE><br /><br />
1.29<br /><br />
<br /><br />
"Customs Duties" means all import (or export) tariffs and duties and<br /><br />
other mandatory payments, other than Administrative Fees, as stipulated<br /><br />
by applicable laws, rules or regulations of Georgia with respect to the<br /><br />
import or export of Petroleum, materials, equipment, goods and any<br /><br />
other similar items.<br /><br />
<br /><br />
1.30<br /><br />
<br /><br />
"Day" means a calendar day.<br /><br />
<br /><br />
1.31<br /><br />
<br /><br />
"Development Area" means all or any part of the Contract Area specified<br /><br />
in a Development Plan approved, or deemed approved, by the Coordination<br /><br />
Committee as herein provided.<br /><br />
<br /><br />
1.32<br /><br />
<br /><br />
"Development Plan" is a plan presented by the Contractor in accordance<br /><br />
with Article 9.5 and approved, or deemed approved, by the Coordination<br /><br />
Committee as herein provided. Any development plan which has not yet<br /><br />
been so approved shall be a Draft Development Plan.<br /><br />
<br /><br />
1.33<br /><br />
<br /><br />
"Dispute" means any difference of view or disagreement between the<br /><br />
First Party and the Second Party in relation to or in connection with,<br /><br />
or arising out of any terms and conditions of this Contract, but does<br /><br />
not include (a) any difference of view or disagreement between the<br /><br />
First Party and the Second Party which under the provisions of this<br /><br />
Contract is to be referred for determination to a Sole Expert pursuant<br /><br />
to Article 30.9 or (b) any difference of view or disagreement falling<br /><br />
under Article 30.8.<br /><br />
<br /><br />
1.34<br /><br />
<br /><br />
"Dispute Parties" shall have the meaning as ascribed thereto in Article<br /><br />
30<br /><br />
<br /><br />
1.35<br /><br />
<br /><br />
"Dollar" or "US$" or "$" means the currency of the United States of<br /><br />
America.<br /><br />
<br /><br />
1.36<br /><br />
<br /><br />
"Double Tax Treaty" means any international treaty or convention for<br /><br />
the avoidance of double taxation of income and/or capital which is<br /><br />
applicable in Georgia.<br /><br />
<br /><br />
1.37<br /><br />
<br /><br />
"Effective Date" is defined in Article 32.2.<br /><br />
<br /><br />
1.38<br /><br />
<br /><br />
"Exploration Programme" shall mean all the exploration activities for<br /><br />
previously undiscovered Petroleum, which shall include geological,<br /><br />
geophysical, aerial and other survey activities and interpretation of<br /><br />
data relating thereto and the drilling of shot holes, core holes,<br /><br />
stratigraphic tests, exploratory wells and tests thereof for the<br /><br />
10<br /><br />
<br /><br />
<PAGE><br /><br />
<br /><br />
discovery of Petroleum and other related operations.<br /><br />
1.39<br /><br />
<br /><br />
"Finance Costs" means in respect of debt incurred in carrying out<br /><br />
Petroleum Operations, approved (including all their terms in respect<br /><br />
thereof) by the Co-ordination Committee and owed to a party which is<br /><br />
not an Affiliate of the Contractor, all amounts of interest, fees and<br /><br />
charges paid in respect thereof, including any refinancing thereof, and<br /><br />
in respect of such debt so approved and owed to an Affiliate of the<br /><br />
Contractor, it shall include interest only to the extent it does not<br /><br />
exceed a rate which would have been agreed between independent parties.<br /><br />
<br /><br />
1.40<br /><br />
<br /><br />
"First Dispute Party" has the meaning assigned to it in Article 30.<br /><br />
<br /><br />
1.41<br /><br />
<br /><br />
"Force Majeure" is defined in Article 25.1.<br /><br />
<br /><br />
1.42<br /><br />
<br /><br />
"Foreign Employee" is defined in Article 17.19.<br /><br />
<br /><br />
1.43<br /><br />
<br /><br />
"Foreign Exchange" means any lawful currency other than the currency of<br /><br />
Georgia.<br /><br />
<br /><br />
1.44<br /><br />
<br /><br />
"Foreign Subcontractors" means Subcontractors in respect of which the<br /><br />
Contractor has complied with Article 17.24.<br /><br />
<br /><br />
1.45<br /><br />
<br /><br />
"Gas Sales Contract" is any contract to be entered into for the sale of<br /><br />
Natural Gas.<br /><br />
<br /><br />
1.46<br /><br />
<br /><br />
"Good Oilfield Practices" means all those things that are generally<br /><br />
accepted in the international petroleum industry as good, safe,<br /><br />
environmentally sound, economical and efficient in exploring for and<br /><br />
producing Petroleum.<br /><br />
<br /><br />
1.47<br /><br />
<br /><br />
"Insolvency Event" means, with respect to a Contractor Party<br /><br />
(i)<br /><br />
<br /><br />
the appointment, without recall within 60 Days of appointment,<br /><br />
of a liquidator, other than for the purposes of amalgamation<br /><br />
<br /><br />
or reconstruction; or<br /><br />
(ii)<br /><br />
<br /><br />
the appointment, without recall or revocation of appointment<br /><br />
or resignation within 60 Days of appointment, of an<br /><br />
administrator, receiver or administrative receiver in respect<br /><br />
of the whole or part of the assets and undertaking of that<br /><br />
Contractor Party; or<br /><br />
11<br /><br />
<br /><br />
<PAGE><br /><br />
(iii)<br /><br />
<br /><br />
outside Bermuda, any procedure analogous with either (a) or<br /><br />
(b) above in any other jurisdiction.<br /><br />
<br /><br />
1.48<br /><br />
<br /><br />
"IVOG" means Ioris Valley Oil and Gas Limited, of Lilo Station,<br /><br />
Chirnakhuli 9, Tbilisi, Georgia, a company half of which is owned by<br /><br />
Contractor and half by Georgian Oil.<br /><br />
<br /><br />
1.49<br /><br />
<br /><br />
"Letter of Credit" means, with reference to Article 8.2.4, an<br /><br />
engagement by a bank made on the instructions of the Contractor that<br /><br />
the bank will hounour demands for payment to the State Agency, subject<br /><br />
to the conditions specified in the Letter of Credit.<br /><br />
<br /><br />
1.50<br /><br />
<br /><br />
"Licence" means either:<br /><br />
(i)<br /><br />
<br /><br />
the Licence issued in connection with the Original Agreements,<br /><br />
provisionally issued by the Chairman of the specialised office<br /><br />
on Licensing and Informatics of Georgian Oil and formally<br /><br />
issued on 13 October 1995 by the Department of Protection of<br /><br />
Mineral Resources and Mining in the Ministry of Environmental<br /><br />
Protection, together with all annexes thereto and any<br /><br />
extension, renewal, re-issue or amendment thereof, including<br /><br />
that provided in 26.10.1 or<br /><br />
<br /><br />
(ii)<br /><br />
<br /><br />
any Licence issued to the Contractor.<br /><br />
<br /><br />
1.51<br /><br />
<br /><br />
"Local Sales" is defined in Article 17.22.2.<br /><br />
<br /><br />
1.52<br /><br />
<br /><br />
"Marketing Team" is described in Article 16.5.<br /><br />
<br /><br />
1.53<br /><br />
<br /><br />
"Measurement Point" means the physical location at which title to<br /><br />
Petroleum passes to Parties entitled thereto, and specified in a<br /><br />
Development Plan.<br /><br />
<br /><br />
1.54<br /><br />
<br /><br />

ARTICLE 2<br /><br />
SCOPE OF CONTRACT AND GENERAL PROVISIONS<br /><br />
<br /><br />
2.1<br /><br />
<br /><br />
The State hereby ratifies and confirms to the Contractor the License<br /><br />
for its term, for the purpose and in accordance with the provisions of<br /><br />
the Contract.<br /><br />
<br /><br />
2.2<br /><br />
<br /><br />
Subject to the terms and conditions of the Contract, the State hereby<br /><br />
grants to the Contractor, (and Operating Company as herein provided),<br /><br />
the exclusive rights to conduct Petroleum Operations in the Contract<br /><br />
Area during the term of this Contract.<br /><br />
<br /><br />
2.3<br /><br />
<br /><br />
This Contract is an existing agreement for the purposes of the<br /><br />
Petroleum Law as that term is defined in Article 1.36 thereof and shall<br /><br />
enjoy any and all benefits attributed to it by Georgian law.<br /><br />
<br /><br />
2.4<br /><br />
<br /><br />
The Contractor shall be responsible to the State for the execution of<br /><br />
all Petroleum Operations, including the activities of the Operating<br /><br />
Company, all in accordance with the provisions of this Contract.<br /><br />
The Contractor shall provide the financial and technical resources<br /><br />
required for the execution of the Petroleum Operations, and its other<br /><br />
obligations under this Contract. Subject to the other provisions of the<br /><br />
Contract, in performing the Petroleum Operations, the Contractor shall<br /><br />
conduct all operations diligently in accordance with Good Oilfield<br /><br />
Practices and in compliance with applicable laws, rules and<br /><br />
regulations.<br /><br />
The Contractor may borrow funds from Third Parties and/or Affiliated<br /><br />
Companies for the financing required for the investments necessary for<br /><br />
Petroleum Operations. Finance Costs charged for such loans shall be<br /><br />
recoupable as Costs and Expenses as provided in Article 11 and the<br /><br />
Accounting Procedure.<br /><br />
<br /><br />
2.5<br /><br />
<br /><br />
<PAGE><br /><br />
<br /><br />
Except as provided in Article 9.8.4, the Contractor shall be reimbursed<br /><br />
for its investment and expenditures in connection with the conduct of<br /><br />
Petroleum<br /><br />
17<br /><br />
Operations not by way of reimbursement in cash, but only by receipt of<br /><br />
its share of Petroleum from the Contract Area to which it may become<br /><br />
entitled by way of Costs and Expenses from Cost Recovery Petroleum<br /><br />
under Article 11 and other provisions of this Contract. If Cost<br /><br />
Recovery Petroleum produced from Development Areas within the Contract<br /><br />
Area is insufficient to reimburse the Contractor for Costs and Expenses<br /><br />
incurred by the Contractor, the Contractor shall bear its own losses in<br /><br />
respect of any shortfall.<br /><br />
<br /><br />
2.6<br /><br />
<br /><br />
Where the Contractor is more than one person or entity, any obligation<br /><br />
of the Contractor hereunder shall be a joint and several obligation of<br /><br />
all of the persons and entities who constitute the Contractor, except<br /><br />
for the following which shall be a several obligation of each of said<br /><br />
<br /><br />
persons and entities: i) the obligation to pay Profit Tax or any other<br /><br />
tax assessed and levied on profit or net income in accordance with<br /><br />
Article 17; ii) the obligation to observe stipulations relating to<br /><br />
confidentiality set out in Article 28, except in respect of their<br /><br />
application to anything done or to be done by the Contractor in his<br /><br />
capacity as such; and iii) the obligation to observe stipulations<br /><br />
relating to foreign exchange set forth in Article 19, except in respect<br /><br />
of their application to anything done or to be done by the Contractor<br /><br />
in his capacity as such.<br /><br />
2.7<br /><br />
<br /><br />
<PAGE><br /><br />
<br /><br />
The State has appointed the State Agency as its representative for the<br /><br />
purposes set out in Article 8 of the Petroleum Law and Georgian Oil as<br /><br />
its representative for the purposes set out in Article 9 of the<br /><br />
Petroleum Law, with right of substitution and removal, each to exercise<br /><br />
the State functions and to perform the State obligations under the<br /><br />
Contract as prescribed by the Petroleum Law and to enjoy the benefit as<br /><br />
herein provided. The State will give notice to the Contractor of the<br /><br />
appointment and removal and substitution of its representatives. The<br /><br />
Contractor will be entitled to assume that each State Representative<br /><br />
has full authority to represent the State for those State purposes<br /><br />
under the Contract assigned to it according to the Petroleum Law,<br /><br />
including those where herein specific reference is made to the State<br /><br />
Representative.<br /><br />

ARTICLE 3<br /><br />
CONTRACT AREA<br /><br />
<br /><br />
3.1<br /><br />
<br /><br />
The Contract Area is as set out by the geographic location and<br /><br />
co-ordinates described in Annex "B" attached hereto and delineated on<br /><br />
the map which forms part thereof. The total area of the Contract Area<br /><br />
may hereafter be reduced only in accordance with the provisions of this<br /><br />
Contract.<br /><br />
<br /><br />
3.2<br /><br />
<br /><br />
Except as for all rights and authorisations necessary for the<br /><br />
implementation of the provisions of this Contract, no right is granted<br /><br />
in favour of the Contractor to the use or disposal of any other natural<br /><br />
or man-made resources or aquatic resources other than as provided in<br /><br />
Article 3.2 and Article 13.5. For the sake of clarity, it is understood<br /><br />
that produced hydrocarbons and associated substances may be injected<br /><br />
into underground reservoirs provided the purpose of such activity is to<br /><br />
avoid discharge of deleterious substances into the environment or to<br /><br />
enhance hydrocarbon recovery or to conserve hydrocarbons for which<br /><br />
there is no immediate commercial market. It is also understood that<br /><br />
certain waters may be utilised in the Petroleum Operations envisioned<br /><br />
herein to enhance hydrocarbon recovery or process the hydrocarbons for<br /><br />
sale.<br /><br />
<br /><br />
3.3<br /><br />
<br /><br />
Contractor shall have the right of free ingress and egress to and over<br /><br />
the Contract Area over State lands and waters on, over, and adjoining<br /><br />
the Contract Area for the purpose of Petroleum exploration,<br /><br />
development, production, and removal. The State Agency will assist<br /><br />
Contractor to obtain other necessary easements and rights of way.<br /><br />
<br /><br />
3.4<br /><br />
<br /><br />
Contractor may, subject to approval and permitting required by the laws<br /><br />
and regulations of Georgia and to any contractual arrangements with<br /><br />
third parties as necessary or convenient, re-inject Petroleum extracted<br /><br />
from the Contract Area for operational reasons, including drilling,<br /><br />
testing, re-working, or other activities to enhance or maintain the<br /><br />
recovery of Petroleum or for storage of Petroleum for which there is no<br /><br />
immediate market, and re-inject produced water and associated<br /><br />
substances into underground reservoirs capable of commercial Petroleum<br /><br />
<br /><br />
<PAGE><br /><br />
<br /><br />
19<br /><br />
production or other strata if the purpose of such activity is to avoid<br /><br />
discharge of deleterious substances into the environment. Petroleum<br /><br />
re-injected for operational purposes is not to be deemed as "produced".<br /><br />
Petroleum produced from the Contract Area for which there is no<br /><br />
immediate commercial market may be also re-injected into appropriate<br /><br />
reservoirs or other strata, either on or off the Contract Area, for<br /><br />
<br /><br />
storage. Title to such stored Petroleum shall pass to the Parties at<br /><br />
the Measurement Point at the time the stored Petroleum is withdrawn<br /><br />
from storage and sold or otherwise disposed of. All obligations of the<br /><br />
Parties to account for and to pay taxes or other obligations on or with<br /><br />
respect to such stored Petroleum shall accrue at the time title passes.<br /><br />
20<br /><br />

<br /><br />
ARTICLE 4<br /><br />
CONTRACT TERM<br /><br />
4.1<br /><br />
<br /><br />
The term of the Contract shall continue from the Effective Date for a<br /><br />
period of twenty years.<br /><br />
<br /><br />
4.2<br /><br />
<br /><br />
If in respect of any Development Area, Commercial Production, as set<br /><br />
forth in a revised Development Plan, remains possible beyond the twenty<br /><br />
year period specified in Article 4.1 the Contractor, after giving<br /><br />
notice to Georgian Oil and the State Agency at least one (1) year prior<br /><br />
to the end of such period, and after obtaining approval by the<br /><br />
Co-ordination Committee of such revised Development Plan shall be<br /><br />
entitled to have an extension of the term of this Contract with respect<br /><br />
to such Development Area for an additional term of fifteen (15) years,<br /><br />
or the producing life of the Development Area, whichever is lesser,<br /><br />
subject to the approval of the State Agency, such approval not to be<br /><br />
withheld unreasonably.<br /><br />

<br /><br />
the remainder of the Contract Area (if and to the extent the<br /><br />

within the Development Area, or (b) the base of the deepest<br /><br />

ARTICLE 6<br /><br />
CO-ORDINATION COMMITTEE<br /><br />
<br /><br />
6.1<br /><br />
<br /><br />
For the purpose of providing the overall supervision and direction and<br /><br />
ensuring the performance of the Petroleum Operations, Georgian Oil and<br /><br />
the Contractor shall establish a Co-ordination Committee within<br /><br />
forty-five (45) Days of the Effective Date.<br /><br />
<br /><br />
6.2<br /><br />
<br /><br />
The Co-ordination Committee shall comprise a total of six (6) members.<br /><br />
Georgian Oil shall appoint a total of three (3) representatives and the<br /><br />
Contractor shall appoint three (3) representatives to form the<br /><br />
Co-ordination Committee. Georgian Oil and the Contractor shall each<br /><br />
designate one of its representatives as its chief representative. All<br /><br />
the aforesaid representatives shall have the right to attend and<br /><br />
present their views at meetings of the Co-ordination Committee. Each<br /><br />
representative shall have the right to appoint an alternate who shall<br /><br />
be entitled to attend all meetings of the Co-ordination Committee. When<br /><br />
a decision is to be made on any proposal, the chief representative (or<br /><br />
in his absence, his alternate) from each Party shall be the spokesman<br /><br />
on behalf of such Party and shall cast a single vote.<br /><br />
The first chairman of the Co-ordination Committee shall be the chief<br /><br />
representative of the Contractor (or his alternate) and the first vice<br /><br />
<br /><br />
chairman shall be the chief representative of Georgian Oil (or his<br /><br />
alternate).<br /><br />
The chairman of the Co-ordination Committee shall preside over meetings<br /><br />
of the Co-ordination Committee, and in the absence of the chairman (or<br /><br />
his alternate), the vice-chairman shall preside. Each Party may<br /><br />
designate a reasonable number of advisors, who may attend, but shall<br /><br />
not be entitled to vote at, Co-ordination Committee meetings. Such<br /><br />
advisors may speak only with the permission of the chairman or<br /><br />
vice-chairman.<br /><br />
For the purposes of clarification and for the avoidance of any doubt,<br /><br />
the chairman<br /><br />
25<br /><br />
<br /><br />
<PAGE><br /><br />
<br /><br />
shall have no determinative casting vote.<br /><br />
6.3<br /><br />
<br /><br />
A regular meeting of the Co-ordination Committee shall be held at least<br /><br />
once each Calendar Quarter. The secretary to be designated pursuant to<br /><br />
this Article shall be responsible for calling such regular meetings of<br /><br />
the Co-ordination Committee and shall do so at the request of the<br /><br />
chairman by sending a notice to the Parties. Other meetings, if<br /><br />
necessary, may be held at any time at the request of Georgian Oil or<br /><br />
the Contractor. In each case, the secretary shall give the Parties at<br /><br />
least 30 Days notice (or such shorter period as the Parties may agree)<br /><br />
of the proposed meeting date, the time and location of the meeting.<br /><br />
<br /><br />
6.4<br /><br />
<br /><br />
The Parties hereby empower the Co-ordination Committee to:<br /><br />
6.4.1<br /><br />
<br /><br />
review and approve any Work Programme, Budget, production<br /><br />
schedule and lifting schedule proposed by the Contractor and<br /><br />
any amendment thereof, and verify and supervise the accounting<br /><br />
of costs and the conformity of the operating and accounting<br /><br />
records with the terms of this Contract and Annexes "C" and<br /><br />
"E" hereof;<br /><br />
<br /><br />
6.4.2<br /><br />
<br /><br />
review and approve Development Plans, including the respective<br /><br />
development operations and Budgets, and the demarcation of a<br /><br />
Development Area, all after determining the commerciality<br /><br />
thereof;<br /><br />
<br /><br />
6.4.3<br /><br />
<br /><br />
approve or confirm the following specific items of procurement<br /><br />
and expenditure:<br /><br />
i)<br /><br />
<br /><br />
approve procurement and purchase contracts of any item<br /><br />
within a Budget with a unit price exceeding one hundred<br /><br />
thousand US$ (US$100,000) or any single purchase order of<br /><br />
total monetary value exceeding two hundred and fifty<br /><br />
thousand US$ (US$250,000);<br /><br />
<br /><br />
ii) approve a lease of equipment, or an engineering<br /><br />
subcontract or a service contract within a Budget worth<br /><br />
more than two hundred and fifty thousand US$ (US$250,000)<br /><br />
in total; and<br /><br />
26<br /><br />
<br /><br />
<PAGE><br /><br />
<br /><br />
iii) confirm excess expenditures pursuant to Article 10.5<br /><br />
hereof and the expenditures pursuant to Article 10.6<br /><br />
hereof;<br /><br />
iv) Unless otherwise agreed by the Coordination Committee,<br /><br />
every contract in excess of two hundred and fifty<br /><br />
thousand US$ (US$250,000) should be negotiated and<br /><br />

Company.<br /><br />

<br /><br />
review and approve the insurance programme proposed by the<br /><br />

Without prejudice to the foregoing, it is accepted that part<br /><br />

6.5<br /><br />
<br /><br />
Decisions of the Co-ordination Committee shall be unanimous. All<br /><br />
decisions made unanimously shall be deemed to be formal decisions and<br /><br />
shall be conclusive and equally binding upon the Parties.<br /><br />
<br /><br />
6.6<br /><br />
<br /><br />
In the event that the Co-ordination Committee fails to reach agreement:<br /><br />
6.6.1<br /><br />
<br /><br />
within thirty (30) Days of the date of submission, concerning<br /><br />
the approval of any Work Programme or Budget submitted by the<br /><br />
Contractor, the proposal of the Contractor will be deemed to<br /><br />
have been approved and to be binding; provided, however, in<br /><br />
the case of a Work Programme to give effect to the provisions<br /><br />
of a Development Plan, it is consistent with the requirements<br /><br />
of that Development Plan as approved or deemed to have been<br /><br />
approved by the Coordination Committee;<br /><br />
28<br /><br />
<br /><br />
<PAGE><br /><br />
6.6.2<br /><br />
<br /><br />
within ninety (90) Days from the date of submission,<br /><br />
concerning the approval of a Development Plan submitted by the<br /><br />
Contractor, or concerning a proposal submitted by the<br /><br />
Contractor to amend a Development Plan, either Georgian Oil or<br /><br />
the Contractor, or both of them jointly, may, in accordance<br /><br />
with Article 30, refer the disagreement to a Sole Expert who<br /><br />
will be asked to determine whether or not the Development Plan<br /><br />
as submitted by the Contractor, or as the case may be, as<br /><br />
amended in accordance with the Contractor's proposal, would<br /><br />
satisfy the requirements relating to Development Plans set out<br /><br />
in Article 9.<br /><br />
<br /><br />
6.6.3<br /><br />
<br /><br />
A determination by a Sole Expert of a disagreement referred to<br /><br />
<br /><br />
him under Article 6.6.2 shall be final and binding on the<br /><br />
Parties with effect that the proposal submitted by the<br /><br />
Contractor to the Coordination Committee will be deemed to<br /><br />
have been approved, or as the case may be, rejected, provided,<br /><br />
however, that if the proposal seeking approval of a<br /><br />
Development Plan is deemed to have been rejected the<br /><br />
Contractor at its election shall either as soon as practicable<br /><br />
after the determination of the Sole Expert has been<br /><br />
communicated to the Parties submit an alternative proposal or<br /><br />
inform Georgian Oil that the discovery to which the<br /><br />
Development Plan relates is no longer considered by the<br /><br />
Contractor to be commercial.<br /><br />
6.4<br /><br />
<br /><br />
A matter which requires urgent handling may be decided by the<br /><br />
Co-ordination Committee without convening a meeting, with the<br /><br />
Co-ordination Committee making decisions through telexes, e-mail, or<br /><br />
faxes or the circulation of documents, subsequently confirmed in<br /><br />
writing by the chief representative from each party.<br /><br />
<br /><br />
6.8<br /><br />
<br /><br />
The Co-ordination Committee shall nominate a secretary, to record<br /><br />
minutes of the meetings of the Co-ordination Committee. The secretary<br /><br />
shall take a record of each proposal voted on and the results of such<br /><br />
vote at each meeting of the Co-ordination Committee. Each<br /><br />
representative of the Parties shall sign and be provided with a copy of<br /><br />
such record at the end of such meeting. The secretary shall provide<br /><br />
each Party with a copy of the minutes of each meeting of the<br /><br />
Co-ordination Committee within thirty (30) Days after the end of such<br /><br />
meeting. Each Party shall thereafter have a period of fifteen (15) Days<br /><br />
to give notice of any objections to the minutes to the secretary.<br /><br />
Failure to give notice within the said fifteen (15) Day period shall be<br /><br />
deemed approval of those minutes. In any event the record of proposals<br /><br />
voted on to be provided at the end of each meeting shall be conclusive<br /><br />
and take precedence<br /><br />
29<br /><br />
<br /><br />
<PAGE><br /><br />
<br /><br />
over the minutes. The Co-ordination Committee shall provide the State<br /><br />
Agency with a copy of the approved minutes.<br /><br />
6.9<br /><br />
<br /><br />
All costs and expenses incurred with respect to the activities of the<br /><br />
Co-ordination Committee shall be paid or reimbursed by the Contractor<br /><br />
and shall be Costs and Expenses in accordance with the Accounting<br /><br />
Procedures.<br /><br />

ARTICLE 7<br /><br />
OPERATING COMPANY<br /><br />
7.1<br /><br />
<br /><br />
The Contractor and Georgian Oil shall re-register in Georgia their<br /><br />
existing joint venture company Ioris Valley Oil and Gas as a juridical<br /><br />
person having limited liability. The object of such company shall be to<br /><br />
fulfil the functions of and act as Operating Company for Petroleum<br /><br />
Operations (including, but not limited to, the employment and<br /><br />
remuneration of staff) pursuant to the instructions of the Contractor<br /><br />
and only in accordance with the technical, operational and management<br /><br />
instructions of the Contractor, which shall be in accordance with Work<br /><br />
Programmes and Budgets and Development Plans. The Contractor shall be<br /><br />
fully liable for all actions and omissions of Operating Company<br /><br />
performed or omitted within the scope of the above mentioned, it being<br /><br />
agreed and understood the Operating Company is obligated to comply with<br /><br />
the terms of this Contract and its Charter referred to below.<br /><br />
<br /><br />
7.2<br /><br />
<br /><br />
The Charter of the Operating Company will be as set forth in Annex E.<br /><br />
<br /><br />
7.3<br /><br />
<br /><br />
The Operating Company, pursuant to the instructions of the Contractor,<br /><br />
which shall be in accordance with Work Programmes, Budgets and<br /><br />
Development Plans, as approved by the Coordination Committee as herein<br /><br />
provided, shall<br /><br />
7.3.1<br /><br />
<br /><br />
perform Petroleum Operations reasonably, economically and<br /><br />
efficiently in accordance with such instructions<br /><br />
<br /><br />
7.3.2<br /><br />
<br /><br />
assist the Contractor in preparation of the Work Programmes<br /><br />
and Budgets and Development Plans;<br /><br />
<br /><br />
7.3.3<br /><br />
<br /><br />
propose and, when approved by Contractor, undertake<br /><br />
procurement of installations, equipment and supplies and enter<br /><br />
into subcontracts and service contracts with service providers<br /><br />
and vendors related to the Petroleum Operations;<br /><br />
31<br /><br />
<br /><br />
<PAGE><br /><br />
7.3.4<br /><br />
<br /><br />
prepare and submit for approval to the Contractor a personnel<br /><br />

by the Coordination Committee;<br /><br />
<br /><br />
7.3.5<br /><br />
<br /><br />

<br /><br />
7.3.6<br /><br />

<br /><br />

<br /><br />
7.5<br /><br />
<br /><br />
The Operating Company shall conduct Petroleum Operations on a no profit<br /><br />

<br /><br />
7.6<br /><br />
<br /><br />
The Operating Company may use Petroleum produced from the area for the<br /><br />

ARTICLE 8<br /><br />
MINIMUM WORK PROGRAMME<br /><br />
8.1<br /><br />
<br /><br />
The Contractor shall perform the Minimum Work Programme, as set forth<br /><br />
in Article 8.2, and shall complete said Minimum Work Programme not<br /><br />
later than 12 months after the Effective Date.<br /><br />
<br /><br />
8.2<br /><br />
<br /><br />
The Minimum Work Programme shall consist of:<br /><br />
8.2.1<br /><br />
<br /><br />
Within 12 months of the Effective Date, Contractor will<br /><br />
undertake to shoot and process seismic at a cost of $1.25<br /><br />
million which may be up to 200 km of new data.<br /><br />
<br /><br />
8.2.2<br /><br />
<br /><br />
Within 12 months of the Effective Date, the Contractor will<br /><br />
carry out rehabilitation work in the Development Areas on the<br /><br />
Samgori, Patardzeuli, South Dome and Krtsanisi Fields<br /><br />
(outlined in red on the map in Annex B) to the value of $0.75<br /><br />
million.<br /><br />
<br /><br />
8.2.3<br /><br />
<br /><br />
Within 18 months of the Effective Date, the Contractor will<br /><br />
complete a technical and economic evaluation of all known oil<br /><br />
or gas discoveries in the Contract Area. In the event that the<br /><br />
Contractor concludes that any such discovery may result in a<br /><br />
Commercial Discovery, then the procedures described in Article<br /><br />
9 shall apply. In the event that the Contractor concludes that<br /><br />
any such discovery would not lead to a Commercial Discovery,<br /><br />
then the area of the discovery shall be relinquished at the<br /><br />
first opportunity, unless there is demonstrable prospectivity<br /><br />
in horizons above or below the discovery horizon.<br /><br />
<br /><br />
8.2.4<br /><br />
<br /><br />
Financing of the Minimum Work Programme will be guaranteed by<br /><br />
a stand-by Letter of Credit for $2 million. The Letter of<br /><br />
<br /><br />
Credit will be made out in favour of the State Agency for<br /><br />
payment not before 31st _______2002 according to either of the<br /><br />
following terms and conditions:<br /><br />
<br /><br />
<PAGE><br /><br />
<br /><br />
(i)<br /><br />
<br /><br />
Default or partial default in execution of the<br /><br />
Minimum Work Programme<br /><br />
<br /><br />
(ii)<br /><br />
<br /><br />
Termination of the Contract as per the provisions of<br /><br />
Article 29.2.2<br /><br />
33<br /><br />
<br /><br />
The value of the Letter of Credit will be automatically<br /><br />
reduced by the amount of any payment made by NPL on account of<br /><br />
the Minimum Work Programme. All payments must be made by NPL's<br /><br />
bank, make reference to the Letter of Credit, and be approved<br /><br />
by the Co-ordination Committee and the State Agency.<br /><br />
8.3<br /><br />
<br /><br />
After the completion of the acquisition of the initial seismic data<br /><br />
(and additional seismic data, if deemed necessary by the Contractor),<br /><br />
the Contractor may, within 18 Months of the Effective Date, present to<br /><br />
the Coordination Committee an Exploration or Appraisal Programme,<br /><br />
which, if necessary, may provide for the drilling of an exploration or<br /><br />
appraisal well, the depth of such will be defined by the seismic data<br /><br />
as determined by Contractor, and shall commence such Exploration or<br /><br />
Appraisal Programme, as approved by the Coordination Committee, within<br /><br />
24 Months of the Effective Date.<br /><br />
8.4 If the Contractor fails to present such an Exploration<br /><br />
or Appraisal Programme because the Contractor has determined that<br /><br />
the seismic surveys have not defined one or more structures with<br /><br />
sufficient commercial potential to justify at least an exploration<br /><br />
or appraisal well of the type described above, then Georgian Oil and<br /><br />
the Contractor shall discuss in good faith on how to proceed. If no<br /><br />
agreement is reached concerning a mutually acceptable Exploration<br /><br />
Programme then all the areas outside the Development Areas shall be<br /><br />
relinquished within three (3) years<br /><br />
<br /><br />
8.5<br /><br />
<br /><br />
If an exploration well is drilled as aforesaid and the Contractor<br /><br />
concludes therefrom that there are significant quantities of Petroleum<br /><br />
which may result in a Commercial Discovery and gives a notice under<br /><br />
Article 9.1, then the provisions of Article 9.2 shall apply.<br /><br />
<br /><br />
8.6<br /><br />
<br /><br />
Upon completion of an Exploration or Appraisal Programme which has<br /><br />
resulted in the drilling of a well, the Contractor, at its option,<br /><br />
shall have the right to continue an Exploration Programme in the<br /><br />
Contract Area for two (2) years. If as a result of this additional<br /><br />
Exploration Programme, the Contractor believes therefrom that there are<br /><br />
<br /><br />
<PAGE><br /><br />
<br /><br />
34<br /><br />
not sufficient quantities of Petroleum to lead to a Commercial<br /><br />
Discovery, then Georgian Oil and the Contractor shall discuss in good<br /><br />
faith on how to proceed with further exploration under this Contract.<br /><br />
Subsequently, if no agreement is reached concerning a mutually<br /><br />
acceptable Exploration Programme then all the areas outside the<br /><br />
Development Areas shall be relinquished within 3 (three) years.<br /><br />
Notwithstanding anything to the contrary contained herein, if there<br /><br />
exists a conflict in the provisions of this Article 8 and the<br /><br />
relinquishment provisions required under Article 5.1, then the<br /><br />
provisions of Article 5.1 shall prevail.<br /><br />
<br /><br />
8.7<br /><br />
<br /><br />
Commencing with the operations described in this Article, Contractor<br /><br />
shall use its reasonable and diligent efforts to reduce the timing of<br /><br />
the implementation of the operations consistent with Good Oil Field<br /><br />
Practices.<br /><br />
<br /><br />
8.8<br /><br />
<br /><br />
Contractor shall, with respect to any report or proposal it submits to<br /><br />
the Coordination Committee pursuant to this Article 8, submit a copy at<br /><br />
the same time to Georgian Oil and to State Agency.<br /><br />
<br /><br />
8.9<br /><br />
<br /><br />
At the request of the State Agency, the Contractor agrees to meet with<br /><br />
the State Agency for consultative purposes concerning regulatory issues<br /><br />
<br /><br />
related to Work Programmes.<br /><br />
8.10<br /><br />
<br /><br />
It is agreed that the Samgori, Patardzeuli, South Dome and Krtsanisi<br /><br />
Fields (outlined in red on the map in Annex B) are Development Areas as<br /><br />
of the Effective Date.<br /><br />
<br /><br />
8.11<br /><br />
<br /><br />
The Contractor will diligently continue rehabilitation work in the<br /><br />
Development Areas throughout the term of the Contract or until, in the<br /><br />
Contractor's view, production declines to an uneconomic level, in order<br /><br />
to achieve the most efficient rate of production for the fields. If the<br /><br />
Contractor determines that production from such Development Areas has<br /><br />
declined to an uneconomic level, then the Contractor shall immediately<br /><br />
relinquish any such uneconomic Development Areas. Nothing in this<br /><br />
Article 8.11 should prevent the Contractor suspending operations<br /><br />
temporarily through cyclical falls in the price of oil or gas.<br /><br />
35<br /><br />
<br /><br />
<PAGE><br /><br />
<br /><br />
ARTICLE 9<br /><br />
PROCEDURE FOR APPROVAL OF<br /><br />
APPRAISAL AND DEVELOPMENT PLANS<br /><br />
9.1<br /><br />
<br /><br />
If the Contractor, following the drilling of any exploration well,<br /><br />
concludes therefrom that there are significant quantities of Petroleum<br /><br />
which may result in a Commercial Discovery, the Contractor will notify<br /><br />
the Coordination Committee within 45 Days of the completion of the well<br /><br />
that it intends to prepare an Appraisal Programme for presentation to<br /><br />
the Coordination Committee. In addition to the foregoing the<br /><br />
Contractor, should it wish to carry out appraisal work in any part of<br /><br />
the Contract Area, shall present to the Coordination Committee a<br /><br />
proposed Appraisal Programme. The proposed Appraisal Programme shall<br /><br />
specify, in reasonable detail, the work proposed to be carried out by<br /><br />
the Contractor, including seismic work, drilling of wells and technical<br /><br />
studies, and the estimated timetable within which such work will be<br /><br />
conducted, including commencement and completion dates.<br /><br />
<br /><br />
9.2<br /><br />
<br /><br />
The Contractor shall carry out the Appraisal Programme as approved or<br /><br />
deemed to be approved by the Coordination Committee. Within ninety (90)<br /><br />
Days after completion of such Appraisal Programme, the Contractor shall<br /><br />
provide to the Coordination Committee a schedule describing the<br /><br />
estimated completion of the laboratory and other studies' completion to<br /><br />
enable Contractor to submit to the Coordination Committee a<br /><br />
comprehensive evaluation report on the Appraisal Programme. Such<br /><br />
evaluation report shall include, but not be limited to, geological<br /><br />
conditions, such as structural configuration, physical properties and<br /><br />
extent of reservoir rocks, pressure, volume and temperature analysis of<br /><br />
the reservoir fluid, fluid characteristics, including gravity of liquid<br /><br />
hydrocarbons, sulphur percentage, sediment and water percentage, and<br /><br />
product yield pattern, Natural Gas composition, production forecasts<br /><br />
(per well and per Reservoir), and estimates of recoverable reserves.<br /><br />
36<br /><br />
<br /><br />
<PAGE><br /><br />
9.3<br /><br />
<br /><br />
Together with any evaluation report submitted in accordance with<br /><br />
Article 9.2 or at any other time together with a reasonably detailed<br /><br />
report supporting one of the following statements, the Contractor shall<br /><br />
submit to the Coordination Committee a written declaration, including<br /><br />
one of the following statements:<br /><br />
9.3.1<br /><br />
<br /><br />
that the Contractor believes that Commercial Production from<br /><br />
the Appraisal Area is feasible;<br /><br />
<br /><br />
9.3.2<br /><br />
<br /><br />
that the Contractor believes that Commercial Production from<br /><br />
the Appraisal Area is not feasible; or<br /><br />
<br /><br />
9.3.3<br /><br />
<br /><br />
that Commercial Production can be determined only after<br /><br />
further specified work that the Contractor commits to carry<br /><br />
out under a further Appraisal Programme in specified areas<br /><br />
within or outside the relevant Appraisal Area. The Contractor<br /><br />
shall submit such an Appraisal Programme to the Coordination<br /><br />
Committee within 90 days from submission of the above<br /><br />
declaration.<br /><br />
<br /><br />
9.4<br /><br />
<br /><br />
In the event that the Contractor makes a statement under Article 9.3.3,<br /><br />
the Contractor shall be entitled to retain the relevant Appraisal Area<br /><br />
temporarily pending the completion with reasonable diligence of the<br /><br />
further work committed by the Contractor under said Article, at which<br /><br />
time the Contractor shall advise the Coordination Committee of its<br /><br />
conclusion as to whether or not there is in fact a new Commercial<br /><br />
Discovery and the provisions of Article 9.3.1 or Article 9.3.2 shall be<br /><br />
applied accordingly.<br /><br />
<br /><br />
9.5<br /><br />
<br /><br />
If the Contractor states pursuant to Article 9.3.1 that it believes<br /><br />
that Commercial Production is feasible, the Contractor shall submit to<br /><br />
the Coordination Committee for review and approval a proposed<br /><br />
Development Plan in respect of the relevant Commercial Discovery. The<br /><br />
Development Plan shall be submitted within 3 to 12 months of such<br /><br />
declaration, depending on the complexity of the development. The<br /><br />
Contractor, with any assistance requested of the Operating Company,<br /><br />
shall proceed promptly and diligently to prepare the Development Plan<br /><br />
and, if the Development Plan is approved or deemed to be approved by<br /><br />
the Coordination Committee as herein provided, implement it in<br /><br />
accordance with Good Oilfield Practices.<br /><br />
37<br /><br />
<br /><br />
<PAGE><br /><br />
9.6<br /><br />
<br /><br />
The Contractor's proposed Development Plan to be submitted pursuant to<br /><br />
Article 9.5 shall:<br /><br />
9.6.1<br /><br />
<br /><br />
contain the Contractor's proposal for the designation of the<br /><br />
Development Area which shall, except in cases where the<br /><br />
Contractor proposes in accordance with Good Oilfield Practices<br /><br />
to develop Petroleum in an area or areas overlying proven or<br /><br />
potential producing horizons which may or may not be<br /><br />
subdivided into separate Reservoirs under a single Development<br /><br />
Plan, be a single area not exceeding the lateral extent of the<br /><br />
Reservoir in respect of which a statement has been made by the<br /><br />
Contractor pursuant to article 9.3.1 together with a<br /><br />
reasonable margin surrounding the periphery of that area;<br /><br />
<br /><br />
9.6.2<br /><br />
<br /><br />
be prepared on sound engineering and economic principles in<br /><br />
accordance with accepted standards prevailing in the<br /><br />
international petroleum industry and designed to ensure:<br /><br />
(i)<br /><br />
<br /><br />
the economic recovery of Petroleum by the efficient,<br /><br />
beneficial and timely use of the Petroleum resources<br /><br />
of the Development Area;<br /><br />
<br /><br />
(ii)<br /><br />
<br /><br />
protection for the environment taking account of any<br /><br />
environmental impact assessment studies which may<br /><br />
have been undertaken by or on behalf of the<br /><br />
Contractor and under the laws, rules and regulations<br /><br />
at the time Petroleum Operations are performed from<br /><br />
time to time;<br /><br />
<br /><br />
(iii)<br /><br />
<br /><br />
give details of the Contractor's proposals for the<br /><br />
development and operation of the Development Area<br /><br />
that Contractor believes will be required based on<br /><br />
information available at the time, including details<br /><br />
of:<br /><br />
- facilities and infrastructure which may be<br /><br />
required up to the Measurement Point either within<br /><br />
or outside the Development Area;<br /><br />
- production parameters, timing, number and location<br /><br />
of wells;<br /><br />
<br /><br />
<PAGE><br /><br />
<br /><br />
38<br /><br />
- the facilities and infrastructure (including<br /><br />
proposed locations) to be installed for production<br /><br />
storage and loading of petroleum;<br /><br />
- an estimate of the overall costs of the relevant<br /><br />
<br /><br />
Petroleum Operations and estimates of the time<br /><br />
required to complete each phase of the Development<br /><br />
Plan;<br /><br />
<br /><br />
9.7<br /><br />
<br /><br />
provide a production forecast and indicate any other<br /><br />
factor, including factors relating to the<br /><br />
transportation and disposal of Petroleum, that would<br /><br />
affect the economic and technical feasibility of the<br /><br />
Development Plan;<br /><br />
<br /><br />
(v)<br /><br />
<br /><br />
provide details of the Contractor's proposals for the<br /><br />
employment and training of citizens of Georgia; and<br /><br />
<br /><br />
(vi)<br /><br />
<br /><br />
include an abandonment and site restoration programme<br /><br />
and a funding procedure for such programme in<br /><br />
accordance with the requirements of Article 9.7.<br /><br />
<br /><br />
Subject to the limitation set forth in Article 24.3, each abandonment<br /><br />
and site restoration programme included in a Development Plan shall:<br /><br />
9.7.1<br /><br />
<br /><br />
describe removal and abandonment measures deemed necessary in<br /><br />
accordance with Good Oilfield Practices following completion<br /><br />
of production from the relevant Development Area together with<br /><br />
an estimate of the costs thereof. The abandonment plan shall<br /><br />
provide for the removal of facilities and equipment used in<br /><br />
Petroleum Operations or their in place abandonment, if<br /><br />
appropriate, in the Development Area and insofar as practical<br /><br />
restoration of used areas to a condition as defined in the<br /><br />
Development Plan. For the sake of clarity, it shall be<br /><br />
understood that the intent is to restore, insofar as<br /><br />
practical, to conditions which were shown in the environmental<br /><br />
baseline studies referred to in Article 24.3; and<br /><br />
39<br /><br />
<br /><br />
<PAGE><br /><br />
9.7.2<br /><br />
<br /><br />
9.8<br /><br />
<br /><br />
(iv)<br /><br />
<br /><br />
establish in respect of the measures described in 9.7.1 above<br /><br />
an abandonment and site restoration fund estimated from time<br /><br />
to time to be sufficient to fund those measures and placed in<br /><br />
a special interest bearing US$ account ("the Special<br /><br />
Account"), to be held in the joint names of the State Agency<br /><br />
and the Contractor and dedicated exclusively to meeting<br /><br />
expenditures for abandonment and site restoration. Except as<br /><br />
provided in Article 17.4 of the Petroleum Law, no taxes shall<br /><br />
be imposed on any amounts paid into, received or earned by, or<br /><br />
held in the Special Account and payments made into the Special<br /><br />
Account by the Contractor shall be treated as expenses<br /><br />
recoverable as Costs and Expenses.<br /><br />
<br /><br />
Discharge of abandonment obligations:<br /><br />
9.8.1<br /><br />
<br /><br />
Unless, not later than one Year prior to date on which the<br /><br />
rights of the Contractor under this Contract will terminate,<br /><br />
the State has informed the Contractor by notice in writing<br /><br />
that on termination another contractor, or Georgian Oil, will<br /><br />
take over the Development Area as a going concern, the<br /><br />
Contractor will be responsible for carrying out the<br /><br />
abandonment and site restoration programme here in this<br /><br />
Article described proceeding with all due diligence and in the<br /><br />
event that the funds available in the special interest bearing<br /><br />
account are insufficient for that purpose, will make up the<br /><br />
shortfall.<br /><br />
<br /><br />
9.8.2<br /><br />
<br /><br />
In respect of the obligations of the Contractor under Article<br /><br />
9.8.1, this Contract shall, notwithstanding the provision of<br /><br />
Article 4, remain in force until the Contractor has discharged<br /><br />
those obligations in full, and for that purpose the provisions<br /><br />
of Article 30 shall continue to be applicable.<br /><br />
<br /><br />
9.8.3<br /><br />
<br /><br />
If the State gives the Contractor a notice of the kind<br /><br />
referred to in Article 9.8.1 the Contractor shall have no<br /><br />
further responsibility for carrying out the abandonment and<br /><br />
site restoration programme and title to the funds in the<br /><br />
Special Account shall vest exclusively in the State Agency.<br /><br />

9.8.4<br /><br />

If the Contractor has discharged in full its obligations under<br /><br />

after meeting the related costs, such surplus shall first be<br /><br />
used to recover any unrecovered Costs and Expenses and any<br /><br />

9.9<br /><br />
<br /><br />
Any significant changes to an approved Development Plan or proposals<br /><br />
related to extension of a Development Area or for enhanced recovery<br /><br />

<br /><br />
9.10<br /><br />
<br /><br />
Subject to the terms of this Contract, the Contractor shall carry out,<br /><br />
at its own expense and financial risk, all the necessary Petroleum<br /><br />
Operations to implement an approved Development Plan. However, if the<br /><br />
Contractor is able to demonstrate to the reasonable satisfaction of the<br /><br />
Coordination Committee that exploitation turns out not to be<br /><br />
commercially profitable, the Coordination Committee shall decide on the<br /><br />
steps to be taken as a consequence of such an event, and the Contractor<br /><br />
shall not be obligated to continue implementation of the original<br /><br />
Development Plan.<br /><br />

ARTICLE 10<br /><br />
ANNUAL WORK PROGRAMMES AND BUDGETS<br /><br />
10.1<br /><br />
<br /><br />
The Contractor shall be responsible for the procurement of<br /><br />
installations, equipment and supplies and entering into contracts for<br /><br />
the purchase of goods and services with Foreign Subcontractors and<br /><br />
others required for Petroleum Operations, all in accordance with<br /><br />
approved Annual Work Programmes and Budgets. Such activities may be<br /><br />
delegated to the Operating Company.<br /><br />
<br /><br />
10.2<br /><br />
<br /><br />
Within ninety (90) Days after the Effective Date, the Contractor shall<br /><br />
submit to the Co-ordination Committee for its approval an Annual Work<br /><br />
Programme and Budget for the remainder of the then current Calendar<br /><br />
Year and a forecast for the next succeeding Calendar Year.<br /><br />
<br /><br />
10.3<br /><br />
<br /><br />
Before 31 October in each Calendar Year, the Contractor shall prepare<br /><br />
and submit to the Co-ordination Committee for its review a proposed<br /><br />
Annual Work Programme and Budget for the next Calendar Year. Article<br /><br />
6.4 shall apply to the approval of Annual Work Programmes and Budgets<br /><br />
and modifications thereto.<br /><br />
<br /><br />
10.4<br /><br />
<br /><br />
In connection with the review and approval of an Annual Work Programme<br /><br />
and Budget, the Contractor shall submit to the Co-ordination Committee<br /><br />
such supporting data as may be requested by the Co-ordination<br /><br />
Committee.<br /><br />
<br /><br />
10.5<br /><br />
<br /><br />
Subject to the provisions of Article 6.4, the Contractor may, in<br /><br />
accordance with the following provisions, incur expenditures in excess<br /><br />
of an approved Budget or expenditures outside an approved Budget in<br /><br />
carrying out an approved Work Programme, provided that the objectives<br /><br />
in the approved Work Programme are not substantially changed, subject<br /><br />
to the following conditions:<br /><br />
(i)<br /><br />
<br /><br />
In carrying out an approved Annual Work Programme the<br /><br />
Contractor may, if necessary, incur excess expenditures of no<br /><br />
more than ten percent (10%) of the approved Budget in any<br /><br />
<br /><br />
specified budgetary category. The Contractor<br /><br />
42<br /><br />
<br /><br />
<PAGE><br /><br />
<br /><br />
shall report quarterly the aggregate amount of all such excess<br /><br />
expenditures to the Co-ordination Committee for information.<br /><br />
(ii)<br /><br />
<br /><br />
For the efficient performance of Petroleum Operations, the<br /><br />
Contractor may, without approval, undertake certain individual<br /><br />
projects which are not included in an approved Annual Work<br /><br />
Programme and Budget, for a maximum expenditure of two hundred<br /><br />
and fifty thousand US$ (US$250,000) per Calendar Year, but<br /><br />
shall, within ten (10) Days after such expenditures are<br /><br />
incurred, report to the Co-ordination Committee for<br /><br />
information.<br /><br />
<br /><br />
(iii)<br /><br />
<br /><br />
Excess expenditures under this Article 10.5 shall not exceed<br /><br />
five percent (5%) of the approved or modified annual Budget<br /><br />
for the Calendar Year. If such excess is expected to be in<br /><br />
excess of said five percent (5%) of the approved total annual<br /><br />
Budget, the Contractor shall present its reasons therefor to<br /><br />
the Co-ordination Committee and obtain its approval prior to<br /><br />
incurring such expenditures.<br /><br />
<br /><br />
10.6<br /><br />
<br /><br />
In case of emergency, the Contractor (or the Operating Company on<br /><br />
behalf of the Contractor) may incur emergency expenditures for the<br /><br />
amount actually needed but shall report such expenditures to the<br /><br />
Co-ordination Committee as soon as practicable after they are made.<br /><br />
Such emergency expenditures shall not be subject to Article 10.5 above.<br /><br />
<br /><br />
10.7<br /><br />
<br /><br />
Except as provided otherwise in this Contract, Petroleum Operations<br /><br />
will only be performed in accordance with an approved or modified<br /><br />
Annual Work Programme and Budget.<br /><br />
