ARTICLE 11<br /><br />
ALLOCATION OF PRODUCTION, RECOVERY OF COSTS AND<br /><br />
EXPENSES, PRODUCTION SHARING, AND RIGHT OF EXPORT<br /><br />
11.1<br /><br />
<br /><br />
The Contractor shall provide or procure the provision of all resources,<br /><br />
including funds, required to conduct Petroleum Operations under<br /><br />
approved Annual Work Programmes under this Contract, except as<br /><br />
otherwise provided in this Contract, and the Contractor shall be<br /><br />
entitled to recover its Costs and Expenses from Petroleum produced from<br /><br />
the Contract Area as provided below.<br /><br />
<br /><br />
11.2<br /><br />
<br /><br />
Prior Costs and Expenses and Prior Cost Recovery Petroleum<br /><br />
11.2.1<br /><br />
<br /><br />
Cost and Expenses incurred by the Contractor or IVOG in<br /><br />
connection with Petroleum Operations prior to the Effective<br /><br />
Date and summarised in Annex F shall be deemed to be Costs and<br /><br />
Expenses for the purposes of this Contract and shall be deemed<br /><br />
to be incurred on the Effective Date and shall be fully<br /><br />
recoverable from Cost Recovery Petroleum in accordance with<br /><br />
the provisions of this Contract.<br /><br />
<br /><br />
11.2.2<br /><br />
<br /><br />
Costs and Expenses incurred by the Contractor between 1<br /><br />
January 2000 and the Effective Date, but not included in Annex<br /><br />
F, shall be audited as soon as possible thereafter. Subject to<br /><br />
approval by the Co-ordination Committee and the State Agency,<br /><br />
such Costs and Expenses shall be deemed to be Costs and<br /><br />
Expenses for the purposes of this Contract and shall be deemed<br /><br />
to be incurred on the Effective Date and shall be fully<br /><br />
recoverable from Cost Recovery Petroleum in accordance with<br /><br />
the provisions of this Contract.<br /><br />
<br /><br />
11.2.3<br /><br />
<br /><br />
Cost Recovery Petroleum taken by the Contractor in connection<br /><br />
with Petroleum Operations prior to the Effective Date and<br /><br />
summarised in Annex F shall be deemed to be Cost Recovery<br /><br />
Petroleum for the purposes of this Contract and shall be<br /><br />
deemed to have been taken on the Effective Date<br /><br />
<br /><br />
<PAGE><br /><br />
<br /><br />
44<br /><br />
<br /><br />
11.3<br /><br />
<br /><br />
The Contractor shall have the right to use free of charge Petroleum<br /><br />
produced from the Contract Area to the extent required for Petroleum<br /><br />
Operations under the Contract. The amount of Petroleum which the<br /><br />
Contractor shall be entitled to use for Petroleum Operations shall not<br /><br />
exceed the amount which would be expected to be used in accordance with<br /><br />
international Petroleum industry practice in the exercise of Good<br /><br />
Oilfield Practices. For the avoidance of doubt, such Petroleum shall be<br /><br />
used only for the benefit of Petroleum Operations and not for the<br /><br />
personal gain of any Party.<br /><br />
<br /><br />
11.4<br /><br />
<br /><br />
Available Crude Oil and Available Natural Gas shall be measured at the<br /><br />
applicable Measurement Point and allocated as set forth below in<br /><br />
Articles 11.5 and 11.10.<br /><br />
<br /><br />
11.5<br /><br />
<br /><br />
The Contractor shall be entitled to recover all Costs and Expenses<br /><br />
incurred in respect of Petroleum Operations from a maximum of fifty<br /><br />
percent (50%) per Calendar Quarter of all Available Crude Oil and<br /><br />
Available Natural Gas from the Contract Area (hereinafter referred to<br /><br />
as Cost Recovery Crude Oil and Cost Recovery Natural Gas, as the case<br /><br />
may be).<br /><br />
Recovery of Costs and Expenses shall be in a manner consistent with the<br /><br />
Accounting Procedure and Article 11.6.<br /><br />
<br /><br />
11.6<br /><br />
<br /><br />
Costs and Expenses shall be recoverable from Cost Recovery Petroleum on<br /><br />
a first in, first out basis (i.e. Costs and Expenses incurred will be<br /><br />
recovered according to the date they were incurred, earliest first and<br /><br />
measured in US$ in accordance with Article 18.1) and shall be<br /><br />
calculated on a Calendar Quarter basis.<br /><br />
<br /><br />
11.7<br /><br />
<br /><br />
To the extent that in a Calendar Quarter outstanding recoverable Costs<br /><br />
and Expenses related to the Contract Area exceed the value of all Cost<br /><br />
Recovery Crude Oil and Cost Recovery Natural Gas for such Calendar<br /><br />
Quarter, the excess shall be carried forward for recovery in the next<br /><br />
succeeding Calendar Quarters until fully recovered, but in no case<br /><br />
after termination of the Contract. In amplification of the foregoing a<br /><br />
full audit shall be undertaken in every Calendar Year to ensure<br /><br />
compliance, among other matters, with the principles of Article 11.5.<br /><br />
<br /><br />
<PAGE><br /><br />
<br /><br />
45<br /><br />
<br /><br />
11.8<br /><br />
<br /><br />
Recovery of Costs and Expenses shall be achieved by transferring to a<br /><br />
Party at the Measurement Point title to quantities of Cost Recovery<br /><br />
Petroleum of equivalent value (determined in accordance with Article<br /><br />
12) to the Costs and Expenses to be recovered in accordance with this<br /><br />
Article 11. [No change]<br /><br />
<br /><br />
11.9<br /><br />
<br /><br />
To the extent that the value of Cost Recovery Petroleum received by a<br /><br />
Party from the Contract Area during a Calendar Quarter is greater or<br /><br />
less than the Party was entitled to receive for that Calendar Quarter,<br /><br />
an appropriate adjustment shall be made in accordance with the<br /><br />
Accounting Procedure in the subsequent Calendar Quarters.<br /><br />
<br /><br />
11.10<br /><br />
<br /><br />
Following recovery of Costs and Expenses from Cost Recovery Petroleum<br /><br />
in each Calendar Quarter in accordance with the provisions of this<br /><br />
Article 11, the remaining Petroleum, including any portion of Cost<br /><br />
Recovery Petroleum not then required or available for recovery of Costs<br /><br />
and Expenses (hereinafter referred to as "Profit Oil" or "Profit<br /><br />
Natural Gas") shall be allocated in each Calendar Quarter between<br /><br />
Georgian Oil and the Contractor as follows:<br /><br />
11.10.1 Fifty percent (50%) of the Profit Oil (and Profit Natural Gas)<br /><br />
resulting from Petroleum Operations will be allocated to<br /><br />
Georgian Oil and fifty percent (50%) to the Contractor, so<br /><br />
long as the cumulative Costs and Expenses, plus finance costs<br /><br />
incurred by the Contractor exceed the value of the cumulative<br /><br />
Cost Recovery Petroleum, cumulative Profit Oil and cumulative<br /><br />
Profit Natural Gas given to the Contractor, calculated from<br /><br />
the Effective Date to the end of the prior quarter.<br /><br />
<br /><br />
11.10.2 If at any time the value of the cumulative Cost Recovery<br /><br />
Petroleum, cumulative Profit Oil and cumulative Profit Natural<br /><br />
Gas delivered to the Contractor exceeds the cumulative Costs<br /><br />
and Expenses, plus interest incurred by the Contractor (but<br /><br />
excluding interest already included in Costs and Expenses and<br /><br />
excluding interest on interest), then seventy percent (70%) of<br /><br />
the Profit Oil (and Profit Natural Gas) resulting from<br /><br />
Petroleum Operations will be allocated to Georgian Oil and<br /><br />
thirty percent<br /><br />
<PAGE><br /><br />
<br /><br />
46<br /><br />
(30%) to the Contractor, calculated from the Effective Date to<br /><br />
the end of the prior quarter.<br /><br />
<br /><br />
11.11<br /><br />
<br /><br />
Notwithstanding Articles 11.5 and 11.10, when the value of the<br /><br />
cumulative Cost Recovery Petroleum, cumulative Profit Oil and<br /><br />
cumulative Profit Natural Gas delivered to the Contractor exceeds the<br /><br />
cumulative Costs and Expenses, plus finance costs incurred by the<br /><br />
Contractor, and calculated from the Effective Date to the end of the<br /><br />
prior quarter, then Georgian Oil will be entitled to receive, as a<br /><br />
priority, up to 250,000 tons of oil (or oil equivalent) from a maximum<br /><br />
of fifty percent (50%) per Calendar Quarter of all Available Crude Oil<br /><br />
and Available Natural Gas from the Contract Area (the Base Level Oil).<br /><br />
11.11.1 During the period that Base Level Oil is being delivered to<br /><br />
Georgian Oil, the Contractor shall be entitled to recover all<br /><br />
Costs and Expenses, calculated from the Effective Date to the<br /><br />
end of the prior quarter incurred in respect of Petroleum<br /><br />
Operations, as Cost Recovery Petroleum from a maximum of fifty<br /><br />
percent (50%) per Calendar Quarter of the remaining Available<br /><br />
Crude.<br /><br />
11.11.2 During the period that Base Level Oil is being delivered to<br /><br />
Georgian Oil, after delivery of Base Level Oil and Cost<br /><br />
Recovery Petroleum the remaining Available Crude Oil and<br /><br />
Available Natural Gas resulting from Petroleum Operations in<br /><br />
the Contract Area will be allocated as Profit Oil (and Profit<br /><br />
Natural Gas) with fifty percent (50%) being delivered to<br /><br />
Georgian Oil and fifty percent (50%) being delivered to the<br /><br />
Contractor.<br /><br />
<br /><br />
11.12<br /><br />
<br /><br />
<PAGE><br /><br />
<br /><br />
The Contractor shall prepare and provide to Georgian Oil and the State<br /><br />
Agency not less than ninety (90) Days prior to the beginning of each<br /><br />
Calendar Quarter a written<br /><br />
47<br /><br />
forecast setting out the total quantity of Petroleum that the<br /><br />
Contractor estimates can be produced and saved hereunder during each of<br /><br />
the next four (4) Calendar Quarters in accordance with Good Oilfield<br /><br />
Practices and the Annual Work Programme approved in accordance with<br /><br />
Article 10.<br /><br />
<br /><br />
11.13<br /><br />
<br /><br />
Crude Oil, whether as Cost Recovery Petroleum or as Profit Oil, shall<br /><br />
be measured at the Measurement Point for purposes of the Contract and<br /><br />
delivered to Georgian Oil and Contractor who as owners shall take in<br /><br />
kind, assume risk of loss and separately dispose of their respective<br /><br />
entitlements of Crude Oil. All Natural Gas shall be sold on a jointly<br /><br />
committed basis or as otherwise provided in accordance with Article 16<br /><br />
of this Contract.<br /><br />
<br /><br />
11.14<br /><br />
<br /><br />
For the avoidance of any doubt, title to their relevant shares of<br /><br />
Petroleum shall pass from the State to Georgian Oil and Contractor as<br /><br />
appropriate at the Measurement Point and the Operating Company will<br /><br />
have no title to any Petroleum.<br /><br />
Georgian Oil and the Contractor shall agree on procedures for taking<br /><br />
volumes of Crude Oil corresponding to their respective entitlements on<br /><br />
a regular basis and in a manner that is appropriate having regard to<br /><br />
the respective destinations and uses of the Crude Oil, all in<br /><br />
accordance with the provisions of this Contract. If necessary, Georgian<br /><br />
Oil and the Contractor will enter into a lifting agreement setting out<br /><br />
<br /><br />
the agreed procedures for taking volumes of Crude Oil, and such<br /><br />
agreement shall comply with the principles of Good Oilfield Practices.<br /><br />
Details of all Costs and Expenses approved as herein provided shall be<br /><br />
given by the Contractor to the State Agency and Georgian Oil on a<br /><br />
quarterly basis.<br /><br />

<br /><br />
<PAGE><br /><br />
<br /><br />
ARTICLE 12<br /><br />
CRUDE OIL AND NATURAL GAS VALUATION<br /><br />
12.1<br /><br />
<br /><br />
12.2<br /><br />
<br /><br />
The value of Crude Oil that constitutes Cost Recovery Crude Oil and is<br /><br />
sold by Contractor to Third Parties in "fairly valued" transactions<br /><br />
shall be the net realised price (i.e., after deducting commissions and<br /><br />
brokerages) ex works at the Measurement Point. The sale is "fairly<br /><br />
valued" if<br /><br />
(i)<br /><br />
<br /><br />
the price is the sole consideration for the sale; and<br /><br />
<br /><br />
(ii)<br /><br />
<br /><br />
the terms of the sale are not affected by any commercial<br /><br />
relationship, other than that created by the contract of sale<br /><br />
itself, between the seller or an Affiliate and the buyer or an<br /><br />
Affiliate; and<br /><br />
<br /><br />
(iii)<br /><br />
<br /><br />
the seller or an Affiliate does not have any interest in the<br /><br />
subsequent resale or disposal of the Crude Oil or any product<br /><br />
derived therefrom.<br /><br />
<br /><br />
It is the intent of the Parties that the value of Cost Recovery<br /><br />
Petroleum that is sold by Contractor other than to Third Parties in<br /><br />
"fairly valued" transactions shall reflect the prevailing international<br /><br />
market price for Crude Oil saved and sold from the Contract Area ex<br /><br />
works the Measurement Point. For the purpose of determining the value<br /><br />
and allocation of Cost Recovery Petroleum taken and disposed of by the<br /><br />
Parties and/or their assignees under this Contract during each Calendar<br /><br />
Quarter, Georgian Oil and the Contractor shall agree upon a basket of<br /><br />
no more than four (4) Crude Oils freely traded in international<br /><br />
markets, and the value of Cost Recovery Petroleum shall be adjusted to<br /><br />
reflect the weighted average daily f.o.b. prices for term contract<br /><br />
sales from Petroleum producing countries in international markets for<br /><br />
the same Calendar Quarter of such basket of Crude Oils, it being<br /><br />
understood that the following principles will apply:<br /><br />
(i)<br /><br />
<br /><br />
Each of such basket marker Crude Oils shall originate from the<br /><br />
closest<br /><br />
49<br /><br />
<br /><br />
<PAGE><br /><br />
<br /><br />
geographic location to the Contract Area as possible and have<br /><br />
the same primary geographic market as the Contract Area Crude<br /><br />
Oil being valued. The weighted average of the basket shall be<br /><br />
such that the average gravity, sulphur content and product<br /><br />
yield of the basket and the average gravity, sulphur content<br /><br />
and product yield of the Crude Oil produced under this<br /><br />
Contract shall approximate each other as nearly as is<br /><br />
possible; and<br /><br />
(ii)<br /><br />
<br /><br />
The prices for individual referenced Crude Oil markers used<br /><br />
within the basket shall be based upon the numerical average of<br /><br />
a daily report of the actual price for each referenced Crude<br /><br />
Oil marker as published in agreed internationally recognised<br /><br />
publications; and<br /><br />
<br /><br />
(iii)<br /><br />
<br /><br />
Adjustment provisions will be incorporated into the basket<br /><br />
formula to take account of transportation costs and location<br /><br />
differentials between the marker basket of Crude Oils and the<br /><br />
Crude Oil produced under this Contract arriving at a<br /><br />
designated sales point (where the sales point is not the<br /><br />
Measurement Point) and to take account of gravity and sulphur<br /><br />
content variation beyond a pre-agreed range; and<br /><br />
<br /><br />
12.3<br /><br />
<br /><br />
<PAGE><br /><br />
<br /><br />
(iv)<br /><br />
<br /><br />
Contractor's third party fairly valued sales prices received<br /><br />
for Crude Oil produced under this Contract shall be the basis<br /><br />
used to determine appropriate changes to the adjustments set<br /><br />
out in (iii) above;<br /><br />
<br /><br />
(v)<br /><br />
<br /><br />
Unless agreed otherwise, the last calculated weighted average<br /><br />
basket price shall serve as the provisional price for a<br /><br />
Calendar Quarter until a new price is determined.<br /><br />
<br /><br />
In the event that Georgian Oil and the Contractor are unable to agree<br /><br />
upon the<br /><br />
50<br /><br />
basket of Crude Oils envisaged in Article 12.2 above, or the principles<br /><br />
relating thereto, then either Georgian Oil or the Contractor or both of<br /><br />
them jointly may pursuant to Article 30, refer the matter or matters in<br /><br />
issue for determination by a Sole Expert. Pending such determination,<br /><br />
the price shall be as determined under Article 12.2 (iv) above.<br /><br />
<br /><br />
12.4<br /><br />
<br /><br />
<PAGE><br /><br />
<br /><br />
Natural Gas shall be valued at the actual revenues received by<br /><br />
Contractor less transportation, storage, treatment, processing,<br /><br />
liquefaction and all other associated costs incurred by the Contractor<br /><br />
beyond the Measurement Point in supplying Natural gas to customers<br /><br />
beyond the Measurement Point. If the Contractor bears the cost of<br /><br />
installing and operating the pipeline required to transport Natural Gas<br /><br />
produced from the Contract Area to the market for such Natural Gas and<br /><br />
such pipeline is located downstream of the Measurement Point, the<br /><br />
Contractor shall be entitled to deduct a tariff from the sales price of<br /><br />
the Natural Gas for the purpose of determining the value of Cost<br /><br />
Recovery Petroleum. The tariff associated with such natural gas<br /><br />
pipeline shall be computed on the basis of the investment incurred in<br /><br />
such pipeline, the operating costs of such pipeline and a reasonable<br /><br />
return on Contractor's investment.<br /><br />
51<br /><br />
ARTICLE 13<br /><br />
ANCILLARY RIGHTS OF THE CONTRACTOR AND OPERATING COMPANY<br /><br />
<br /><br />
13.1<br /><br />
<br /><br />
The State and Georgian Oil shall provide or otherwise procure access<br /><br />
for the Contractor to all existing facilities and infrastructure, which<br /><br />
is available on an open access basis for private commercial purposes,<br /><br />
which for the sake of clarification does not include such facilities or<br /><br />
infrastructure subject to contractual or treaty obligations or<br /><br />
restrictions, in the Contract Area owned by the State or Georgian Oil<br /><br />
necessary for the purpose of carrying out Petroleum Operations during<br /><br />
the term of the Contract. Such access shall be on terms as regards<br /><br />
access and tariffs no less favourable than the best terms then being<br /><br />
offered to other private commercial Third Parties namely non-State<br /><br />
owned entities, for comparable usage.<br /><br />
<br /><br />
13.2<br /><br />
<br /><br />
Provided that Georgian Oil and the State Agency are provided with<br /><br />
copies of the following data, the Contractor shall, subject to the<br /><br />
confidentiality provisions herein provided, have the right to use,<br /><br />
reproduce, reprocess and export all existing geoscience, engineering,<br /><br />
environmental and geodetic data (including magnetic tapes and films),<br /><br />
maps, surveys, reports, and studies it deems necessary to carry out<br /><br />
Petroleum Operations hereunder, including, but not limited to, magnetic<br /><br />
surveys, seismic surveys, well logs and analysis, core analysis, well<br /><br />
files, geological and geophysical maps and reports, reservoir studies,<br /><br />
reserve calculations, accurate geodetic co-ordinates for the location<br /><br />
of all wells and seismic lines and all other pertinent data relative to<br /><br />
the Contract Area. Georgian Oil and the Contractor may sell such data,<br /><br />
subject to the approval of the Co-ordination Committee and the prior<br /><br />
consent of the State Agency and, in the event of such approval, subject<br /><br />
to the entering into of a confidentiality agreement on terms comparable<br /><br />
to those herein set forth by the purchaser thereof. The proceeds from<br /><br />
any such sale shall be shared in accordance with the provisions of<br /><br />
Article 11.10.<br /><br />
52<br /><br />
<br /><br />
<PAGE><br /><br />
13.3<br /><br />
<br /><br />
The Contractor shall have the right within the Contract Area to conduct<br /><br />
all geoscience, engineering, environmental and geodetic studies it<br /><br />
deems necessary to carry out Petroleum Operations hereunder. Said<br /><br />
studies may include, but are not limited to, seismic surveys, magnetic<br /><br />
surveys, global positioning surveys, aerial photography, and the<br /><br />
collection of soil/water/oil/gas/rock samples for scientific and<br /><br />
environmental studies. The Contractor shall be granted access to and/or<br /><br />
permission to fly, subject to obtaining appropriate consents (which<br /><br />
will not be unreasonably withheld or delayed), over the Contract Area<br /><br />
to conduct said studies. The Contractor shall have the right to import<br /><br />
equipment and supplies necessary to conduct said studies as well as the<br /><br />
right to export data, film and samples, subject to the provisions of<br /><br />
Article 13.2, to laboratories outside the State to conduct such<br /><br />
studies.<br /><br />
<br /><br />
13.4<br /><br />
<br /><br />
The agents, employees, and personnel of the Contractor or the<br /><br />
Subcontractors, may enter or leave the Contract Area and have free<br /><br />
access, within the scope of their functions, to all installations put<br /><br />
in place by the Contractor or otherwise utilised in Petroleum<br /><br />
Operations and to installations used for Petroleum Operations outside<br /><br />
the Contract Area.<br /><br />
<br /><br />
13.5<br /><br />
<br /><br />
Subject to applicable laws, rules and regulations, as herein provided,<br /><br />
including the prior approval of any appropriate State bodies as well as<br /><br />
any local governmental bodies, and the approval of the Coordination<br /><br />
Committee to a draft Work Programme describing the utilisation<br /><br />
hereinbelow contemplated and the Development Plan and the agreement of<br /><br />
relevant landowners, the Contractor shall have the right to utilise the<br /><br />
upper soil, mature timber, clay, sand, lime, gypsum and stones other<br /><br />
than precious stones, and any other similar substances, necessary for<br /><br />
the performance of Petroleum Operations. The Contractor, subject as<br /><br />
aforesaid, may utilise the surface and subsurface water necessary for<br /><br />
Petroleum Operations on condition that reasonable efforts are taken to<br /><br />
minimise potentially adverse effects on irrigation and navigation, and<br /><br />
that land, houses and the watering places are not<br /><br />
53<br /><br />
<br /><br />
<PAGE><br /><br />
adversely affected.<br /><br />
13.6<br /><br />
<br /><br />
Subject to applicable laws, rules and regulations, as herein provided,<br /><br />
including the prior approval of any appropriate State bodies as well as<br /><br />
any local governmental bodies, obtained through the State Agency, which<br /><br />
shall not be unreasonably withheld, and the approval of the<br /><br />
Coordination Committee to a draft Work Programme describing the<br /><br />
utilisation hereinbelow contemplated and the Development Plan and the<br /><br />
agreement of relevant owners, the Contractor, to the extent necessary<br /><br />
for the performance of the Petroleum Operations, may clear land, dig,<br /><br />
pierce, drill, construct, operate and maintain pits, tanks, wells,<br /><br />
trenches, excavations, dams, canals, water pipes, reservoirs, maritime<br /><br />
storage facilities, primary distillation units, separating units for<br /><br />
first oil extraction, sulphur factories and other Petroleum producing<br /><br />
facilities, as well as pipelines, pumping stations, compressor<br /><br />
stations, generator units, power plants, high voltage lines, telephone,<br /><br />
telegraph, radio, internet connections, and any other means of public<br /><br />
or private communication (including satellite communication systems),<br /><br />
warehouses, offices, personnel housing, hospitals, schools, docks,<br /><br />
harbours, dikes, jetties, dredges, breakwaters, underwater piers and<br /><br />
other installations, ships, vehicles, railroad cars, roads, bridges,<br /><br />
ferry-boats, airplanes, airstrips and other means of transportation,<br /><br />
garages, hangars, maintenance and repair shops.<br /><br />

It is recognised by the Parties that in order to maximise the benefit<br /><br />
of Petroleum Operations to the State, Georgian Oil and the Contractor,<br /><br />
it is in the interests of the State to promote cooperation among<br /><br />
Georgian and foreign enterprises carrying on Petroleum Operations in<br /><br />

operation among themselves. The State Agency and Georgian Oil, at their<br /><br />
discretion, hereby agree to seek to promote, using reasonable efforts<br /><br />
under the circumstances, subject to contractual commitments, treaty<br /><br />
obligations and the<br /><br />

required formalities.<br /><br />

shall act individually in their capacity as employers. The works,<br /><br />
hours, wages, and all other conditions relating to their employment<br /><br />

Foreign Employees are engaged under a contract subject to Georgian law,<br /><br />

Contractor, taking into<br /><br />

<br /><br />
ARTICLE 15<br /><br />
MEASUREMENT OF PETROLEUM<br /><br />
15.1<br /><br />
<br /><br />
All Petroleum produced, Saved and not used in the Petroleum Operations<br /><br />
in accordance with Article 11.3 shall be measured at the Measurement<br /><br />
Point. Georgian Oil and State Agency shall be afforded access to the<br /><br />
Measurement Point by Contractor as long as such access does not<br /><br />
significantly interfere with Petroleum Operations.<br /><br />
<br /><br />
15.2<br /><br />
<br /><br />
The Measurement Point shall be at the end of the facilities for which<br /><br />
the costs are included as Costs and Expenses. The Measurement Point<br /><br />
shall be determined in accordance with the provisions set out in<br /><br />
Articles 9 and 11.<br /><br />
<br /><br />
15.3<br /><br />
<br /><br />
All Petroleum shall be measured in accordance with standards generally<br /><br />
acceptable in the international Petroleum industry and certified<br /><br />
Georgian standards. All measurement equipment shall be installed,<br /><br />
maintained and operated by the Contractor. The Contractor and Georgian<br /><br />
Oil and State Agency shall be entitled periodically to inspect the<br /><br />
measuring equipment installed and all charts and other measurement or<br /><br />
test data at all reasonable times. The accuracy of measuring equipment<br /><br />
shall be verified by tests at regular intervals and upon request by<br /><br />
State Agency or Georgian Oil or the Contractor, using means and methods<br /><br />
generally accepted in the international Petroleum industry.<br /><br />
<br /><br />
15.4<br /><br />
<br /><br />
Should a meter malfunction occur, the Contractor shall immediately have<br /><br />
the meter repaired, adjusted and corrected and following such repairs,<br /><br />
adjustment or correction shall have it tested or calibrated to<br /><br />
establish its accuracy. Upon the discovery of metering error, the<br /><br />
Contractor shall have the meter tested immediately and shall take the<br /><br />
necessary steps to correct any error that may be discovered.<br /><br />
<br /><br />
15.5<br /><br />
<br /><br />
In the event a measuring error is discovered, the Contractor shall use<br /><br />
all reasonable efforts to determine the correct production figures for<br /><br />
the period during which there<br /><br />
60<br /><br />
<br /><br />
<PAGE><br /><br />
<br /><br />
was a measuring error and correct previously used readings. The<br /><br />
Contractor shall submit to the Co-ordination Committee and State Agency<br /><br />
a report on the corrections carried out. In determining the correction,<br /><br />
the Contractor shall use, where required, the information from other<br /><br />
measurements made inside or outside the Development Area. If it proves<br /><br />
impossible to determine when the measuring error first occurred, the<br /><br />
commencement of the error shall be deemed to be the point in time<br /><br />
halfway between the date of the last previous test and the date on<br /><br />
which the existence of the measuring error was first discovered.<br /><br />
15.6<br /><br />
<br /><br />
All measurements for all purposes in this Contract shall be adjusted to<br /><br />
standard conditions of pressure at sea level and temperature at sixty<br /><br />
(60) degrees Fahrenheit.<br /><br />
61<br /><br />
<br /><br />
<PAGE><br /><br />
<br /><br />
ARTICLE 16<br /><br />
NATURAL GAS<br /><br />
16.1<br /><br />
<br /><br />
Associated Natural Gas<br /><br />
16.1.1<br /><br />
<br /><br />
Associated Natural Gas produced within the Contract Area shall<br /><br />
be used primarily for purposes related to the Production<br /><br />
Operations and production enhancement, including, without<br /><br />
limitation, oil treating, gas injection, gas lifting and power<br /><br />
generation.<br /><br />
<br /><br />
16.1.2<br /><br />
<br /><br />
Based on the principle of full utilisation of the Associated<br /><br />
Natural Gas and with no impediment to normal production of the<br /><br />
Crude Oil, any Development Plan shall include a plan of<br /><br />
<br /><br />
utilisation of Associated Natural Gas. If there is any excess<br /><br />
Associated Natural Gas remaining in any Oil Field after<br /><br />
utilisation pursuant to Article 16.1.1 (hereafter referred to<br /><br />
as "Excess Associated Natural Gas"), the Contractor shall<br /><br />
carry out a feasibility study regarding the commercial<br /><br />
utilisation of such Excess Associated Natural Gas.<br /><br />
If Georgian Oil and the Contractor agree that Excess<br /><br />
Associated Natural Gas has no commercial value, then such<br /><br />
Natural Gas shall be disposed of by the Contractor through<br /><br />
reinjection, venting, flaring or otherwise as may be provided<br /><br />
in an approved Development Plan, and subject to approval from<br /><br />
the State Agency.<br /><br />
If Georgian Oil and the Contractor agree that Excess<br /><br />
Associated Natural Gas has commercial value, they will<br /><br />
endeavour to enter into gas sales agreement(s) and/or other<br /><br />
commercial and/or technical arrangements with Third Parties<br /><br />
required to develop such Natural Gas. Investments in the<br /><br />
facilities necessary for production, transportation and<br /><br />
delivery of Excess Associated Natural Gas shall be made by the<br /><br />
Contractor.<br /><br />
62<br /><br />
<br /><br />
<PAGE><br /><br />
<br /><br />
If either Georgian Oil or the Contractor considers that Excess<br /><br />
Associated Natural Gas has commercial value while the other<br /><br />
considers that Excess Associated Natural Gas has no commercial<br /><br />
value, the one who considers Excess Associated Natural Gas to<br /><br />
have commercial value may utilise such Excess Associated<br /><br />
Natural Gas, at its own cost and expense and without impeding<br /><br />
the production of Crude Oil and without affecting the shares<br /><br />
of Crude Oil and Natural Gas otherwise to be allocated under<br /><br />
the other provisions of this Contract, but if such Excess<br /><br />
Associated Natural Gas is not so utilised at any time or from<br /><br />
time to time, then such Excess Associated Natural Gas shall be<br /><br />
disposed of by the Contractor, in a manner approved by the<br /><br />
State Agency.<br /><br />
16.1.3<br /><br />
<br /><br />
16.2<br /><br />
<br /><br />
Investments made in conjunction with the utilisation of both<br /><br />
Associated Natural Gas and Excess Associated Natural Gas,<br /><br />
together with investments incurred after approval of a<br /><br />
Development Plan in carrying out feasibility studies on the<br /><br />
utilisation of Excess Associated Natural Gas, shall be Costs<br /><br />
and Expenses.<br /><br />
<br /><br />
Non-associated Natural Gas<br /><br />
16.2.1<br /><br />
<br /><br />
When any Non-associated Natural Gas is discovered within the<br /><br />
Contract Area, the Contractor may present proposals for<br /><br />
appraisal and development as follows:<br /><br />
After Non-associated Natural Gas has been discovered within<br /><br />
the Contract Area, the Contractor shall present to the<br /><br />
Co-ordination Committee, a report, including, without<br /><br />
limitation, an initial estimate of the boundaries of the<br /><br />
Non-associated Natural Gas Reservoir and a range of<br /><br />
recoverable reserves.<br /><br />
The Contractor shall be required to decide whether to submit<br /><br />
an Appraisal Programme as soon as is practical in all the<br /><br />
circumstances but not later than thirty-six (36) Months from<br /><br />
the date of the submission of the<br /><br />
63<br /><br />
<br /><br />
<PAGE><br /><br />
discovery report.<br /><br />
<br /><br />
If the Contractor commits to an approved Appraisal Programme<br /><br />
for the Non-associated Natural Gas Reservoir, delineation and<br /><br />
review of the potential of the Non-associated Natural Gas<br /><br />
Reservoir will continue for a period not longer than three (3)<br /><br />
Years from the Approval of the Appraisal Programme. During the<br /><br />
<br /><br />
review period and the period of the Appraisal Programme, the<br /><br />
Contractor shall maintain all rights and interests in the<br /><br />
relevant portion of the Contract Area.<br /><br />
The expenses incurred by the Contractor in carrying out the<br /><br />
said review, evaluation and Appraisal Programme shall be Costs<br /><br />
and Expenses.<br /><br />
16.2.2<br /><br />
<br /><br />
Following the completion and review of the Appraisal<br /><br />
Programme, the Contractor shall submit an appraisal report to<br /><br />
the Co-ordination Committee and may submit a Development Plan<br /><br />
for approval in accordance with Article 9.5. Georgian Oil and<br /><br />
the Contractor shall also endeavour to finalise Gas Sales<br /><br />
Contract(s) and other agreements necessary for the commercial<br /><br />
exploitation of such Non-associated Natural Gas.<br /><br />
<br /><br />
16.2.3<br /><br />
<br /><br />
Unless otherwise agreed between the Contractor and Georgian<br /><br />
Oil, all Non-associated Natural Gas (and excess Associated<br /><br />
Natural Gas) produced from the Contract Area under a<br /><br />
Development Plan which has been approved, or deemed to have<br /><br />
been approved, by the Co-ordination Committee shall be sold by<br /><br />
the Contractor on its own behalf and as agent for Georgian Oil<br /><br />
on a joint dedicated basis on terms common to both Parties.<br /><br />
Every such agreement shall require the express approval of<br /><br />
Georgian Oil which shall not be unreasonably withheld.<br /><br />
Georgian Oil may engage independent experts, as proper and<br /><br />
reasonable, to make the necessary examination of any such<br /><br />
agreement the costs of which shall be reimbursed to Georgian<br /><br />
Oil by the Contractor and shall constitute Costs and Expenses.<br /><br />
64<br /><br />
<br /><br />
<PAGE><br /><br />
<br /><br />
<PAGE><br /><br />
<br /><br />
16.2.4<br /><br />
<br /><br />
Where Non-associated Natural Gas (or excess Associated Natural<br /><br />
Gas) is sold by the Contractor on a joint dedicated basis<br /><br />
pursuant to Article 16.2.3, the provisions of Article 11,<br /><br />
relating to the allocation of Petroleum for recovery of costs<br /><br />
and production sharing, shall apply to the distribution of the<br /><br />
proceeds from the sale of Non-associated Natural Gas with<br /><br />
effect that Georgian Oil and the Contractor shall have title<br /><br />
in undivided shares to the Non-associated Natural Gas<br /><br />
available for sale on a joint dedicated basis and will hold<br /><br />
those shares in undivided proportions equal to the proportions<br /><br />
in which during that period they were entitled to share<br /><br />
available Petroleum. Accordingly the net proceeds from the<br /><br />
sale on a joint dedicated basis of Non-associated Natural Gas<br /><br />
in any given period shall be divided between Georgian Oil and<br /><br />
the Contractor in the proportions in which they had title to<br /><br />
the Non-associated Natural Gas sold.<br /><br />
<br /><br />
16.2.5<br /><br />
<br /><br />
The production period for any Non-associated Natural Gas<br /><br />
within the Contract Area shall be a period equal to the<br /><br />
greater of the term of the Gas Sales Contract(s) or other<br /><br />
commercial Natural Gas agreement for such Non-associated<br /><br />
Natural Gas and twenty-five (25) consecutive Years beginning<br /><br />
on the date of commencement of Commercial Production of such<br /><br />
Non-associated Natural Gas. Such period shall not exceed the<br /><br />
maximum term of the Contract, plus any extensions permitted<br /><br />
under Article 4,2. Georgian Oil and the Contractor shall<br /><br />
endeavour to conclude Gas Sales Contract(s) and implement a<br /><br />
Development Plan for Non-associated Natural Gas so as to<br /><br />
deplete each Reservoir within its production period and within<br /><br />
the term of this Contract, subject always to the application<br /><br />
of Good Oilfield Practices.<br /><br />
<br /><br />
16.2.6<br /><br />
<br /><br />
In the event that the development of Non-associated Natural<br /><br />
Gas appears to be uneconomic under the provisions of this<br /><br />
Contract, the Parties shall meet to discuss amending the terms<br /><br />
of this Contract. In the event the<br /><br />
65<br /><br />
Parties are unable to agree upon modifications to make<br /><br />
development, production, and marketing of a Non-associated<br /><br />
<br /><br />
Natural Gas discovery economic to the Contractor, the State<br /><br />
and Georgian Oil agree that they will not enter into any<br /><br />
arrangements for the development of such Non-associated<br /><br />
Natural Gas discovery with any Third Parties under less<br /><br />
favourable terms to the State and Georgian Oil than the<br /><br />
Contractor's last offer under the negotiations above, without<br /><br />
first offering such development and terms to the Contractor.<br /><br />
State and Georgian Oil shall notify Contractor in writing<br /><br />
within thirty (30) days of receipt of any such offer, giving<br /><br />
the full details of such offer. Contractor shall have one<br /><br />
hundred eighty (180) days following its receipt of notice of<br /><br />
the Third Party offer to match the offer. This right of first<br /><br />
refusal shall run concurrent with the term of this Contract<br /><br />
and shall survive the expiration or termination of this<br /><br />
Contract for a period of five (5) years. If the Third Party<br /><br />
offer to the State and Georgian Oil is on more favourable<br /><br />
commercial terms to the State and Georgian Oil than<br /><br />
Contractor's last offer, the above limitation on the State and<br /><br />
Georgian Oil shall not apply.<br /><br />
16.3<br /><br />
<br /><br />
The Contractor may participate in the installation and operation of the<br /><br />
pipeline(s) required to transport Non-associated Natural Gas produced<br /><br />
from the Contract Area to the market for such Non-associated Natural<br /><br />
Gas and share with Georgian Oil in any revenues, in the proportion in<br /><br />
which Article 11 they were entitled to share available Petroleum,<br /><br />
generated from the use of said pipeline(s) by others. If the Contractor<br /><br />
participates in the installation and operation of such pipeline(s), the<br /><br />
installation and operation of such pipeline(s) shall be included in<br /><br />
Development Plan and Petroleum Operations under this Contract.<br /><br />
<br /><br />
16.4<br /><br />
<br /><br />
If the State-owned company or other entity, or Georgian Oil provides<br /><br />
Natural Gas<br /><br />
<br /><br />
<PAGE><br /><br />
<br /><br />
66<br /><br />
transportation services to the Contractor, then the tariffs charged to<br /><br />
the Contractor for such services shall be non-discriminatory,<br /><br />
reasonably based on the investment necessary to provide the<br /><br />
transportation services and in no event will exceed the rates then<br /><br />
available to other Third Parties for comparable services based on<br /><br />
comparable usage and comparable agreement terms. The State through such<br /><br />

that such transportation services will be provided in a time frame that<br /><br />
will not delay field development, all as may be set forth in an<br /><br />

<br /><br />
16.5<br /><br />
<br /><br />
The Co-ordination Committee may appoint a Marketing Team to investigate<br /><br />

markets and, if necessary, improved Natural Gas terms which may<br /><br />
include, among other things with respect to Natural Gas:<br /><br />
the local Georgian market needs and demands;<br /><br />
the Parties shall have the right to submit potential customers for<br /><br />
Natural Gas sales;<br /><br />
the local Georgian market shall have priority if the commercial terms<br /><br />

available to Contractor in other markets;<br /><br />
provisions for a holiday or exemption from Profits Tax and Mineral<br /><br />
Usage Tax;<br /><br />
Cost Recovery out of up to 100% of production; and<br /><br />
a reduced share of the Profit Natural Gas for the Parties representing<br /><br />
the State.<br /><br />

ARTICLE 17<br /><br />

TAX/FISCAL REGIME<br /><br />
17.1<br /><br />
<br /><br />
In the event that Contractor introduces other Contractors to this<br /><br />

individually.<br /><br />
<br /><br />
17.2<br /><br />
<br /><br />
Contractor, Foreign Subcontractor, Foreign Employee and Operating<br /><br />
Company shall be entitled to full and complete exemption from all Taxes<br /><br />
prior to or after the Effective Date of this Contract, except as<br /><br />
otherwise provided for in this Contract and the Georgian Tax Code. It<br /><br />
is acknowledged by the Parties that any modification of Taxes payable<br /><br />
or imposition of new Taxes may be cause for enforcement of the<br /><br />
provisions of Article 27.3 of this Contract at the discretion of the<br /><br />
Contractor.<br /><br />
<br /><br />
17.3<br /><br />
<br /><br />
It is acknowledged that Georgia may enter into Double Tax Treaties<br /><br />
which may have the effect of giving relief from Taxes to, but not<br /><br />
limited to, the Contractor, Foreign Subcontractors and Foreign<br /><br />
Employees.<br /><br />
<br /><br />
17.4<br /><br />
<br /><br />
Contractor Party shall be subject to the following Taxes in accordance<br /><br />
with the Laws of Georgia as set forth in the Tax Code of Georgia in<br /><br />
effect on the date of signing of this Contract:<br /><br />
(i)<br /><br />
<br /><br />
the Tax on Profits (the "Profit Tax") which is at the rate<br /><br />
currently prescribed in the Tax Code of Georgia for those<br /><br />
existing agreements that were signed prior to entry into force<br /><br />
of the Tax Code of Georgia;<br /><br />
<br /><br />
(ii)<br /><br />
<br /><br />
the Mineral Usage Tax (the "Mineral Usage Tax");<br /><br />
<br /><br />
(iii)<br /><br />
<br /><br />
VAT on Local Sales;<br /><br />
<br /><br />
(iv)<br /><br />
<br /><br />
Social Tax and Medical Insurance Contribution on Georgian<br /><br />
nationals ("the Social Taxes"); and<br /><br />
68<br /><br />
<br /><br />
<PAGE><br /><br />
(v)<br /><br />
<br /><br />
17.5<br /><br />
<br /><br />
Customs Duties and VAT on sales of equipment or assets<br /><br />
imported free of Customs Duties and VAT and subsequently sold<br /><br />
by Contractor for purposes other than the Petroleum<br /><br />
Operations.<br /><br />
<br /><br />
Except for the Taxes listed in Article 17.4, neither the Operating<br /><br />
Company nor any Contractor Party shall be subject to any other Taxes,<br /><br />
bonuses, duties, levies, funds or similar types of payments of any<br /><br />
nature imposed prior to the date of signing of this Contract, currently<br /><br />
or in the future by the State or any other Governmental entity or<br /><br />
subdivision of the State, including, but not limited to Enterprise<br /><br />
Property Tax, VAT (otherwise than in the cases indicated at Article<br /><br />
17.4 (iii) and (v)), Stamp Duty, Profit Repatriation Tax, Export Duty,<br /><br />
Customs Duty, Freight Tax, Dividend Tax, Land Tax, Property Transfer<br /><br />
Tax, Road Use Tax, Excise Tax, Entrepreneur's Tax, fees for<br /><br />
administration (with the exception of any Administrative Fees as<br /><br />
defined in Article 1.2) any Taxes on the transportation and export of<br /><br />
Petroleum, and any Taxes related to the assignment of all or a portion<br /><br />
of the Contractor's interest under this Contract in accordance with the<br /><br />
Laws of Georgia as set forth in the Tax Code of Georgia in effect on<br /><br />
the date of signing of this Contract.<br /><br />
In the event that the Contractor becomes liable to Taxes not listed in<br /><br />
Article 17.4 above, notwithstanding the provisions of Article 17.2 and<br /><br />
27.3, such additional Taxes shall be considered as Costs and Expenses<br /><br />
for the purposes of determining Cost Recovery Petroleum.<br /><br />
<br /><br />
17.6.<br /><br />
<br /><br />
<PAGE><br /><br />
<br /><br />
Contractor Party shall be liable for the Profit Tax at the rate of ten<br /><br />
percent (10%) on the taxable base defined in Article 17.8. The rate of<br /><br />
Mineral Usage Tax shall be five percent (5%) on the value of produced<br /><br />
Petroleum excluding VAT for the duration of the Contract.<br /><br />
69<br /><br />
<br /><br />
17.7<br /><br />
<br /><br />
Assumption, payment and discharge of taxes shall take place as follows:<br /><br />
The State shall ensure that Georgian Oil (or its successors or<br /><br />
assignees) shall assume, pay and discharge when due, in the name and on<br /><br />
behalf of Contractor, Profit Tax liability and Mineral Usage Tax<br /><br />
liability for each Calendar Year calculated in accordance with this<br /><br />
Article 17 out of Georgian Oil's share of Profit Oil and Profit Natural<br /><br />
Gas for each Calendar Year. For the avoidance of ambiguity, this<br /><br />
obligation of Georgian Oil as related to the Mineral Usage Tax and<br /><br />
Profit Tax under this Article 17.7 shall also extend to the Operating<br /><br />
Company if, under the laws of Georgia, under the License it is deemed<br /><br />
liable instead of the Contractor Parties for the payment of Profit Tax<br /><br />
or Mineral Usage Tax. Also for the avoidance of ambiguity, Georgian Oil<br /><br />
shall have the obligation to obtain any necessary consents or approvals<br /><br />
from the Tax Inspectorate in relation to the provisions of this Article<br /><br />
17.7 within one (1) month from the date of signing this Contract, as<br /><br />
more fully described in Article 32.2.<br /><br />
The obligation of Georgian Oil to assume, pay and discharge<br /><br />
Contractor's entire Profit Tax and Mineral Usage Tax liability in<br /><br />
accordance with the provisions of this Article 17.7 shall fulfil the<br /><br />
entire Profit Tax and Mineral Usage Tax liability of Contractor and of<br /><br />
Operating Company, if it has any such liability, as set out above.<br /><br />
<br /><br />
17.8<br /><br />
<br /><br />
The calculation of the taxable base for Contractor for a Calendar Year<br /><br />
shall be as follows:<br /><br />
17.8.1<br /><br />
<br /><br />
The taxable base for each Contractor Party shall be determined<br /><br />
as the total of each such Contractor Party's sales revenues<br /><br />
from Cost Recovery Petroleum, Profit Oil and Profit Natural<br /><br />
Gas acquired by that Contractor Party pursuant to Article 11<br /><br />
of this Contract increased by an amount equal to the<br /><br />
Contractor's Profit Tax and Mineral Usage Tax paid on its<br /><br />
behalf by Georgian Oil pursuant to Article 17.7 of this<br /><br />
Contract and reduced by the amount of Mineral Usage Tax and<br /><br />
Deductions.<br /><br />
70<br /><br />
<br /><br />
<PAGE><br /><br />
<br /><br />
"Deductions" shall include all costs incurred by each Contractor Party<br /><br />
during each Calendar Year in connection with Petroleum Operations,<br /><br />
whether incurred in Georgia or elsewhere and whether paid by the<br /><br />
Contractor Party directly or through the Operating Company, including<br /><br />
the following:<br /><br />
<br /><br />
17.8.2<br /><br />
<br /><br />
(i)<br /><br />
<br /><br />
the Contractor Party's Costs and Expenses recoverable<br /><br />
from Cost Recovery Petroleum in accordance with<br /><br />
Article 11; and<br /><br />
<br /><br />
(ii)<br /><br />
<br /><br />
the Contractor Party's share of costs and the<br /><br />
Contractor Party's own costs incurred during a<br /><br />
Calendar Year in respect of Petroleum Operations<br /><br />
which are not included in Costs and Expenses<br /><br />
determining Cost Recovery Petroleum in Article 11 of<br /><br />
this Contract, including any transportation and other<br /><br />
associated costs incurred when Profit Oil is not sold<br /><br />
at the Measurement Point; and<br /><br />
<br /><br />
(iii)<br /><br />
<br /><br />
any loss calculated in accordance with Article 17.9<br /><br />
of this Contract.<br /><br />
<br /><br />
Sales revenues from Cost Recovery Petroleum shall be defined<br /><br />
as the value of the volumes of Cost Recovery Petroleum taken<br /><br />
and disposed of by the Contractor and/or his assignees under<br /><br />
this Contract during a Calendar Year and determined by<br /><br />
applying the principles of valuation set out in Article 12 of<br /><br />
this Contract. Sales revenues from Profit Oil and Profit<br /><br />
Natural Gas shall be defined as the value of the volumes of<br /><br />
Profit Oil and Profit Natural Gas taken and disposed of by the<br /><br />
Contractor and/or his assignees under this Contract during a<br /><br />
Calendar Year.<br /><br />
Profit Oil volumes and Profit Natural Gas volumes sold to<br /><br />
Third Parties will be valued at the actual price received at<br /><br />
<br /><br />
the Measurement Point where actually sold at the Measurement<br /><br />
Point. Where Profit Oil volumes are not<br /><br />
71<br /><br />
<br /><br />
<PAGE><br /><br />
<br /><br />
sold at the Measurement Point, they shall be valued at the<br /><br />
actual price received at the sales point less transportation<br /><br />
and other associated costs incurred by the Contractor in<br /><br />
transporting such Profit Oil from the Measurement Point to the<br /><br />
actual sales point. The value of sales of Profit Oil and<br /><br />
Profit Natural Gas to any Affiliate or sales involving barter<br /><br />
will be determined by applying the principles of valuation as<br /><br />
set out in Article 12 of this Contract.<br /><br />
17.8.3<br /><br />
<br /><br />
For the purposes of this Article 17 and specifically for the<br /><br />
purposes of calculating the taxable base of Contractor in<br /><br />
accordance with this Article 17.8 and Article 17.9, the costs<br /><br />
and expenses approved by the Parties pursuant to Article 11.2<br /><br />
shall be deemed to have been incurred on the Effective Date of<br /><br />
this Contract.<br /><br />
<br /><br />
17.9<br /><br />
<br /><br />
If in calculating the taxable base of Contractor the total sum of<br /><br />
Deductions exceeds sales revenues from Cost Recovery Petroleum, Profit<br /><br />
Oil and Profit Natural Gas in any Calendar Year, the resulting loss may<br /><br />
be carried forward by Contractor to the following Calendar Year and to<br /><br />
subsequent Calendar Years, one at a time in chronological order, and<br /><br />
shall be deductible in full and without restriction in computing<br /><br />
Contractor's taxable base in such Calendar Year(s) until such time as<br /><br />
the loss is wholly offset against Contractor's taxable base, or<br /><br />
otherwise in accordance with the Tax Code of Georgia.<br /><br />

17.21<br /><br />
<br /><br />
The only Taxes to be levied by the State or by any other Governmental<br /><br />

any person or other legal entity making payments to a Foreign<br /><br />
Subcontractor (the "Withholding Tax"). The Withholding Tax shall be<br /><br />
calculated and will apply as follows:<br /><br />
17.21.1 The Withholding Tax will be calculated at a fixed rate of four<br /><br />
percent (4%) of any payment made to a Foreign Subcontractor in<br /><br />
respect of work and/or services undertaken in Georgia in<br /><br />
connection with Petroleum Operations pursuant to this<br /><br />
<br /><br />
Contract. For the avoidance of doubt, work and/or services<br /><br />
performed by Foreign Subcontractors outside Georgia are not<br /><br />
subject to the Withholding Tax.<br /><br />
17.21.2 Any person or other legal entity making payments to a Foreign<br /><br />
Subcontractor must pay the Withholding Tax to the Tax<br /><br />
Inspectorate upon making the payment to the Foreign<br /><br />
Subcontractor. The Tax<br /><br />
<PAGE><br /><br />
<br /><br />
75<br /><br />
Inspectorate shall issue the person or other legal entity<br /><br />
making the payment with proper official receipts in the name<br /><br />
of the Foreign Subcontractor within fifteen (15) Days of the<br /><br />
payment of the Withholding Tax that evidence the payment of<br /><br />
the Withholding Tax stating the date, the amount, and other<br /><br />
particulars customary for such receipts. The State Agency and<br /><br />
Georgian Oil shall provide the Contractor with any necessary<br /><br />
assistance in obtaining such receipts.<br /><br />
17.21.3 In the event that such Withholding Tax is paid late, the<br /><br />
person responsible for the Withholding Tax to the Tax<br /><br />
Inspectorate shall be subject to interest at the rate<br /><br />
determined by the Tax Code of Georgia for late payment,<br /><br />
calculated from the latest date that the Withholding Tax<br /><br />
should have been paid to the Tax Inspectorate.<br /><br />
17.21.4 A Foreign Subcontractor will continue to be subject to the<br /><br />
provisions of any applicable Double Tax Treaty.<br /><br />
<br /><br />
17.22<br /><br />
<br /><br />
Value Added Tax ("VAT") shall be imposed, and VAT refunds shall be<br /><br />
made, as follows:<br /><br />
17.22.1 Goods, works and services supplied directly or indirectly to a<br /><br />
Contractor Party or to the Operating Company for the purposes<br /><br />
of Petroleum Operations shall be exempt from VAT.<br /><br />
17.22.2 The Contractor shall charge VAT at the current rate of twenty<br /><br />
percent (20%) on Petroleum sold locally within Georgia which<br /><br />
is not intended for export in circumstances in which the<br /><br />
purchaser is a Georgian national or Georgian entity ("Local<br /><br />
Sales").<br /><br />
17.22.3 The Contractor shall be entitled to a refund of any VAT paid<br /><br />
on local purchases within forty-five (45) business Days of the<br /><br />
submission of a request to the Tax Inspectorate. The refund<br /><br />
shall be equal to VAT paid on local purchases in excess of VAT<br /><br />
charged on Local Sales. If a full<br /><br />
<br /><br />
<PAGE><br /><br />
<br /><br />
76<br /><br />
VAT refund is not paid within forty five (45) business Days as<br /><br />
specified above, the Contractor shall be entitled to recover<br /><br />
the relevant amount as Costs and Expenses in accordance with<br /><br />
the provisions of Article 11.<br /><br />
17.22.4 All imports, including, but not limited to, goods, equipment,<br /><br />
works or services acquired by a Contractor Party, its<br /><br />
Affiliates, their Subcontractors or the Operating Company for<br /><br />
the purpose of the Petroleum Operations shall be exempt from<br /><br />
VAT.<br /><br />
17.22.5 Exports of Petroleum by each Contractor Party shall be liable<br /><br />
to VAT at the rate of zero per cent (0%).<br /><br />
17.22.6 All exports and re-exports by a Contractor Party or its<br /><br />
Affiliates or Subcontractors of goods, works and services<br /><br />
supplied for the purposes of Petroleum Operations, including,<br /><br />
but not limited to, re-export of goods imported into Georgia<br /><br />
for the purposes of Petroleum Operations shall be exempt from<br /><br />
VAT or be liable to VAT at the rate of zero percent (0%) as<br /><br />
the case may be.<br /><br />
<br /><br />
17.22.7 The Tax Inspectorate shall provide each Contractor Party and<br /><br />
its Affiliates, Operating Company and Foreign Subcontractors<br /><br />
with certificates confirming the VAT exemption provided in the<br /><br />
Tax Code of Georgia and referred to in Articles 17.23.1 and<br /><br />
17.23.4 within thirty (30) Days of the Contractor Party<br /><br />
requesting such a certificate. State Agency and Georgian Oil<br /><br />
shall provide the Contractor with any necessary assistance in<br /><br />
this respect.<br /><br />
77<br /><br />
<br /><br />
<PAGE><br /><br />
17.23<br /><br />
<br /><br />
Contractor and its Affiliates shall have no liability or responsibility<br /><br />
for any Taxes which its Subcontractors do not pay or for any other<br /><br />
failure of such Subcontractors to comply with the laws of Georgia.<br /><br />
<br /><br />
17.24<br /><br />
<br /><br />
The Contractor shall treat a Subcontractor as a Foreign Subcontractor<br /><br />
for the purposes of Article 17.21 provided that:<br /><br />
(i)<br /><br />
<br /><br />
the Subcontractor is a legal entity organised outside Georgia;<br /><br />
and<br /><br />
<br /><br />
(ii)<br /><br />
<br /><br />
the Subcontractor has demonstrated to the Contractor's<br /><br />
satisfaction that it does not have a Georgian Tax registration<br /><br />
certificate.<br /><br />

ARTICLE 18<br /><br />
ACCOUNTING, FINANCIAL REPORTING AND AUDIT<br /><br />
18.1<br /><br />
<br /><br />
The Contractor shall maintain books and accounts of Petroleum<br /><br />
Operations in accordance with the Accounting Procedure. These shall be<br /><br />
maintained in US$ in accordance with generally accepted international<br /><br />
Petroleum industry accounting principles, which US$ maintained books<br /><br />
and accounts shall control for the purposes of this Contract and the<br /><br />
rights and obligations of the Parties hereunder. In addition, these<br /><br />
books and accounts shall also be maintained in Lari to the extent<br /><br />
required and provided by law. All books and accounts which are made<br /><br />
available to Georgian Oil and the State in accordance with the<br /><br />
provisions of the Accounting Procedure shall be prepared both in the<br /><br />
Georgian and English languages.<br /><br />
<br /><br />
18.2<br /><br />
<br /><br />
The Accounting Procedure specifies the procedure to be used to verify<br /><br />
and establish promptly and conclusively the amount of Costs and<br /><br />
Expenses in respect of the matters covered by this Contract.<br /><br />
<br /><br />
18.3<br /><br />
<br /><br />
Sales revenues, expenditures, financial results, tax liabilities, and<br /><br />
loss carry-forwards of Contractor shall be determined in accordance<br /><br />
with the rules, rights, and obligations set forth in this Contract in<br /><br />
so far as such sales revenues, expenditures, financial results, tax<br /><br />
liabilities, and loss carry-forwards are related to Petroleum<br /><br />
Operations under this Contract.<br /><br />
<br /><br />
18.4<br /><br />
<br /><br />
The Co-ordination Committee may, and if requested by Georgian Oil<br /><br />
shall, appoint an independent auditor of international standing,<br /><br />
familiar with international Petroleum industry accounting practice, to<br /><br />
conduct an audit of the Contractor's accounts and records in respect of<br /><br />
Petroleum Operations for each Calendar Year, provided, however, any<br /><br />
such audit shall be no more frequent than on an annual basis. The costs<br /><br />
of such auditor shall be borne by the Contractor and treated as Costs<br /><br />
and Expenses. In the event that the Co-ordination Committee cannot<br /><br />
reach agreement on the appointment of such auditor, the view of<br /><br />
Georgian Oil as to such<br /><br />
79<br /><br />
<br /><br />
<PAGE><br /><br />
appointment shall prevail.<br /><br />
18.5<br /><br />
<br /><br />
Contractor shall during the term of the Contract, at its own expense,<br /><br />
prepare and submit, in both English and Georgian, to Georgian Oil and<br /><br />
the State Agency its own financial statements for each of its<br /><br />
<br /><br />
accounting periods audited in accordance with international auditing<br /><br />
standards.<br /><br />
18.6<br /><br />
<br /><br />
<PAGE><br /><br />
<br /><br />
Pursuant to paragraph 1.3.1 of the Accounting Procedure set out in<br /><br />
Annex C, the State Agency or Georgian Oil shall have the right to audit<br /><br />
the Contractor's accounts and records at their discretion.<br /><br />

ARTICLE 19<br /><br />
CURRENCY, PAYMENTS AND EXCHANGE CONTROL<br /><br />
<br /><br />
19.1<br /><br />
<br /><br />
The Contractor and its Affiliates and the Operating Company shall have<br /><br />
the right to open, maintain, and operate Foreign Exchange bank accounts<br /><br />
both in and outside of Georgia and local currency bank accounts inside<br /><br />
Georgia.<br /><br />
<br /><br />
19.2<br /><br />
<br /><br />
The Contractor and its Affiliates and the Operating Company shall have<br /><br />
the right to transfer all funds received in or converted to Foreign<br /><br />
Exchange in Georgia to bank accounts outside of Georgia without payment<br /><br />
of any Taxes for the right to effect such transfer of funds.<br /><br />
The Contractor and its Affiliates and the Operating Company shall have<br /><br />
the right to transfer funds outside of Georgia in the form of dividends<br /><br />
or the payment of principal and interest on loans used for funding<br /><br />
Petroleum Operations without the payment of or withholding of any<br /><br />
Taxes.<br /><br />
At the Effective Date the Parties are not aware of any such taxes in<br /><br />
the Tax Code of Georgia and any subsequent imposition would result in<br /><br />
the implementation of Article 27.3.<br /><br />
<br /><br />
19.3<br /><br />
<br /><br />
The Contractor and its Affiliates and Foreign Subcontractors and the<br /><br />
Operating Company shall have the right to hold, receive and retain<br /><br />
outside Georgia and freely use all funds received and derived directly<br /><br />
or indirectly from Petroleum Operations by them outside Georgia without<br /><br />
any obligation to repatriate or return the funds to Georgia, including,<br /><br />
but not limited to, all payments received from export sales of<br /><br />
Contractor's share of Petroleum and any sales proceeds from an<br /><br />
assignment of its interest in this Contract. [No change]<br /><br />
<br /><br />
19.4<br /><br />
<br /><br />
The Contractor and its Affiliates and Foreign Subcontractors and the<br /><br />
Operating Company, with respect to Foreign Exchange maintained in<br /><br />
Georgia, shall be<br /><br />
<br /><br />
<PAGE><br /><br />
<br /><br />
81<br /><br />
exempt from all legally required or mandatory conversions of Foreign<br /><br />
Exchange into local or other currency, except to the extent such<br /><br />
conversion is non-discriminatory and required because of a national<br /><br />
emergency as declared by the State, the parliament of Georgia or the<br /><br />
national bank of Georgia. Notwithstanding the foregoing provisions of<br /><br />
this Article 19 the Contractor and the Operating Company will pay<br /><br />
citizens of Georgia and Georgian legal entities engaged by them in<br /><br />
Petroleum Operations in local currency for so long as this is a<br /><br />
requirement of the law of Georgia.<br /><br />
<br /><br />
19.5<br /><br />
<br /><br />
The Contractor and its Affiliates and Foreign Subcontractors and the<br /><br />
Operating Company have the right in accordance with applicable laws to<br /><br />
import into Georgia funds required for Petroleum Operations under this<br /><br />
Contract in Foreign Exchange.<br /><br />
<br /><br />
19.6<br /><br />
<br /><br />
The Contractor and its Affiliates and Foreign Subcontractors and the<br /><br />
Operating Company shall have the right to pay outside of Georgia for<br /><br />
goods, works and services of whatever nature in connection with the<br /><br />
conduct of Petroleum Operations under this Contract without having<br /><br />
first to transfer to Georgia the funds for such payments.<br /><br />
<br /><br />
19.7<br /><br />
<br /><br />
Whenever such a need arises, the Contractor and its Affiliates and<br /><br />
Foreign Subcontractors and the Operating Company shall be entitled to<br /><br />
purchase local currency with Foreign Exchange and convert local<br /><br />
currency into Foreign Exchange, at banks authorised to do business in<br /><br />
<br /><br />
Georgia, at the most favourable exchange rate legally available to<br /><br />
private commercial parties and in any event at an exchange rate which<br /><br />
shall be no less beneficial than that granted to other foreign<br /><br />
investors by the National Bank of Georgia, if the National Bank of<br /><br />
Georgia engages in currency exchanges for private parties, without the<br /><br />
payment of any Taxes.<br /><br />
19.8<br /><br />
<br /><br />
<PAGE><br /><br />
<br /><br />
The Contractor and its Affiliates and Foreign Subcontractors shall have<br /><br />
the right to pay outside Georgia principal and interest on loans used<br /><br />
for funding Petroleum Operations without having to first transfer to<br /><br />
Georgia the funds for such payment and without payment of any<br /><br />
withholding taxes.<br /><br />
82<br /><br />
<br /><br />
19.9<br /><br />
<br /><br />
The Contractor and its Affiliates and Foreign Subcontractors and the<br /><br />

allowances and benefits of their foreign personnel working in Georgia<br /><br />
in Foreign Exchange outside Georgia, subject to the obligations of such<br /><br />
personnel under Article 17 hereof.<br /><br />
<br /><br />
19.10<br /><br />
<br /><br />
The Contractor and its Affiliates and the Operating Company shall have<br /><br />
the right to pay their Foreign Subcontractors working on Petroleum<br /><br />
Operations in Georgia in Foreign Exchange outside Georgia, subject to<br /><br />
the obligations of the Contractor and such Foreign Subcontractors under<br /><br />
Article 17 hereof.<br /><br />

19.11.<br /><br />

Conversions of currency shall be recorded at the rate actually<br /><br />
experienced in that conversion. Expenditures incurred and amounts<br /><br />
received in currency other than US$ shall be translated to US$ at the<br /><br />
official rate as posted by the National Bank of Georgia at the close of<br /><br />
business on the date upon which such expenditures are incurred or<br /><br />
amounts received.<br /><br />

ARTICLE 20<br /><br />
IMPORT AND EXPORT<br /><br />
<br /><br />
20.1<br /><br />
<br /><br />
Contractor and each of its Affiliates and their agents, and<br /><br />
Subcontractors and the Operating Company shall have the right to import<br /><br />
and re-export from Georgia free of any Taxes, other than VAT, which<br /><br />
shall be applied at a rate of zero percent (0 %), and restrictions,<br /><br />
including, but not limited to, Customs Duties, in their own name<br /><br />
materials, equipment, machinery and tools, vehicles, spare parts,<br /><br />
foodstuffs, goods and supplies necessary in the Contractor's reasonable<br /><br />
opinion for the proper conduct and achievement of Petroleum Operations<br /><br />
and only in connection therewith. Notwithstanding the above, if for any<br /><br />
reason any Taxes are levied on import or re-export by each Contractor<br /><br />
Party and each of their Affiliates and their agents, Subcontractors and<br /><br />
the Operating Company, then such Taxes shall be treated as Costs and<br /><br />
Expenses for the purposes of determining Cost Recovery Petroleum.<br /><br />
<br /><br />
20.2<br /><br />
<br /><br />
Contractor and each of its Affiliates, their agents and Subcontractors<br /><br />
and the Operating Company shall have the right to sell any materials or<br /><br />
equipment or goods which were used in Petroleum Operations provided<br /><br />
that customs duties at the applicable rate as well as VAT and other<br /><br />
applicable Taxes shall be payable by the importer on the written down<br /><br />
value of such items, if they are sold in Georgia to a person who would<br /><br />
not be exempt from the payment of Customs Duties, VAT or other such<br /><br />
Taxes on the import of such items. The proceeds therefore shall be<br /><br />
applied as in the Accounting Procedure provided.<br /><br />
<br /><br />
20.3<br /><br />
<br /><br />
The Contractor, its customers and their carriers shall have the right<br /><br />
to freely export, free of all Taxes, other than VAT, which shall be<br /><br />
applied at a rate of zero per cent (0%), including, but not limited to,<br /><br />
Customs Duties, and at any time, the share of Petroleum to which<br /><br />
Contractor is entitled in accordance with the provisions of this<br /><br />
Contract.<br /><br />
<br /><br />
<PAGE><br /><br />
<br /><br />
84<br /><br />
<br /><br />
20.4<br /><br />
<br /><br />
Petroleum to which the Contractor is entitled in accordance with the<br /><br />
provisions of this Contract shall not be subject to any requirements<br /><br />
imposed currently or in the future by the State or any other<br /><br />
Governmental entity or subdivision of the State as to export quotas or<br /><br />
export licenses or any other similar requirements.<br /><br />
<br /><br />
20.5<br /><br />
<br /><br />
All copies of original records and data and representative portions of<br /><br />
all samples or information prepared or obtained by the Contractor and<br /><br />
its Affiliates and their Subcontractors and the Operating Company with<br /><br />
regard to activities under this Contract which is exported for use<br /><br />
thereof by the Contractor, including, but not limited to, processing,<br /><br />
analysing or studying, shall be exempt from any requirements imposed,<br /><br />
currently or in the future, by the State or any other Governmental<br /><br />
entity or subdivision of the State as to export licenses, any<br /><br />
restrictions on export and Customs Duties or Taxes with respect to such<br /><br />
data and information.<br /><br />
<br /><br />
20.6<br /><br />
<br /><br />
The Contractor shall be exempt from any obligatory registration,<br /><br />
existing currently or in the future in Georgia, as exporters of<br /><br />
Petroleum.<br /><br />
<br /><br />
20.7<br /><br />
<br /><br />
Foreign Employees of the Contractor and its Affiliates and the<br /><br />
Operating Company, and Foreign Subcontractors and their dependants<br /><br />
shall have the right after arrival to import into Georgia personal and<br /><br />
household effects free of Customs Duties or other Taxes, provided,<br /><br />
however, that Customs Duties at the applicable rate or other applicable<br /><br />
Taxes shall become payable by the importer in respect of the sales<br /><br />

import or sale of such items, provided, however, any such effects may<br /><br />
be re-exported without the payment of any Customs Duties or other<br /><br />
Taxes.<br /><br />

ARTICLE 21<br /><br />
EXPORT OF HYDROCARBONS, TRANSFER OF<br /><br />
OWNERSHIP, AND REGULATIONS FOR DISPOSAL<br /><br />
<br /><br />
21.1<br /><br />
<br /><br />
The Contractor, any purchaser from him and their respective carriers<br /><br />
shall, for the duration of this Contract, have the unrestricted right<br /><br />
to export from any export point selected by the Contractor for such<br /><br />
purpose, the share of Petroleum to which the Contractor is entitled<br /><br />
under this Contract.<br /><br />
Access to such export points shall be provided to the above parties on<br /><br />
terms, including access and tariffs, no less favourable as is then<br /><br />
generally available to private commercial Third Parties, namely<br /><br />
non-State owned or controlled entities for comparable usage.<br /><br />
<br /><br />
21.2<br /><br />
<br /><br />
Title to Petroleum produced under this Contract shall pass to Georgian<br /><br />
Oil and the Contractor at the Measurement Point unless otherwise agreed<br /><br />
in a lifting agreement.<br /><br />
<br /><br />
21.3<br /><br />
<br /><br />
The Contractor and Georgian Oil shall each be entitled to designate (at<br /><br />
their own cost) an employee, independent company or consultant who<br /><br />
shall check the liftings of Petroleum from the Measurement Point.<br /><br />
<br /><br />
21.4<br /><br />
<br /><br />
Before the Commencement of Commercial Production Georgian Oil and the<br /><br />
Contractor will enter into a lifting agreement on appropriate terms.<br /><br />
Such lifting agreement shall provide that if one of the Parties is<br /><br />
unable to lift its share of Petroleum in due time, with the result that<br /><br />
Petroleum Operations shall be interfered with or disrupted, then after<br /><br />
the giving of such notice as is practical under the circumstances, any<br /><br />
other Party may dispose of it, and thereafter at its option give back<br /><br />
to such non-lifting Party an equivalent amount of Petroleum or the<br /><br />
actual net proceeds from such disposal, after taking into account any<br /><br />
necessary costs reasonably incurred. Such lifting agreement shall also<br /><br />
provide that Contractor Parties and Georgian Oil (and any purchaser<br /><br />
from any such Party, and their respective carriers) shall have access<br /><br />
to the lifting point for lifting their shares of Petroleum subject to<br /><br />
laws, regulations and safety, capacity, environmental, scheduling and<br /><br />
<br /><br />
operational requirements.<br /><br />
86<br /><br />
<br /><br />
<PAGE><br /><br />
<br /><br />
87<br /><br />

ARTICLE 22<br /><br />
OWNERSHIP OF ASSETS<br /><br />
22.1<br /><br />
<br /><br />
Ownership of all assets, whether fixed or moveable, acquired by or on<br /><br />
behalf of the Contractor in connection with Petroleum Operations, shall<br /><br />
vest in the State, without consideration, on the day the original cost<br /><br />
thereof has been recovered by the Contractor as Costs and Expenses from<br /><br />
Cost Recovery Petroleum.<br /><br />
<br /><br />
22.2<br /><br />
<br /><br />
Notwithstanding the provisions of Article 22.1, the Contractor shall<br /><br />
enjoy continued free, exclusive and unrestricted use of all assets<br /><br />
acquired by or on behalf of the Contractor in connection with Petroleum<br /><br />
Operations at no cost or loss of benefit to the Contractor until the<br /><br />
termination of this Contract or until, if earlier, they are no longer<br /><br />
required for Petroleum Operations. The Contractor, shall bear the<br /><br />
custody and maintenance of such assets and all risks of loss or damage<br /><br />
thereto for so long as they are required for Petroleum Operations,<br /><br />
provided, however, that all costs necessary to operate, maintain and<br /><br />
repair such assets and to replace or repair any damage or loss shall be<br /><br />
recoverable as Costs and Expenses from Cost Recovery Petroleum.<br /><br />
<br /><br />
22.3<br /><br />
<br /><br />
When the Contractor relinquishes part of the Contract Area, all<br /><br />
moveable assets located in the relinquished Contract Area may be<br /><br />
transferred to any part of the remaining Contract Area for conducting<br /><br />
Petroleum Operations and all fixed assets located on the relinquished<br /><br />
Contract Area shall vest in the State. When the Contract comes to an<br /><br />
end, all moveable assets whose cost has not been recovered by the<br /><br />
Contractor as Costs and Expenses from Cost Recovery Petroleum remain<br /><br />
the property of the Contractor, subject to any adjustment necessary to<br /><br />
account for partial recovery of costs.<br /><br />
<br /><br />
22.4<br /><br />
<br /><br />
The provisions of Articles 22.1, 22.2 and 22.3. shall not apply to<br /><br />
materials or other property that are rented or leased to the<br /><br />
Contractor, its Affiliates, the Operating Company or Subcontractors or<br /><br />
which belong to employees of the Contractor, its Affiliates, the<br /><br />
Operating Company or Subcontractors<br /><br />
88<br /><br />
<br /><br />
<PAGE><br /><br />
<br /><br />
89<br /><br />
<br /><br />
<PAGE><br /><br />
