ARTICLE 23<br /><br />
INSURANCE<br /><br />
23.1<br /><br />
<br /><br />
The Contractor shall obtain and maintain for all Petroleum Operations<br /><br />
insurance of the type, and in such amount as is customary for<br /><br />
exploration and development in the international petroleum industry in<br /><br />
accordance with Good Oilfield Practices. Said insurance, without<br /><br />
prejudice to the generality of the foregoing, shall cover:<br /><br />
23.1.1<br /><br />
<br /><br />
loss or damage to any and all property, including<br /><br />
installations, equipment, pipelines and other assets, whether<br /><br />
leased or owned, for so long as they are used in the Petroleum<br /><br />
Operations;<br /><br />
<br /><br />
23.1.2<br /><br />
<br /><br />
liability to Third Parties, including property loss or damage<br /><br />
or bodily injury suffered by any Third Party;<br /><br />
<br /><br />
23.1.3<br /><br />
<br /><br />
liability for damages resulting from sudden or accidental<br /><br />
pollution arising out of Petroleum Operations;<br /><br />
<br /><br />
23.1.4<br /><br />
<br /><br />
expenses for wild well control; and<br /><br />
<br /><br />
23.1.5<br /><br />
<br /><br />
destruction of Crude Oil in storage, following extraction from<br /><br />
the Reservoir and removal or transportation to surface storage<br /><br />
facilities.<br /><br />
The Contractor shall require its Subcontractors to carry<br /><br />
insurance of the type and in such amount as is customary, for<br /><br />
on-shore exploration and development, in the international<br /><br />
petroleum industry in accordance with Good Oilfield Practices.<br /><br />
The Contractor shall exhibit to the Co-ordination Committee<br /><br />
and the State Agency certificates of insurance or other<br /><br />
statements from brokers or underwriters confirming any<br /><br />
insurance providing coverage with respect to Petroleum<br /><br />
Operations or procured pursuant to this Article 23.1,<br /><br />
including, but not limited to, the identity of the insurers,<br /><br />
types and amounts of coverage, applicable deductibles,<br /><br />
premiums paid and changes thereto. The premiums for all<br /><br />
insurance (excluding premiums for insurance covering the<br /><br />
marketing of Petroleum) obtained by the Contractor for<br /><br />
Petroleum Operations pursuant to this Article 23.1, as well<br /><br />
<br /><br />
<PAGE><br /><br />
<br /><br />
90<br /><br />
as deductibles for such insurance, in amounts as approved by<br /><br />
the Co-ordination Committee, shall be deemed to be recoverable<br /><br />
as Costs and Expenses from Cost Recovery Petroleum.<br /><br />
<br /><br />
23.2<br /><br />
<br /><br />
<PAGE><br /><br />
<br /><br />
The Contractor, notwithstanding the provisions of Article 23.1, may<br /><br />
self-insure, subject to the agreement of Georgian Oil, which shall not<br /><br />
be unreasonably withheld, it being understood that the basis of the<br /><br />
terms of any such self-insurance shall be international insurance<br /><br />
industry standards for comparable risks.<br /><br />

ARTICLE 24<br /><br />
ENVIRONMENT, HEALTH, SAFETY AND LIABILITY<br /><br />
<br /><br />
24.1<br /><br />
<br /><br />
Notwithstanding the other provisions of this Contract, the Contractor<br /><br />
shall indemnify and hold harmless the State and Georgian Oil against<br /><br />
all losses, damages and liability arising under any claim, demand,<br /><br />
action or proceeding brought or instituted against the State or<br /><br />
Georgian Oil by any employee of the Contractor or any Subcontractor or<br /><br />
dependent thereof, for personal injuries, industrial illness, death or<br /><br />
damage to personal property sustained in connection with, related to or<br /><br />
arising out of the performance or non-performance of this Contract<br /><br />
regardless of the fault or negligence in whole or in part of any entity<br /><br />
or individual; provided, however, that such losses, damages and<br /><br />
liabilities are not caused by or do not arise out of the performance or<br /><br />
non-performance of this Contract by the State and/or Georgian Oil, and<br /><br />
the State and/or Georgian Oil shall indemnify and hold the Contractor<br /><br />
(including for this purpose any Affiliate, the Operating Company and<br /><br />
all Subcontractors) harmless against all such damage, losses and<br /><br />
liabilities.<br /><br />
<br /><br />
24.2<br /><br />
<br /><br />
The Contractor (including for this purpose any Affiliate, the Operating<br /><br />
Company and all Subcontractors) shall indemnify the State and Georgian<br /><br />
Oil for all loss or damage suffered by the State or Georgian Oil<br /><br />
arising out of the Contractor's Petroleum Operations if such Petroleum<br /><br />
Operations were not in accordance with Good Oilfield Practices or<br /><br />
applicable laws, rules and regulations and, notwithstanding the<br /><br />
foregoing, for any loss or damage to the environment or any cultural or<br /><br />
national monument arising out of conduct of the Petroleum Operations;<br /><br />
provided, however, that the Contractor (including for this purpose any<br /><br />
Affiliate, the Operating Company and all Subcontractors) shall have no<br /><br />
liability hereunder if and to the extent any loss and damage is caused<br /><br />
by or arises out of any breach of this Contract (and any other<br /><br />
agreements that may be entered into by and between the Contractor, the<br /><br />
State or Georgian Oil in respect of the Petroleum Operations) or breach<br /><br />
of duty by the State or Georgian Oil. Notwithstanding the foregoing the<br /><br />
Contractor (including for this purpose any Affiliate, the Operating<br /><br />
Company and all Subcontractors) shall not be liable to the State or<br /><br />
<br /><br />
Georgian Oil for any punitive or exemplary damages or any other<br /><br />
indirect or consequential damages.<br /><br />
92<br /><br />
<br /><br />
<PAGE><br /><br />
24.3.1<br /><br />
<br /><br />
The Contractor shall not be responsible to the State or<br /><br />
Georgian Oil for, and shall bear no cost, expense or liability<br /><br />
of the State or Georgian Oil for, any claim, damage or loss to<br /><br />
the extent such claim, damage or loss does not arise out of a<br /><br />
failure to conduct Petroleum Operations as provided in Article<br /><br />
24.2.<br /><br />
<br /><br />
24.3.2<br /><br />
<br /><br />
The Contractor shall not be liable for damages arising from<br /><br />
any environmental condition or damage existing in the Contract<br /><br />
Area prior to the 10th July 1995, or caused by a Force Majeure<br /><br />
event subsequent to that date, provided, however, that<br /><br />
Contractor shall be laible for environmental conditions or<br /><br />
damages resulting from a Force Majeure event to the extent<br /><br />
that such conditions or damages result from Contractor's<br /><br />
failure to exercise Good Oilfield Practices that would have<br /><br />
prevented or ameliorated such environmental conditions or<br /><br />
damages.<br /><br />
<br /><br />
24.3.3<br /><br />
<br /><br />
Notwithstanding any other provision of this Contract,<br /><br />
Contractor and Georgian Oil acknowledge that, as of the date<br /><br />
of signing of this Contract, there exists on the Contract Area<br /><br />
certain environmental damage, and Contractor and Georgian Oil<br /><br />
agree to perform clean-up and remediation of such damage to<br /><br />
their respective properties as specified in this Article 24.3.<br /><br />
<br /><br />
24.3.4<br /><br />
<br /><br />
Not later than one Month following the Effective Date hereof,<br /><br />
Contractor and Georgian Oil shall prepare, in consultation<br /><br />
with the State Agency and with the approval of the Head of the<br /><br />
State Agency, a clean-up and remediation plan for the Contract<br /><br />
Area. Such plan shall specify the particular areas of<br /><br />
responsibility of the Contractor and Georgian Oil, and it<br /><br />
shall specify the activities required by each of them to<br /><br />
restore the portions of the Contract Area damaged by oilfield<br /><br />
activities whether prior to or subsequent to 10 July 1995, to<br /><br />
a condition acceptable under internationally accepted<br /><br />
standards for the restoration of lands<br /><br />
93<br /><br />
<br /><br />
<PAGE><br /><br />
<br /><br />
damaged by oilfield production and storage activities. The<br /><br />
Contractor and Georgian Oil shall agree a time frame for the<br /><br />
implementation and completion of the clean up and remediation<br /><br />
with the State Agency. The plan shall include work plans for<br /><br />
at least the following:<br /><br />
<br /><br />
24.3.5<br /><br />
<br /><br />
(i)<br /><br />
<br /><br />
Inspection of all wells and well bores for safety and<br /><br />
absence of leakage of Petroleum, both at the surface<br /><br />
and down hole;<br /><br />
<br /><br />
(ii)<br /><br />
<br /><br />
Plugging and abandonment, consistent with<br /><br />
internationally acceptable standards, of all wells<br /><br />
and well bores not capable of economic production;<br /><br />
<br /><br />
(iii)<br /><br />
<br /><br />
Equipping each well capable of economic production<br /><br />
with suitable wellhead equipment and casing for<br /><br />
prevention of loss or leakage of Petroleum, or repair<br /><br />
and refurbishment of existing equipment;<br /><br />
<br /><br />
(iv)<br /><br />
<br /><br />
Removal and proper disposition of spilled Petroleum,<br /><br />
drilling fluids, and other waste materials, and, to<br /><br />
the extent practicable, restoration of soil; and<br /><br />
<br /><br />
(v)<br /><br />
<br /><br />
Removal and proper disposition of all scrap, junk,<br /><br />
and surplus equipment.<br /><br />
<br /><br />
In the event that Contractor fails or refuses to submit a plan<br /><br />
under this Article 24, or fails to implement and complete<br /><br />
clean-up and remediation, the State Agency may take all steps<br /><br />
<br /><br />
to develop and implement a clean-up and remediation plan.<br /><br />
Contractor shall promptly reimburse the State Agency for all<br /><br />
costs and expenses thereof, plus five (5%) percent of such<br /><br />
costs and expense, in addition to all other penalties and<br /><br />
consequences.<br /><br />
24.3.6<br /><br />
<br /><br />
<PAGE><br /><br />
<br /><br />
The State and Georgian Oil shall indemnify the Contractor<br /><br />
against any claim, damage or loss arising from environmental<br /><br />
condition or damage existing on 10 July 1995, subject to the<br /><br />
Contractor's implementing the clean-up and remediation plan<br /><br />
described in this Article 24, and taking all reasonable<br /><br />
actions to mitigate continued impact of of such conditions or<br /><br />
damage, and excluding any<br /><br />
94<br /><br />
and all natural conditions existing on that date or<br /><br />
thereafter. It is understood that the Contractor is<br /><br />
knowledgeable concerning conditions on the Contract Area and<br /><br />
has assumed the risk of pursuing Petrleum Operations thereon.<br /><br />
<br /><br />
24.4<br /><br />
<br /><br />
In conducting Petroleum Operations, the Contractor shall operate<br /><br />
according to Good Oilfield Practices and use best endeavours to<br /><br />
minimise potential disturbances to the environment, including the<br /><br />
surface, subsurface, sea, air, flora, fauna, other natural resources<br /><br />
and property. The order of priority for actions shall be protection of<br /><br />
life, environment, cultural heritage and property.<br /><br />
<br /><br />
24.5<br /><br />
<br /><br />
The Contractor shall take all necessary steps to respond to, and shall<br /><br />
promptly notify the State Agency of, all emergency and other events<br /><br />
(including explosions, leaks and spills), occurring in relation to the<br /><br />
Petroleum Operations which are causing or likely to cause material<br /><br />
environmental damage or material risk to health and safety. Such notice<br /><br />
shall include a summary description of the circumstances and steps<br /><br />
taken and planned by the Contractor to control and remedy the<br /><br />
situation. The Contractor shall provide such additional reports to the<br /><br />
State Agency as are necessary in respect of the effects of such events<br /><br />
and the course of all actions taken to prevent further loss and to<br /><br />
mitigate deleterious effects.<br /><br />
<br /><br />
24.6<br /><br />
<br /><br />
In the event of emergency situations as set forth in 24.5, above, at<br /><br />
the request of the Contractor, the State, without prejudice and in<br /><br />
addition to any indemnification obligations the State may have<br /><br />
hereunder, shall assist the Contractor, to the extent possible, in any<br /><br />
emergency response, remedial or repair effort by making available any<br /><br />
labour, materials and equipment in reasonable quantities requested by<br /><br />
the Contractor which are not otherwise readily available to the<br /><br />
Contractor and by facilitating the measures taken by Contractor to<br /><br />
bring into Georgia personnel, materials and equipment to be used in any<br /><br />
such emergency response or remedial or repair effort. Contractor shall<br /><br />
reimburse the State's reasonable and necessary costs incurred in such<br /><br />
efforts, which reimbursed amounts shall be considered Costs and<br /><br />
Expenses.<br /><br />
<br /><br />
<PAGE><br /><br />
<br /><br />
95<br /><br />
<br /><br />
24.7<br /><br />
<br /><br />
The Contractor shall not be liable to the State, Georgian Oil or Third<br /><br />
Parties for any damages caused by contamination entering the Contract<br /><br />
Area as a result of State, Georgian Oil or Third Party activities<br /><br />
beyond or within the boundaries of the Contract Area. The State shall<br /><br />
be legally and financially responsible for any loss, damage and<br /><br />
liability, including remediation of environmental conditions which may<br /><br />
be required for safe conduct of the Petroleum Operations, caused by the<br /><br />
State's or Georgian Oil's activities beyond or within the Contract<br /><br />
Area.<br /><br />
<br /><br />
24.8<br /><br />
<br /><br />
The Contractor shall not be liable for any loss or damage, including<br /><br />
but not limited to spillage, explosion, contamination or similar<br /><br />
environmental damage, in respect of any storage facilities, pipelines<br /><br />
or means of transportation which are not under the direct possession<br /><br />
and control of the Contractor or its Affiliates or its Subcontractors<br /><br />
or the Operating Company. In addition to the foregoing, the Contractor<br /><br />
shall not be liable for any damage whatsoever in respect of the State<br /><br />
<br /><br />
share of Petroleum, storage or transportation thereof once Georgian Oil<br /><br />
has taken custody of the State share of Petroleum.<br /><br />
24.9<br /><br />
<br /><br />
The State shall make best efforts to ensure the safety and security of<br /><br />
the Contractor's property and personnel in Georgia and to protect them<br /><br />
from loss, injury and damage resulting from war (declared or<br /><br />
undeclared), civil conflict, sabotage, blockade, riot, terrorism,<br /><br />
unlawful commercial extortion, or organised crime. Notwithstanding<br /><br />
anything to the contrary contained herein, Contractor acknowledges and<br /><br />
agrees that the obligations undertaken by the State in this Article<br /><br />
24.9 are no greater than the general obligations of the State towards<br /><br />
citizens of Georgia in respect to the perils named above. Furthermore,<br /><br />
Contractor agrees that it shall have no claim for legal or equitable<br /><br />
relief for failure of the State to comply with the provisions of<br /><br />
Article 24.9, except as may be permitted by law.<br /><br />

24.10<br /><br />

ARTICLE 25<br /><br />
FORCE MAJEURE<br /><br />
25.1<br /><br />
<br /><br />
If as a result of Force Majeure, any Party, including the Contractor is<br /><br />
rendered unable, wholly or in part, to carry out its obligations under<br /><br />
this Contract, other than the obligation to pay any amounts of money<br /><br />
due, then the obligations of such Party so far as and to the extent<br /><br />
that the obligations are affected by such Force Majeure, shall be<br /><br />
suspended during the continuance of any inability so caused, but for no<br /><br />
longer period.<br /><br />
Such Party shall notify all other Parties of the Force Majeure<br /><br />
situation within (14) Days of becoming aware of the circumstances<br /><br />
relied upon and shall keep all other Parties informed of all<br /><br />
significant developments. Such notice shall give reasonably full<br /><br />
particulars of the said Force Majeure, and also estimate the period of<br /><br />
time which such Party will probably require to remedy the Force<br /><br />
Majeure. Failure to give any such notification in a timely fashion<br /><br />
shall mean that the period of Force Majeure shall be deemed to have<br /><br />
commenced on the date of the giving of such notice.<br /><br />
The affected Party shall use all reasonable diligence to remove or<br /><br />
overcome or avoid the Force Majeure situation as quickly as possible in<br /><br />
an economic manner. The period of any such non-performance or delay,<br /><br />
together with such period as may be necessary for the restoration of<br /><br />
any damage done during such delay, shall be added to the time given in<br /><br />
this Contract for the performance of any obligation dependent thereon<br /><br />
and the continuation of any right granted; provided, however, the term<br /><br />
of this Contract shall be not be extended as a result of<br /><br />
<br /><br />
<PAGE><br /><br />
<br /><br />
(i)<br /><br />
<br /><br />
any particular event of Force Majeure, if the duration of any<br /><br />
such particular event of Force Majeure which, together with<br /><br />
any period of time required for restoration, is for a period<br /><br />
of 30 Days or less; and<br /><br />
<br /><br />
(ii)<br /><br />
<br /><br />
the enactment or adoption of a law, rule or regulation by the<br /><br />
State or any local or legislative body of or within Georgia,<br /><br />
whether acting directly or through Georgian Oil, if such law,<br /><br />
rule or regulation is comparable to one which has<br /><br />
98<br /><br />
been enacted or adopted, on or before the date the Contract is<br /><br />
signed, by a member nation of the European Union or any<br /><br />
legislative or regulatory body of the European Union.<br /><br />
Notwithstanding anything to the contrary herein contained, no<br /><br />
<br /><br />
event shall constitute Force Majeure if it does not delay or<br /><br />
prevent the Contractor from engaging in the conduct of<br /><br />
Petroleum Operations.<br /><br />
For the purposes of this Contract, "Force Majeure" shall mean natural<br /><br />
calamities, strikes, sabotage and other production disorders, civil<br /><br />
disturbance, war (declared or undeclared), or other military actions,<br /><br />
terrorist or guerrilla activity, blockade, revolt, earthquake,<br /><br />
avalanche, orders, laws or decrees of any state or governmental entity<br /><br />
of any country, or other similar events beyond the control of the Party<br /><br />
claiming Force Majeure which could not have been prevented by it. [No<br /><br />
change]<br /><br />
25.2<br /><br />
<br /><br />
The exercise by Georgian Oil or by State Agency of any right under this<br /><br />
Contract shall not constitute Force Majeure under any circumstance<br /><br />
<br /><br />
25.3<br /><br />
<br /><br />
It is recognised that a Force Majeure event may pertain only to part of<br /><br />
the Contract Area. In the event part of the License is in Force Majeure<br /><br />
when a Work Programme or a relinquishment become due, then the Work<br /><br />
Programme and/or relinquishment required shall be reduced in size by a<br /><br />
ratio proportionate to the area in Force Majeure divided by the full<br /><br />
size of the then current Contract Area.<br /><br />
Likewise, the time period for a Work Programme and/or relinquishment<br /><br />
for any area under Force Majeure shall be suspended for the time it is<br /><br />
under Force Majeure.<br /><br />
99<br /><br />

ARTICLE 26<br /><br />
ASSIGNMENTS AND GUARANTEES<br /><br />
26.1<br /><br />
<br /><br />
No assignment, mortgage or charge or other encumbrance or transfer (for<br /><br />
the purposes of this Article 26, all of the foregoing an "assignment"<br /><br />
and correlatives thereof) shall be made by the Contractor of its rights<br /><br />
obligations or interests arising under this Contract other than in<br /><br />
accordance with the provisions of this Article 26.<br /><br />
<br /><br />
26.2<br /><br />
<br /><br />
Except in case of an assignment made pursuant to the provisions of<br /><br />
Articles 26.4 and 26.5, the provisions of this Section 26.2 shall first<br /><br />
apply. Any Party, (which shall include Georgian Oil, or any other<br /><br />
successor entity owned by the State, from and after its exercise of its<br /><br />
rights under this Section pursuant to which it shall have become a<br /><br />

interests hereunder or in any circumstances where there is deemed to be<br /><br />

specifying the proposed terms and conditions of the assignment.<br /><br />
Following receipt of those terms and conditions, for a period of thirty<br /><br />
(30) Days, each Party shall have the preferential right to match the<br /><br />
terms and conditions of the proposed assignment or deemed assignment.<br /><br />
This right may be exercised by any Party giving written notice within<br /><br />
said period of its intention to match the relevant terms and conditions<br /><br />
(the "Acceptance") and thereafter the relevant Parties shall negotiate<br /><br />
all necessary documentation. If, within a further period of sixty (60)<br /><br />
Days from the receipt of the Acceptance, the relevant Parties have not<br /><br />
reached substantially final agreement, the Party seeking to assign may<br /><br />
within a further period of thirty (30) Days complete an assignment to a<br /><br />
Third Party on the same terms and conditions. In amplification of the<br /><br />
foregoing sentence and for the avoidance of any doubt, any assignment<br /><br />
to a Third Party shall be subject to the assigning Party and the Third<br /><br />
Party complying with the provisions of this Article 26.<br /><br />
<br /><br />

<br /><br />

to a Third Party or another Contractor provided that<br /><br />

<br /><br />
is an entity with which the State, Georgian Oil and the<br /><br />

Any such assignment shall be subject to the prior written consent of<br /><br />

ARTICLE 27<br /><br />
CONTRACT ENFORCEMENT AND STABILISATION, AND REPRESENTATIONS AND WARRANTIES<br /><br />
27.1<br /><br />
<br /><br />
In the course of performing the Petroleum Operations, the Contractor<br /><br />
shall be subject to all applicable laws, decrees, rules and regulations<br /><br />
of Georgia.<br /><br />
<br /><br />
27.2<br /><br />
<br /><br />
The Parties agree to cooperate in every possible way in order to<br /><br />
achieve the objectives of this Contract. Subject to applicable laws,<br /><br />
decrees, rules and regulations, the State shall facilitate the exercise<br /><br />
of the Contractor's activities by granting it all necessary permits,<br /><br />
licenses and access rights as in this Contract set forth so that the<br /><br />

their own benefit and for the benefit of Georgia.<br /><br />

ARTICLE 28<br /><br />
NOTICES AND CONFIDENTIALITY<br /><br />
28.1<br /><br />
<br /><br />
Except as otherwise specifically provided, all notices authorised or<br /><br />
required between the Parties by any of the provisions of this Contract,<br /><br />
shall be in writing in Georgian and English and delivered in person, by<br /><br />
registered mail, by courier service or by fax (with a copy by mail) to<br /><br />
the addresses, including fax numbers, given for the purpose.<br /><br />
The originating notice given under any provision of this Contract shall<br /><br />
be deemed delivered only when received by the Party to whom such notice<br /><br />
is directed, and the time for such Party to deliver any notice in<br /><br />
response to such originating notice shall run from the date the<br /><br />
originating notice is received. The second or any responsive notice<br /><br />
shall be deemed delivered when received. "Received" for purposes of<br /><br />
this Article with respect to written notice delivered pursuant to this<br /><br />
Contract shall be actual delivery of the notice to the Party to be<br /><br />
notified specified in accordance with this Article.<br /><br />
Each Party shall have the right to change its address at any time<br /><br />
and/or designate that copies of all such notices be directed to another<br /><br />
person at another address, by giving written notice thereof to all<br /><br />
other Parties. Until such notice is given the respective addresses for<br /><br />
service are those set out in Annex D.<br /><br />
<br /><br />

ARTICLE 29<br /><br />
TERMINATION AND BREACH<br /><br />
29.1<br /><br />
<br /><br />
At any time, if in the opinion of the Contractor, acting reasonably and<br /><br />
in good faith, circumstances do not warrant continuation of the<br /><br />
Petroleum Operations in the Contract Area or in any Development Area,<br /><br />
the Contractor may, by giving not less than ninety (90) Days written<br /><br />
notice to that effect to the State Agency with a copy to Georgian Oil<br /><br />
relinquish its rights and be relieved of its obligations pursuant to<br /><br />
this Contract as to the Contract Area or as to that Development Area,<br /><br />
except such rights and obligations as related to the period prior to<br /><br />
such relinquishment, including, without limitation, any obligation<br /><br />
under Articles 5.3, 8 and 9.7.<br /><br />
<br /><br />
29.2<br /><br />
<br /><br />
Subject to the remaining provisions of this Article 29, the State may,<br /><br />
by written notice to the Contractor, terminate the Contract in any of<br /><br />
the following events:<br /><br />
29.2.1<br /><br />
<br /><br />
the Contractor is in material breach of the Contract<br /><br />
(excluding a breach elsewhere in this Article 29.2 referred<br /><br />
to), and such breach continues for ninety (90) Days after<br /><br />
receipt of notice of the breach;<br /><br />
<br /><br />
29.2.2<br /><br />
<br /><br />
the Contractor is in breach of Article 8 of this Contract and<br /><br />
such breach continues thirty (30) Days after receipt of notice<br /><br />
of the breach:<br /><br />
<br /><br />
29.2.3<br /><br />
<br /><br />
any material breach of the provisions of Article 26 where the<br /><br />
Contractor comprises one entity;<br /><br />
<br /><br />
29.2.4<br /><br />
<br /><br />
any failure to comply with any decision of an arbitration<br /><br />
tribunal under Article 30 within the period specified in such<br /><br />
decision or, if none is specified, ninety (90) Days from the<br /><br />
date of such decision;<br /><br />
115<br /><br />
<br /><br />
<PAGE><br /><br />
29.2.5<br /><br />
<br /><br />
any failure within a thirty (30) days to accept and to<br /><br />
commence implementation of the decision of a Sole Expert to<br /><br />
whom, pursuant to the Contract, any matter has been referred;<br /><br />
<br /><br />
29.2.6<br /><br />
<br /><br />
an Insolvency Event occurs with respect to the Contractor<br /><br />
where the Contractor comprises one entity;<br /><br />
<br /><br />
29.2.7<br /><br />
<br /><br />
is in material breach of the Contract pursuant to Article<br /><br />
26.8.<br /><br />
<br /><br />
29.2.8<br /><br />
<br /><br />
Failure to develop known and prospective Petroleum reservoirs<br /><br />
diligently as a reasonable and prudent operator would develop<br /><br />
the same under the same or similar circumstances is a material<br /><br />
breach within the meaning of this Article 29.<br /><br />
<br /><br />
29.2.9<br /><br />
<br /><br />
Failure or refusal to timely complete the clean up and<br /><br />
remediation programme established pursuant to Article 24.3.<br /><br />
<br /><br />
29.3<br /><br />
<br /><br />
In the event that more than one entity constitutes the Contractor or<br /><br />
the Parent Company, and in respect of any such entity (here in this<br /><br />
Article 29 a "Defaulting Participant") an event occurs of the kind<br /><br />
described in Articles 29.2.2, 29.2.3, 29.2.4 or 29.2.5 or any such<br /><br />
entity (also herein referred to as a "Defaulting Participant") is in<br /><br />
material breach of an obligation which as provided in the Contract is a<br /><br />
several obligation, the State and Georgian Oil will not be entitled to<br /><br />
terminate the Contract unless all the entities who constitute the<br /><br />
Contractor and the Parent Company are Defaulting Participants, but may,<br /><br />
acting together, and subject to Article 29.5, serve on the Defaulting<br /><br />
Participants a notice (hereinafter a "Default Assignment Notice").<br /><br />
<br /><br />
29.4<br /><br />
<br /><br />
Where a Default Assignment Notice has been served on a Defaulting<br /><br />
Participant, the Defaulting Participant shall forthwith,<br /><br />
unconditionally, without consideration, and free from all encumbrances,<br /><br />
assign its undivided participating share, including<br /><br />
116<br /><br />
<br /><br />
<PAGE><br /><br />
<br /><br />
rights and obligations, in the Contract to the other Contractors (the<br /><br />
"Non-Defaulting Participants") in undivided shares in proportion to the<br /><br />
undivided shares in which the Non-Defaulting Participants hold their<br /><br />
shares in the Contract and each of the Non-Defaulting Participants<br /><br />
shall be obliged to accept that assignment, including all the<br /><br />
obligations arising after the date thereof. In amplification and<br /><br />
clarification of the foregoing, a Non-Defaulting Participant accepting<br /><br />
such an assignment shall not be responsible for any obligation of the<br /><br />
assigning Defaulting Participant to the State, Georgian Oil or any<br /><br />
Third Party which accrued prior to the date of the assignment.<br /><br />
29.5<br /><br />
<br /><br />
The State may terminate the Contract pursuant to Article 29.2.1 or<br /><br />
serve a Default Assignment Notice only if:<br /><br />
29.5.1<br /><br />
<br /><br />
the State gives not less that thirty (30) Days written notice<br /><br />
("Notice") to the Contractor or, as the case may be, the<br /><br />
Defaulting Participant, of an intention to terminate the<br /><br />
Contract or to serve a Default Assignment Notice, stating in<br /><br />
detail in the Notice the alleged material breach or other<br /><br />
grounds for termination or service of a Default Assignment<br /><br />
Notice relied upon by the State;<br /><br />
<br /><br />
29.5.2<br /><br />
<br /><br />
the Contractor or the Defaulting Participant is given a period<br /><br />
of ninety (90) Days from receipt of the Notice to cure or<br /><br />
remove such material breach or other grounds specified in the<br /><br />
Notice for termination or service of a Default Assignment<br /><br />
<br /><br />
Notice; and<br /><br />
29.5.3<br /><br />
29.6<br /><br />
<br /><br />
<PAGE><br /><br />
<br /><br />
the Contractor or the Defaulting Participant has failed within<br /><br />
such ninety (90) Days to cure or remove such material breach.<br /><br />
<br /><br />
It is acknowledged that the Contractor or the Defaulting Participant<br /><br />
may invoke its arbitration rights under Article 30 and thereby dispute<br /><br />
any such termination. If the Contractor or any Defaulting Participant<br /><br />
submits any matter to arbitration, then such submission shall not<br /><br />
suspend the effectiveness of a termination under Articles 29.2.1,<br /><br />
29.2.2 and 29.7. Further if there should be any violation of any law,<br /><br />
rule or regulation, the applicable provisions thereof shall govern with<br /><br />
respect to the<br /><br />
117<br /><br />
consequences of any such violation.<br /><br />
<br /><br />
29.7<br /><br />
<br /><br />
Notwithstanding anything in this Contract to the contrary, if a Parent<br /><br />
Company fails to comply with its obligations under Article 26 and<br /><br />
further fails to reasonably and in good faith commence acting to<br /><br />
correct such failure within thirty (30) Days of notification thereof;<br /><br />
then such failure to comply shall constitute a material breach with the<br /><br />
result that this Contract shall terminate immediately with respect to<br /><br />
the Affiliate of the defaulting Parent Company which is a Contractor<br /><br />
Party.<br /><br />
<br /><br />
29.8<br /><br />
<br /><br />
The Licence shall terminate, ipso facto, upon the termination or<br /><br />
expiration of this Contract. In the event that this Contract terminates<br /><br />
with respect to fewer than all of the Parties, all rights of such<br /><br />
Parties under the Licence shall terminate, ipso facto, concurrently<br /><br />
with such partial termination.<br /><br />

ARTICLE 30<br /><br />
DISPUTE RESOLUTION<br /><br />
<br /><br />
30.1<br /><br />
<br /><br />
Save in the case of disagreements falling within Article 30.5, for the<br /><br />
purpose of this Article, there are two parties that is to say the State<br /><br />
and Georgian Oil who shall so long as Georgian Oil is designated as the<br /><br />
National Oil Company together constitute the First Dispute Party and<br /><br />
the Contractor who shall constitute the Second Dispute Party, and<br /><br />
references in this Article to the Dispute Parties shall be construed<br /><br />
accordingly. In the event that Georgian Oil ceases to be designated as<br /><br />
the National Oil Company, the Parties will reasonably and in good faith<br /><br />
review this Article 30.1.<br /><br />
<br /><br />
30.2<br /><br />
<br /><br />
The Parties hereby consent to submit to the International Centre for<br /><br />
Settlement of Investment Disputes (ICSID) any Dispute in relation to or<br /><br />
arising out of this Contract for settlement by arbitration pursuant to<br /><br />
the Convention on the Settlement of Investment Disputes between States<br /><br />
and Nationals of Other States (the "Convention"). It is acknowledged<br /><br />
that the State has signed and deposited its instrument of ratification<br /><br />
of the Convention on the 7th of August 1992 and the Dispute Parties may<br /><br />
rely on the Convention having entered into force in the Republic of<br /><br />
Georgia without qualification on the 6th September 1992.<br /><br />
<br /><br />
30.3<br /><br />
<br /><br />
The Dispute Parties agree that, for the purposes of Article 25(1) of<br /><br />
the Convention, any Dispute is a legal dispute arising directly out of<br /><br />
an investment.<br /><br />
<br /><br />
30.4<br /><br />
<br /><br />
For the purposes of Article 25(2) of the Convention, it is agreed that<br /><br />
NPL is a national of Bermuda and any wholly owned subsidiaries shall be<br /><br />
treated as nationals of the latter state for the purposes of the<br /><br />
Convention.<br /><br />
<br /><br />
30.5<br /><br />
<br /><br />
In the event that a dispute arises among the private Parties to this<br /><br />
Contract and neither the State nor Georgian Oil is a Dispute Party, the<br /><br />
private Parties, unless otherwise agreed among the private Parties to<br /><br />
the Contract, hereby submit to arbitration in London, United Kingdom in<br /><br />
accordance with the arbitration rules of the London Court of<br /><br />
<br /><br />
International Arbitration. Judgement upon any arbitral award<br /><br />
119<br /><br />
<PAGE><br /><br />
under this Article 30.5 may be entered in any jurisdiction by any court<br /><br />
having jurisdiction of the relevant Party, its property or assets.<br /><br />
30.6<br /><br />
<br /><br />
Arbitration proceedings shall be conducted in the English language.<br /><br />
<br /><br />
30.7<br /><br />
<br /><br />
Any arbitration tribunal constituted pursuant to this Contract shall<br /><br />
apply the provisions of this Contract as governed and construed<br /><br />
according to the law of Georgia and such rules of international law as<br /><br />
may be applicable.<br /><br />
<br /><br />
30.8<br /><br />
<br /><br />
Contractor, the State and Georgian Oil (with reference to any matter<br /><br />
pertaining to Georgian Oil's role as a State Representative) hereby<br /><br />
consent to submit to ICSID any disagreement arising out of the<br /><br />
Contract, including, without limitation, whether the State and Georgian<br /><br />
Oil have served a valid Default Assignment Notice. The provisions of<br /><br />
Articles 30.2, 30.3, 30.4, 30.7 and 30.8 shall apply to the arbitration<br /><br />
of such disagreement. In the event that Contractor is organised in a<br /><br />
state which is not a party to the Convention, any disagreement shall be<br /><br />
submitted for settlement by arbitration under the Additional Facility<br /><br />
Rules of ICSID.<br /><br />
<br /><br />
30.9<br /><br />
<br /><br />
Either the First Dispute Party or the Second Dispute Party may commence<br /><br />
a Sole Expert determination with respect to any matter in dispute<br /><br />
between such Dispute Parties which may be or is required to be referred<br /><br />
to a Sole Expert under the provisions of the Contract (or with respect<br /><br />
to any other matter which the First Dispute Party and the Second<br /><br />
Dispute Party may otherwise agree to so refer) by giving written notice<br /><br />
to such effect. Such notice shall contain a statement describing the<br /><br />
issue and all relevant information associated therewith. A Sole Expert<br /><br />
shall be an independent and impartial person of international standing<br /><br />
with relevant qualifications and experience appointed pursuant to the<br /><br />
mutual agreement of the First Dispute Party and the Second Dispute<br /><br />
Party. The Sole Expert shall act as an expert and not as an arbitrator<br /><br />
or mediator and, unless otherwise agreed, shall be instructed to<br /><br />
resolve the dispute referred to him within thirty (30) Days of his<br /><br />
appointment. Upon the selection of the Sole Expert, the Dispute Party<br /><br />
receiving the notice of referral above shall submit its own statement<br /><br />
containing all information it considers relevant with respect to the<br /><br />
matter in dispute. The decision of the Sole<br /><br />
120<br /><br />
<br /><br />
<PAGE><br /><br />
Expert shall be final and binding and not subject to any appeal. If the<br /><br />
First Dispute Party and the Second Dispute Party are unable to agree on<br /><br />
the appointment of a Sole Expert within twenty (20) Days after a<br /><br />
Dispute Party has received a notice of referral under this Clause 30.10<br /><br />
the Sole Expert shall be selected by the Secretary General of ICSID and<br /><br />
the person so selected shall be deemed to have been appointed by the<br /><br />
Dispute Parties.<br /><br />
30.10<br /><br />
<br /><br />
The fees and expenses of the Sole Expert appointed under the provisions<br /><br />
of Article 30.9 or other provision of this Contract shall be borne by<br /><br />
the losing Dispute Party and shall not be considered Costs and<br /><br />
Expenses.<br /><br />
<br /><br />
30.11<br /><br />
<br /><br />
It is further agreed by the Parties, that no registered presence that<br /><br />
the Contractor may establish or may be required to establish in<br /><br />
Georgia, including but not limited to the formation of an Operating<br /><br />
Company, registration of an NPL representative office, registration<br /><br />
with the tax authorities or creation of a permanent establishment for<br /><br />
tax purposes, shall constitute a Georgian legal entity for the purposes<br /><br />
of Article 30.2 of the Petroleum Law. To amplify the foregoing, the<br /><br />
State and Georgian Oil hereby irrevocably and unconditionally confirm<br /><br />
that the arbitration agreement set forth in Article 5 of the Original<br /><br />
Contract, as amended hereunder is valid, effective and binding on the<br /><br />
State and Georgian Oil.<br /><br />

authorised body, and each of which shall have equal legal force and<br /><br />

arbitration the English version shall (after the Georgian version has<br /><br />
been reviewed and its provisions have been discussed in good faith)<br /><br />
control for interpretative purposes and shall be used as the authentic<br /><br />
version to determine the rights and obligations of the Parties which<br /><br />
shall be determined by reference solely to the English version of this<br /><br />
Contract. [No change]<br /><br />

<br /><br />
Contract shall be amended only by written document signed by all the<br /><br />
Parties.<br /><br />
<br /><br />
31.3<br /><br />
<br /><br />
If and for so long as any provision of this Contract shall be deemed or<br /><br />
judged to be invalid for any reason whatsoever, such invalidity shall<br /><br />
not affect the validity or operation of any other provision of this<br /><br />
Contract except only as far as shall be necessary to give effect to the<br /><br />
construction of such invalidity, and any such invalid provision shall<br /><br />
be deemed severed from this Contract without affecting the validity of<br /><br />
the rest of the Contract.<br /><br />

ANNEX C<br /><br />
ACCOUNTING PROCEDURE<br /><br />
SECTION I<br /><br />
GENERAL PROVISIONS<br /><br />
1.1.<br /><br />
<br /><br />
PURPOSE<br /><br />
The accounting procedures included in this Accounting Procedure<br /><br />
establish a framework of accounting principles as generally accepted<br /><br />
within the international Petroleum industry. The purpose of this<br /><br />
Accounting Procedure is to establish a fair and equitable method for<br /><br />
accounting for Petroleum Operations under the Contract, to classify<br /><br />
expenditures, define Costs and Expenses and prescribe the manner in<br /><br />
which the Contractor's accounts shall be prepared and approved.<br /><br />
<br /><br />
1.2.<br /><br />
<br /><br />
DEFINITIONS<br /><br />
For the purpose of this Accounting Procedure the following terms shall<br /><br />
have the following meanings:<br /><br />
"Accepted Accounting Procedure" shall mean accounting principles,<br /><br />
practices and procedures generally accepted and recognised in the<br /><br />
international Petroleum industry.<br /><br />
"Accounting Procedure" shall mean the accounting principles, practices<br /><br />
and procedures set forth in this Annex C.<br /><br />
"Accruals Accounting Basis" shall mean the basis of accounting which<br /><br />
records the effect of transactions and events on financial conditions<br /><br />
and income when an obligation is created or a right arises.<br /><br />
"Contract" shall mean the production sharing contract this Accounting<br /><br />
Procedure is annexed to.<br /><br />
"Controllable Material" means all materials and equipment controlled<br /><br />
and inventoried by the Contractor. A list of types of such Controllable<br /><br />
Material shall be<br /><br />
128<br /><br />
<br /><br />
<PAGE><br /><br />
furnished to Georgian Oil upon request.<br /><br />
"Material and Equipment" means property, including without limitation<br /><br />
all exploration, appraisal and development facilities together with<br /><br />
supplies and equipment, acquired and held for use in Petroleum<br /><br />
Operations.<br /><br />
The words and phrases defined in the Contract but not defined above<br /><br />
shall have the same meaning in this Accounting Procedure as is given to<br /><br />
them in the Contract.<br /><br />
1.3.<br /><br />
<br /><br />
AUDITS<br /><br />
1.3.1<br /><br />
<br /><br />
The State or Georgian Oil shall have the right to audit the<br /><br />
Contractor's accounts and records maintained under the<br /><br />
Contract with respect to each Calendar Year within two Years<br /><br />
from the end of each such Year as follows. Should Georgian Oil<br /><br />
decide not to perform its own audit, the audit may be<br /><br />
conducted by the State Agency. However, the audit may be<br /><br />
conducted instead by an independent auditor of international<br /><br />
standing familiar with international petroleum industry<br /><br />
practice in accordance with international auditing standards<br /><br />
at the request of Georgian Oil or the State Agency, but not<br /><br />
both. If audit is performed by an independent auditor, the<br /><br />
cost of such auditor should be borne by the Contractor and<br /><br />
treated as Costs and Expenses. For the avoidance of doubt, it<br /><br />
is understood that Contractor shall be subject to no more than<br /><br />
one audit in total in a single Calendar Year.<br /><br />
<br /><br />
1.3.2<br /><br />
<br /><br />
Any audit exceptions shall be made in writing and notified to<br /><br />
the Contractor within ninety (90) Days, following completion<br /><br />
of the audit in question, and failure to give such written<br /><br />
exception within such time shall be deemed to be an<br /><br />
acknowledgement of the correctness of the Contractor's books<br /><br />
and accounts.<br /><br />
129<br /><br />
<br /><br />
<PAGE><br /><br />
1.3.3<br /><br />
<br /><br />
For purposes of auditing, the State or Georgian Oil may<br /><br />
examine and verify, upon providing at least sixty (60) days<br /><br />
advance notice to Contractor and at its sole expense, all<br /><br />
charges and credits relating to the Petroleum Operations, such<br /><br />
as books of account, accounting entries, material records and<br /><br />
inventories, vouchers, payrolls, invoices and any other<br /><br />
documents, correspondence and records including electronic<br /><br />
<br /><br />
records considered necessary by the State or Georgian Oil to<br /><br />
audit and verify the charges and credits. Furthermore, the<br /><br />
auditors shall have the right in connection with such audit,<br /><br />
to visit and inspect at reasonable times, all sites, plants,<br /><br />
facilities, warehouses and offices of the Contractor directly<br /><br />
or indirectly serving the Petroleum Operations and to question<br /><br />
personnel associated with those Operations. Where the State or<br /><br />
Georgian Oil requires verification of charges made by an<br /><br />
Affiliated Company of the Contractor, the State or Georgian<br /><br />
Oil shall have the right to obtain an audit certificate from<br /><br />
an internationally recognised firm of public accountants<br /><br />
acceptable to both the State or Georgian Oil and the<br /><br />
Contractor, which may be the Contractor's statutory auditor.<br /><br />
The auditors shall make every reasonable effort to conduct<br /><br />
their examination in a manner which will result in a minimum<br /><br />
of inconvenience to the Contractor<br /><br />
1.3.4<br /><br />
<br /><br />
The Contractor shall answer any notice of exception under<br /><br />
paragraph 1.3.2 within one hundred eighty (180) Days of the<br /><br />
receipt of such notice. Where the Contractor has, after the<br /><br />
said one hundred eighty (180) Days, failed to answer a notice<br /><br />
of exception the exception shall prevail.<br /><br />
<br /><br />
1.3.5<br /><br />
<br /><br />
All agreed adjustments resulting from an audit and all<br /><br />
adjustments required by prevailing exceptions shall be<br /><br />
promptly made in the Contractor's accounts and any<br /><br />
consequential adjustments to payments due to the State or<br /><br />
Georgian Oil shall be made promptly.<br /><br />
130<br /><br />
<br /><br />
<PAGE><br /><br />
1.3.6<br /><br />
<br /><br />
1.4.<br /><br />
<br /><br />
If the Contractor and the State or Georgian Oil are unable to<br /><br />
reach final agreement on proposed audit adjustments they shall<br /><br />
refer their dispute for binding and final resolution by an<br /><br />
internationally recognised firm of independent public<br /><br />
accountants appointed in accordance with the procedures for<br /><br />
appointing a Sole Expert pursuant to Article 30 of the<br /><br />
Contract. When issues are outstanding with respect to an<br /><br />
audit, the Contractor shall maintain the relevant documents<br /><br />
and permit inspection thereof until the issue is resolved.<br /><br />
<br /><br />
THE CONTRACTOR'S BOOKS<br /><br />
1.4.1<br /><br />
<br /><br />
The Contractor shall maintain at the Contractor's office in<br /><br />
Georgia in English in local currency and US$ and on an Accrual<br /><br />
Accounting Basis books and accounts for Petroleum Operations.<br /><br />
Such books and accounts shall be kept in accordance with<br /><br />
Accepted Accounting Procedure and the provisions of the<br /><br />
Contract and this Accounting Procedure ("Petroleum Operations<br /><br />
Account").<br /><br />
<br /><br />
1.4.2<br /><br />
<br /><br />
All US$ expenditures shall be charged in the amount expended.<br /><br />
Expenditures incurred in currencies other than US$ shall be<br /><br />
translated into US$ in accordance with Article 19.11 of the<br /><br />
Contract. A record shall be kept of the exchange rates used in<br /><br />
translating expenditures incurred in currencies other than<br /><br />
US$. Any gain or loss resulting from the exchange of<br /><br />
currencies required for Petroleum Operations and any fees or<br /><br />
other banking charges levied in connection with such exchange<br /><br />
of currencies or any gain or loss resulting from translation<br /><br />
of expenditures and sales revenues in accordance with the<br /><br />
provisions of Article 19.11 shall be included in Costs and<br /><br />
Expenses and recoverable from Cost Recovery Petroleum and<br /><br />
credited or charged to the Petroleum Operations Account.<br /><br />
<br /><br />
1.4.3<br /><br />
<br /><br />
The Contractor shall maintain books and accounts relating to<br /><br />
Petroleum<br /><br />
131<br /><br />
<br /><br />
<PAGE><br /><br />
Operations for six (6) Years following the end of the Calendar<br /><br />
<br /><br />
Year to which they relate.<br /><br />
1.5.<br /><br />
<br /><br />
PRECEDENCE OF DOCUMENTS<br /><br />
In the event of any inconsistency or conflict between the provisions of<br /><br />
this Accounting Procedure and the provisions of the Contract treating<br /><br />
the same subject differently, the provisions of the Accounting<br /><br />
Procedure shall prevail.<br /><br />
<br /><br />
1.6.<br /><br />
<br /><br />
REVISION OF ACCOUNTING PROCEDURE<br /><br />
This Accounting Procedure may be revised from time to time by mutual<br /><br />
written agreement among the Parties.<br /><br />
<br /><br />
1.7.<br /><br />
<br /><br />
ARBITRATION PROCEDURES<br /><br />
Any dispute in relation to or arising out of this Accounting Procedure<br /><br />
shall, unless otherwise provided in this Accounting Procedure, be<br /><br />
submitted first to a Sole Expert who shall have the rights set forth in<br /><br />
the Contract, the cost of which shall be reimbursable as Cost Recovery<br /><br />
Petroleum. If such matter is not so settled, the dispute shall be<br /><br />
submitted to arbitration in accordance with Article 30 of the Contract.<br /><br />
132<br /><br />
<br /><br />
<PAGE><br /><br />
SECTION II<br /><br />
CLASSIFICATION, DEFINITION AND ALLOCATION OF COSTS<br /><br />
2.1<br /><br />
<br /><br />
SEGREGATION OF COSTS<br /><br />
Costs shall be segregated in accordance with the purposes for which<br /><br />
such costs are incurred. The purposes which shall qualify are those<br /><br />
which have been included in the approved Work Programme and Budget for<br /><br />
the year in which the costs are incurred and other items which have<br /><br />
been agreed by the Parties from time to time. All costs allowable under<br /><br />
Section III relating to Petroleum Operations shall be classified,<br /><br />
defined and allocated as set out below.<br /><br />
<br /><br />
2.2.<br /><br />
<br /><br />
EXPLORATION COSTS<br /><br />
"Exploration Costs" are all direct and allocated indirect costs<br /><br />
incurred in the search for Petroleum in an area which is, or was at the<br /><br />
time when such costs were incurred, part of the Contract Area<br /><br />
including:<br /><br />
2.2.1<br /><br />
<br /><br />
Aerial, geophysical, geochemical, paleontological, geological,<br /><br />
topographical and seismic surveys and studies and their<br /><br />
interpretation and purchased geological and geophysical<br /><br />
information all separately identified.<br /><br />
<br /><br />
2.2.2<br /><br />
<br /><br />
Stratigraphic test hole drilling and water well drilling.<br /><br />
<br /><br />
2.2.3<br /><br />
<br /><br />
Labour, materials, supplies, and services used in drilling<br /><br />
wells with the object of finding Petroleum or appraisal wells<br /><br />
excluding any costs of the subsequent completion of such wells<br /><br />
as producing wells.<br /><br />
133<br /><br />
<br /><br />
<PAGE><br /><br />
2.2.4<br /><br />
<br /><br />
Facilities used solely in support of the purposes described in<br /><br />
Paragraphs 2.2.1, 2.2.2 and 2.2.3 above, including access<br /><br />
roads, all separately identified.<br /><br />
<br /><br />
2.2.5<br /><br />
<br /><br />
That portion of all Service Costs (as defined in Paragraph<br /><br />
2.5) and that portion of all General and Administrative Costs<br /><br />
(as defined in Paragraph 2.6) allocated to Exploration Costs<br /><br />
as determined by the proportionate share of total Costs and<br /><br />
Expenses (excluding General and Administrative Costs and<br /><br />
Service Costs) represented by all other Exploration Costs.<br /><br />
<br /><br />
2.2.6<br /><br />
<br /><br />
2.3<br /><br />
<br /><br />
Any other costs incurred in the search for and appraisal of<br /><br />
Petroleum after the Effective Date but prior to the<br /><br />
Commencement of Commercial Production and not covered under<br /><br />
Paragraph 2.3.<br /><br />
<br /><br />
DEVELOPMENT AND PRODUCTION COSTS<br /><br />
"Development and Production Costs" shall consist of all costs, whether<br /><br />
incurred by acquisition of assets, leasing or other financial<br /><br />
arrangement incurred in:<br /><br />
2.3.1<br /><br />
<br /><br />
Drilling wells, other than wells classified as Exploration<br /><br />
Costs, whether these wells are dry or producing and drilling<br /><br />
wells for the injection of water or gas to enhance recovery of<br /><br />
Petroleum.<br /><br />
<br /><br />
2.3.2<br /><br />
<br /><br />
Completing wells by way of installation of casing or equipment<br /><br />
or otherwise after a well has been drilled for the purpose of<br /><br />
bringing the well into use as a producing well or as a well<br /><br />
for the injection of water or gas to enhance recovery of<br /><br />
Petroleum.<br /><br />
<br /><br />
2.3.3<br /><br />
<br /><br />
Acquisition, construction or provision of Petroleum<br /><br />
production, transport and storage facilities such as<br /><br />
pipelines, flow lines, production and treatment units,<br /><br />
wellhead equipment, subsurface equipment, enhanced recovery<br /><br />
systems, Petroleum storage facilities, and access roads for<br /><br />
134<br /><br />
<br /><br />
<PAGE><br /><br />
production activities.<br /><br />
<br /><br />
2.3<br /><br />
<br /><br />
2.3.4<br /><br />
<br /><br />
Engineering and design studies for the wells and facilities<br /><br />
referred to in Paragraphs 2.3.1, 2.3.2 and 2.3.3.<br /><br />
<br /><br />
2.3.5<br /><br />
<br /><br />
That portion of all Service Costs and that portion of all<br /><br />
General and Administrative Costs allocated to Development and<br /><br />
Production Costs as determined by the proportionate share of<br /><br />
total Petroleum Operations Costs (excluding General and<br /><br />
Administrative Costs and Service Costs) represented by all<br /><br />
other Development and Production Costs.<br /><br />
<br /><br />
OPERATING COSTS<br /><br />
Operating Costs are all costs incurred in Petroleum Operations after<br /><br />
the Commencement of Commercial Production which are other than<br /><br />
Exploration Costs and Development and Production Costs, including those<br /><br />
portions of General and Administrative Costs and Service Costs which<br /><br />
are not allocated to Exploration Costs or Development and Production<br /><br />
Costs.<br /><br />
<br /><br />
2.5<br /><br />
<br /><br />
SERVICE COSTS<br /><br />
Service Costs are costs in support of Petroleum Operations including<br /><br />
warehouses, vehicles, motorised rolling equipment, aircraft, fire and<br /><br />
security stations, workshops, water and sewerage plants, power plants,<br /><br />
housing, community and recreational facilities and furniture, tools and<br /><br />
equipment used in these activities. Service Costs in any Calendar Year<br /><br />
shall include the costs incurred in such year to purchase and/or<br /><br />
construct the said facilities as well as the annual costs of<br /><br />
maintaining and operating the same. All Service Costs shall be<br /><br />
regularly allocated as specified in Paragraphs 2.2.5, 2.3.5 and 2.4 to<br /><br />
Exploration Costs, Development and Production Costs and Operating Costs<br /><br />
and shall be separately shown under each of these categories. Where<br /><br />
Service Costs are incurred in respect of shared facilities the basis of<br /><br />
allocation of costs to Petroleum Operations hereunder shall be<br /><br />
specified.<br /><br />

2.6.1<br /><br />

<br /><br />
(ii)<br /><br />
<br /><br />
are properly allocable to Petroleum Operations under<br /><br />
the Contract.<br /><br />

SECTION III<br /><br />
COSTS, EXPENSES, AND EXPENDITURES AND CREDITS<br /><br />
Except to the extent provided in Paragraph 3.17 of this Section the Contractor<br /><br />
shall charge the Petroleum Operations Account for all Costs and Expenses<br /><br />
incurred and necessary to conduct Petroleum Operations under this Contract as<br /><br />
classified under the headings set forth in Section II of this Accounting<br /><br />
Procedure. For the purposes of this Accounting Procedure Costs and Expenses<br /><br />
referred to in Article 11.2 shall be deemed to be incurred on the Effective Date<br /><br />
of this Contract. Costs and Expenses shall include, but not be limited to:<br /><br />
3.1<br /><br />
<br /><br />
LICENSES, PERMITS<br /><br />
All costs, if any, attributable to the acquisition, maintenance,<br /><br />
renewal or relinquishment of licenses (excluding the Licence as defined<br /><br />
in Article 1.49), permits, contractual and/or surface rights acquired<br /><br />
for Petroleum Operations.<br /><br />
<br /><br />
3.2<br /><br />
<br /><br />
SALARIES, WAGES AND RELATED COSTS<br /><br />
3.2.1<br /><br />
<br /><br />
The employees of Contractor and its Affiliates in Georgia<br /><br />
directly engaged in Petroleum Operations whether temporarily<br /><br />
or permanently assigned. Time of such employees shall be<br /><br />
documented by timesheets.<br /><br />
<br /><br />
3.2.2<br /><br />
<br /><br />
The employees of Contractor and its Affiliates outside Georgia<br /><br />
directly engaged in Petroleum Operations whether temporarily<br /><br />
or permanently assigned, and not otherwise covered in Section<br /><br />
3.7.2. Time of such employees shall be documented by<br /><br />
timesheets.<br /><br />
138<br /><br />
<br /><br />
<PAGE><br /><br />
3.2.3<br /><br />
<br /><br />
Salaries and wages, including everything constituting the<br /><br />
employees' total compensation. To the extent not included in<br /><br />
salaries and wages, the Petroleum Operations Account shall<br /><br />
also be charged with the cost to Contractor of holiday,<br /><br />
vacation, sickness, disability benefits, living and housing<br /><br />
allowances, travel time, bonuses, tax equalisation payments<br /><br />
and other customary allowances applicable to the salaries and<br /><br />
wages chargeable hereunder, as well as costs to Contractor for<br /><br />
employee benefits, including but not limited to employee group<br /><br />
life insurance, group medical insurance, hospitalisation,<br /><br />
retirement, severance payments required by laws or regulations<br /><br />
of the State of Georgia, and other benefit plans of a like<br /><br />
nature applicable to labour costs of Contractor. Contractor's<br /><br />
employees participating in Georgian benefit plans may be<br /><br />
charged at a percentage rate to reflect payments or accruals<br /><br />
made by Contractor applicable to such employees.<br /><br />
<br /><br />
3.2.4<br /><br />
<br /><br />
Expenditures or contributions made pursuant to assessments<br /><br />
imposed by governmental authority for payments with respect<br /><br />
thereto or on account of such employees.<br /><br />
<br /><br />
3.2.5<br /><br />
<br /><br />
Salaries and wages charged in accordance with Contractor's<br /><br />
usual practice, when and as paid or accrued, or on a basis of<br /><br />
the Contractor's average cost per employee for each job<br /><br />
category; and the rates to be charged shall be reviewed at<br /><br />
least annually. In determining the average cost per employee<br /><br />
for each job category, expatriate and national employee<br /><br />
salaries and wages shall be calculated separately. During a<br /><br />
given period of time it is understood that some costs for<br /><br />
<br /><br />
salaries and wages may be charged on an actual basis while the<br /><br />
remaining costs for salaries and wages are charged at a rate<br /><br />
based upon the above described average cost<br /><br />

<br /><br />

<br /><br />

to or from the Contract Area vicinity or location where the<br /><br />

employees and their family, personal and household effects of<br /><br />
the employee and their family, transit expenses, and all other<br /><br />
related reasonable costs in accordance with the Contractor's<br /><br />
and its Affiliates' usual practice.<br /><br />

3.3.3<br /><br />
<br /><br />

another location classified as a foreign location by the<br /><br />

<br /><br />
<PAGE><br /><br />
3.4<br /><br />
<br /><br />
OFFICES, CAMPS AND MISCELLANEOUS FACILITIES<br /><br />
All costs of maintaining any offices, sub-offices, camps, warehouses,<br /><br />

directly serving the Petroleum Operations either within Georgia or<br /><br />
elsewhere. If such facilities serve operations in addition to the<br /><br />
Petroleum Operations the costs shall be allocated to the properties<br /><br />
served on an equitable basis approved by the Parties.<br /><br />
<br /><br />
3.5<br /><br />
<br /><br />
MATERIAL AND EQUIPMENT<br /><br />
Costs of materials and supplies, equipment, machines, tools and any<br /><br />
other goods of a similar nature used or consumed in Petroleum<br /><br />
Operations subject to the following:<br /><br />
3.5.1<br /><br />
<br /><br />
Acquisition - the Contractor shall only supply or purchase<br /><br />
materials for use in Petroleum Operations that may be used in<br /><br />
the foreseeable future. The accumulation of surplus stocks and<br /><br />
inventory shall be avoided so far as is reasonably practical<br /><br />
and consistent with efficient and economical operations.<br /><br />
Inventory levels shall, however, take into account the time<br /><br />
lag for replacement, emergency needs, weather conditions<br /><br />
<br /><br />
affecting operations and similar considerations.<br /><br />
3.5.2<br /><br />
<br /><br />
Components of costs, arm's length transactions - except as<br /><br />
otherwise provided in paragraph 3.5.3 below, material<br /><br />
purchased by the Contractor in arm's length transactions in<br /><br />
the open market for use in the Petroleum Operations under the<br /><br />
Contract shall be valued to include invoice price less trade<br /><br />
and cash discounts (if any), purchase and procurement fees<br /><br />
plus freight and forwarding charges between point of supply<br /><br />
and point of shipment, freight to port of destination,<br /><br />
insurance, taxes, customs duties, consular fees, excise taxes,<br /><br />
other items chargeable against imported materials and, where<br /><br />
applicable, handling and transportation expenses from point of<br /><br />
importation to warehouse or operating site.<br /><br />
141<br /><br />
<br /><br />
<PAGE><br /><br />
3.5.3<br /><br />
<br /><br />
Accounting - such material costs shall be charged to the<br /><br />
accounting records and books in accordance with the "First in,<br /><br />
First out" (FIFO) method;<br /><br />
<br /><br />
3.5.4<br /><br />
<br /><br />
Material purchased from or sold to Affiliates of the<br /><br />
Contractor or transferred from other activities of the<br /><br />
Contractor to or from Petroleum Operations under the Contract<br /><br />
shall be valued and charged or credited at the prices<br /><br />
specified as follows:<br /><br />
3.5.4.1 New material, including new material moved from<br /><br />
inventory (Condition "A"), shall be valued at the<br /><br />
current international net price which shall not<br /><br />
exceed the price prevailing in normal arm's length<br /><br />
transactions in the open market.<br /><br />
3.5.4.2 Used material (Conditions "B", "C" and "D");<br /><br />
(i)<br /><br />
<br /><br />
Material which is in sound and serviceable<br /><br />
condition and is suitable for re-use without<br /><br />
reconditioning shall be classified as Condition<br /><br />
"B" and priced at seventy-five percent (75%) of<br /><br />
the current price of new material defined in<br /><br />
Paragraph 3.5.4.1;<br /><br />
<br /><br />
(ii)<br /><br />
<br /><br />
Material which cannot be classified as Condition<br /><br />
"B" but which after reconditioning will be further<br /><br />
serviceable for its original function shall be<br /><br />
classified as Condition "C" and priced at not more<br /><br />
than fifty percent (50%) of the current price of<br /><br />
new material as defined in 3.5.4.1 above. The cost<br /><br />
of reconditioning shall be charged to the<br /><br />
reconditioned material provided that the value of<br /><br />
Condition "C" material plus the cost of<br /><br />
reconditioning do not exceed the value of<br /><br />
Condition "B" material;<br /><br />
<br /><br />
(iii)<br /><br />
<br /><br />
Material which cannot be classified as Condition<br /><br />
"B" or Condition "C" shall be classified as<br /><br />
Condition "D" and priced at a value commensurate<br /><br />
with its use by the<br /><br />
142<br /><br />
<br /><br />
<PAGE><br /><br />
Contractor. If material is not fit for use by the<br /><br />
Contractor it shall be disposed of as junk.<br /><br />
3.5.4.3 Material involving erection costs shall be charged at<br /><br />
the applicable condition percentage of the current<br /><br />
knocked-down price of new material as defined in<br /><br />
Paragraph 3.5.4.1 above.<br /><br />
3.5.4.4 When the use of material is temporary and its service<br /><br />
to the Petroleum Operations under the Contract does<br /><br />
<br /><br />
not justify the reduction in price as provided for in<br /><br />
paragraph 3.5.4.2(b) hereof, such material shall be<br /><br />
priced on a basis that will result in a net charge to<br /><br />
the accounts under the Contract consistent with the<br /><br />
value of the service rendered.<br /><br />
3.5.4.5 Premium prices - whenever material is not readily<br /><br />
obtainable at published or listed prices because of<br /><br />
national emergencies, strikes or other unusual causes<br /><br />
over which the Contractor has no control, the<br /><br />
Contractor may charge Petroleum Operations for the<br /><br />
required material at the Contractor's actual cost<br /><br />
incurred in providing such material, in making it<br /><br />
suitable for use, and in moving it to the Contract<br /><br />
Area; provided notice in writing is furnished to the<br /><br />
State of the proposed charge prior to charging<br /><br />
Petroleum Operations for such material and the State<br /><br />
shall have the right to challenge the transaction on<br /><br />
audit.<br /><br />

AFFILIATES<br /><br />
Charges for exclusively owned equipment, facilities and utilities of<br /><br />

Project engineering<br /><br />
Source rock analysis<br /><br />
Petrophysical analysis<br /><br />
Geochemical analysis<br /><br />
Drilling supervision<br /><br />
Development evaluation<br /><br />
Accounting and professional services<br /><br />
Other data processing<br /><br />

professional personnel, lost time, governmental assessments, employee<br /><br />

also include all support costs necessary for such technical and<br /><br />
<br /><br />
144<br /><br />
<PAGE><br /><br />
professional personnel to perform such services, such as, but not<br /><br />
limited to, rent, utilities, administration, support staff, drafting,<br /><br />
telephone and other communications expenses, computer support,<br /><br />

the following:<br /><br />
3.18.1<br /><br />
<br /><br />
Any successful insurance claim in connection with Petroleum<br /><br />
Operations where the claim is with respect to operations or<br /><br />
assets which were insured and where the insurance premiums<br /><br />
with respect thereto have been charged to the Petroleum<br /><br />
Operations Account.<br /><br />
<br /><br />
3.18.2<br /><br />
<br /><br />
Any successful claim in connection with Petroleum Operations<br /><br />
where the costs and expenditures relating to the subject of<br /><br />
the claim have been charged to the Petroleum Operations<br /><br />
Account.<br /><br />
<br /><br />
3.18.3<br /><br />
<br /><br />
The sale, exchange or salvage of Material and Equipment<br /><br />
previously charged to Petroleum Operations Account will be<br /><br />
credited to the<br /><br />
148<br /><br />
<br /><br />
<PAGE><br /><br />
Petroleum Operations Account less any expenses associated with<br /><br />
the disposition of the Material and Equipment. Material and<br /><br />
Equipment transferred to the Contractor or an Affiliate will<br /><br />
be credited to the Petroleum Operations Account at fair market<br /><br />
value.<br /><br />
3.18.4<br /><br />
<br /><br />
Legal costs charged to the Petroleum Operations Account and<br /><br />
subsequently recovered by the Contractor.<br /><br />
<br /><br />
3.18.5<br /><br />
<br /><br />
Revenue received from Third Parties for the use of property or<br /><br />
assets the cost of which has been charged to the Petroleum<br /><br />

3.18.6<br /><br />
<br /><br />
Any adjustment received by the Contractor from the suppliers<br /><br />
or manufacturers or their agents in connection with a<br /><br />

the Contractor to the accounts under the Contract.<br /><br />
<br /><br />
3.18.7<br /><br />
<br /><br />
Rentals, refunds, including refunds of taxes paid, or other<br /><br />
credits received by the Contractor which apply to any charge<br /><br />
which has been made to the accounts under the Contract, but<br /><br />

Notwithstanding any provision to the contrary in this Accounting<br /><br />

ARTICLE 2<br /><br />
PURPOSE AND SUBJECT OF ACTIVITIES OF THE COMPANY<br /><br />
2.1<br /><br />
<br /><br />
During Petroleum Operations, the Company shall act as a non-commercial<br /><br />
agent. The purpose of the Company is to hold in its name, the license<br /><br />
for the Samgori - Patardzeuli block and to carry out activities in the<br /><br />
areas of oil and gas exploration, development and production on behalf<br /><br />
of the Contractor in connection to the latter's Production Sharing<br /><br />
Contract signed on _________ with NPL, Joint Stock National Oil Company<br /><br />
Saknavtobi and the State Agency for the Regulation of Oil and Gas<br /><br />
Resources. It has no title to ownership of the produced oil or gas and<br /><br />
hence no right to sell any of the oil or gas so produced.<br /><br />
<br /><br />
2.2<br /><br />
<br /><br />
The subject activities of the Company are any business activity not<br /><br />
prohibited by law, subject to proper licenses and approvals from the<br /><br />
government, including but not limited to:<br /><br />
2.2.1<br /><br />
<br /><br />
Exploration, development, production and transportation of oil<br /><br />
and gas, including the construction of field and processing<br /><br />
facilities, in Georgia;<br /><br />
<br /><br />
2.2.2<br /><br />
<br /><br />
purchase, execute lease or exchange, hire or otherwise acquire<br /><br />
and hold any estate or interest in any lands, buildings,<br /><br />
easements, rights, privileges, concessions, designs,<br /><br />
copyrights, patents, patent rights, licenses, processes,<br /><br />
machinery, plant, and any real or personal property of any<br /><br />
kind necessary or convenient for the purposes of or in<br /><br />
connection with the Company's business;<br /><br />
<br /><br />
2.2.3<br /><br />
<br /><br />
guarantee obligations and contracts;<br /><br />
<br /><br />
2.2.4<br /><br />
<br /><br />
engage in training, servicing and all other activities related<br /><br />
to the business of the Company; and<br /><br />
161<br /><br />

2.2.5<br /><br />
<br /><br />
2.3<br /><br />

do all or any of the above things, either as principals,<br /><br />
agents, trustees, contractors or otherwise, and either alone<br /><br />
or in conjunction with others, and either by or through<br /><br />
agents, trustees, sub-contractors or otherwise.<br /><br />

ARTICLE 4<br /><br />
CHARTER CAPITAL OF THE COMPANY<br /><br />
4.1<br /><br />
<br /><br />
The Charter Capital of the Company registered in 1995 was $10 million.<br /><br />
<br /><br />
4.2<br /><br />
<br /><br />
Each of the Partners had the following interest in and contribution to<br /><br />
the Charter Capital:<br /><br />
NPL:<br /><br />
<br /><br />
$5 million, i.e. 50% of the Charter Capital<br /><br />
<br /><br />
GEORGIAN OIL: $5 million, i.e. 50% of the Charter Capital<br /><br />
4.3<br /><br />
<br /><br />
Partners' interests in the charter capital are reflected in the Charter<br /><br />
and in the Enterprise Register kept at the registering district court.<br /><br />
<br /><br />
4.4<br /><br />
<br /><br />
If a Partner exceeds the time limit set for the making of his<br /><br />
contribution, another Partner may demand in writing that he makes his<br /><br />
contribution, specifying a new time limit and warning that he may be<br /><br />
expelled from the Company. Any additional time period shall be no less<br /><br />
than one month.<br /><br />
In case of failure to meet the above deadline, the Partner whose<br /><br />
contribution is overdue shall lose his share and shall not be entitled<br /><br />
to any profits or benefits earned as a result of his partially<br /><br />
performed obligation. He shall be informed of the above in writing.<br /><br />
<br /><br />
4.5<br /><br />
<br /><br />
The contribution to the Charter Capital is considered to be the<br /><br />
Company's property. The return of the contribution shall be allowed<br /><br />
only by way of decreasing the Charter Capital, which shall be duly<br /><br />
reflected in the Charter. The decrease of the Charter Capital shall be<br /><br />
registered in the Entrepreneurs' Register at the court.<br /><br />
<br /><br />
4.6<br /><br />
<br /><br />
In case the amount of the Charter Capital becomes less than the minimum<br /><br />
amount established by the law (currently two thousand (2,000) Lari), it<br /><br />
shall be urgently replenished up to the established minimum amount.<br /><br />
<br /><br />
4.7<br /><br />
<br /><br />
None of the Partners shall have any special rights to use any assets<br /><br />
which are regarded as property of the Company.<br /><br />
164<br /><br />

<br /><br />
5.2<br /><br />

below, every Partner of the Company or his duly authorised<br /><br />

<br /><br />

partners whose shares in the Company jointly or severally<br /><br />

<br /><br />
5.2.7<br /><br />
<br /><br />
receive dividends in proportion to share ownership, except as<br /><br />
otherwise agreed; and<br /><br />
<br /><br />
5.2.8<br /><br />
<br /><br />
in case of the Company's liquidation, receive the assets of<br /><br />
the Company in proportion to share ownership after covering<br /><br />
the Company's debts.<br /><br />
<br /><br />
Any action in respect to a Partner's share or part thereof, such as<br /><br />
assignment. mortgaging, transfer of title, or any other similar action<br /><br />

In case of assignment or alienation by a Partner of his share, the<br /><br />
