ARTICLE 6<br /><br />
MEETINGS OF THE PARTNERS<br /><br />
6.1<br /><br />
<br /><br />
The highest governing body of the Company shall be the Meeting of the<br /><br />
Partners. The Meeting of the Partners shall determine the general<br /><br />
business policy of the Company, as well as the Company's principal<br /><br />
guidelines, activities and structure. Partners are expected to<br /><br />
personally attend meetings. If a Partner is unable to attend the<br /><br />
Meeting in person, he may vote on any matter on the agenda for such<br /><br />
meeting by appointing a proxy by written notice to the Chairman of the<br /><br />
Meeting prior to the Meeting or by giving notice of his actual vote on<br /><br />
the matter in writing to the Chairman before the Meeting.<br /><br />
<br /><br />
6.2<br /><br />
<br /><br />
The Meeting of the Partners shall be held as necessary, but not less<br /><br />
than once per year. The Meeting of the Partners will be held at the<br /><br />
registered address of the Company unless otherwise agreed by the<br /><br />
Partners.<br /><br />
<br /><br />
6.3<br /><br />
<br /><br />
The Meeting of the Partners shall be convened by the Directorate (as<br /><br />
defined in Article 7) which shall notify the Partners of the meeting<br /><br />
and the draft agenda not later than 8 days prior to the Meeting. Upon<br /><br />
receipt of the notice related to the Meeting, a Partner may, within<br /><br />
five days, introduce changes and/or amendment to the draft agenda of<br /><br />
the Meeting. In the beginning of the Meeting, Partners may vote on<br /><br />
individual issues to be included in the agenda.<br /><br />
<br /><br />
6.4<br /><br />
<br /><br />
Any person attending the Meeting of the Partners in any capacity is<br /><br />
bound by the same rules regarding maintenance of confidentiality and<br /><br />
disclosure of interest which bind the Partners.<br /><br />
<br /><br />
6.5<br /><br />
<br /><br />
The Directorate is responsible to convene immediately the Meeting of<br /><br />
the Partners if it is in the interest of the Company, provided that any<br /><br />
notice given under this article shall give the Partners sufficient time<br /><br />
to travel to such meeting.<br /><br />
<br /><br />
6.6<br /><br />
<br /><br />
The Directorate and a Partner whose shares amount to at least 5% of the<br /><br />
Charter Capital shall be entitled to demand an extraordinary meeting of<br /><br />
the Partners by specifying the purpose and grounds for such meeting and<br /><br />
addressing it to the other Partners.<br /><br />
167<br /><br />
<br /><br />
<PAGE><br /><br />
6.7<br /><br />
<br /><br />
A Meeting shall be entitled to decision-making only if it is attended<br /><br />
by the Partners holding more than 50% of the voting rights.<br /><br />
Notwithstanding the foregoing, the following matters are deemed to be<br /><br />
outside the routine operations of the Company and require the<br /><br />
attendance of all Partners that have the right to vote:<br /><br />
(i)<br /><br />
<br /><br />
amendments to the Charter;<br /><br />
<br /><br />
(ii)<br /><br />
<br /><br />
changes in the Charter Capital or shares therein;<br /><br />
<br /><br />
(iii)<br /><br />
<br /><br />
approval of a competent, properly certified auditor to conduct<br /><br />
auditing activities required by law;<br /><br />
<br /><br />
(iv)<br /><br />
<br /><br />
reorganisation, merger, liquidation or alienation of the<br /><br />
Company or substantially all of its assets;<br /><br />
<br /><br />
(v)<br /><br />
<br /><br />
appointment and release of Directors, the Chief Geologist and<br /><br />
the Chief Accountant:<br /><br />
<br /><br />
(vi)<br /><br />
<br /><br />
representing the Company in legal proceedings against<br /><br />
Directors.<br /><br />
<br /><br />
6.8<br /><br />
<br /><br />
Each Partner must cast all its votes as a block and may not divide its<br /><br />
votes on any matter.<br /><br />
<br /><br />
6.9<br /><br />
<br /><br />
The decisions of the Meeting of the Partners shall be adopted by a<br /><br />
simple majority vote.<br /><br />
<br /><br />
6.10<br /><br />
<br /><br />
The annual, as well as extraordinary Meeting of the Partners need not<br /><br />
be held if each Partner which has the right to vote, gives a written<br /><br />
consent with regard to the issue under consideration. If any Partner is<br /><br />
against such a procedure, an actual Meeting of the Partners shall be<br /><br />
held to discuss the matter.<br /><br />
<br /><br />
6.11<br /><br />
<br /><br />
The Meeting of the Partners shall be presided over by the Chairman of<br /><br />
the Meeting. The representative of NPL shall serve as Chairman of the<br /><br />
meeting in the first year and the representative of Georgian Oil shall<br /><br />
serve as Chairman of the meeting in the second year, thereafter<br /><br />
alternating on an annual basis.<br /><br />
<br /><br />
6.12<br /><br />
<br /><br />
After any and all Meetings of the Partners at which a decision is<br /><br />
adopted, minutes shall be recorded, signed by the Chairman of the<br /><br />
Meeting, and sent to all Partners.<br /><br />
The minutes shall indicate the place, date and time of the Meeting of<br /><br />
the Partners, the list of participating Partners and guests, the<br /><br />
agenda, the issues under consideration,<br /><br />
168<br /><br />
<br /><br />
<PAGE><br /><br />
the decisions of the Meeting of the Partners and any special opinion of<br /><br />
a Partner.<br /><br />
Partners shall confirm their approval or disapproval of the Minutes<br /><br />
within thirty days of receipt thereof.<br /><br />
169<br /><br />
<PAGE><br /><br />
ARTICLE 7<br /><br />
THE DIRECTORATE<br /><br />
7.1.<br /><br />
<br /><br />
The Company shall be managed and represented by the Directorate. The<br /><br />
Directorate shall be responsible for the managing and the supervising<br /><br />
the day-to-day operations of the Company according to the direction of<br /><br />
the Meeting of the Partners.<br /><br />
<br /><br />
7.2.<br /><br />
<br /><br />
The members of the Directorate shall consist of:<br /><br />
<br /><br />
7.3<br /><br />
<br /><br />
-<br /><br />
<br /><br />
A General Director<br /><br />
<br /><br />
-<br /><br />
<br /><br />
A Deputy General Director<br /><br />
<br /><br />
-<br /><br />
<br /><br />
A Technical Director<br /><br />
<br /><br />
-<br /><br />
<br /><br />
A Finance Director<br /><br />
<br /><br />
The General Director shall be authorised to carry out and be<br /><br />
responsible for the following, within the framework of the decisions of<br /><br />
the Partners, the provisions of this Charter and the applicable<br /><br />
legislation:<br /><br />
7.3.1<br /><br />
<br /><br />
Subject to any limitation in the Charter, to represent the<br /><br />
Company in its dealings with outside parties and to conclude,<br /><br />
without a power of attorney, contracts and other obligations<br /><br />
on behalf of the Company. The conclusion by the Company of any<br /><br />
<br /><br />
transaction or a set of related transactions outside the<br /><br />
procedures in the Cost Reimbursement Agreement shall require<br /><br />
the approval of the Partners. The aforementioned limit may be<br /><br />
changed by the decision of the Partners;<br /><br />
<br /><br />
7.4<br /><br />
<br /><br />
7.3.2<br /><br />
<br /><br />
To manage and dispose of the property of the Company in the<br /><br />
ordinary course of business;<br /><br />
<br /><br />
7.3.3<br /><br />
<br /><br />
To ensure the fulfilment of the policies and directives of the<br /><br />
Partners.<br /><br />
<br /><br />
7.3.4<br /><br />
<br /><br />
Implement the decisions of the Partners within the frame work<br /><br />
of this Charter and the applicable legislation.<br /><br />
<br /><br />
The Partners shall appoint a bookkeeper or accountant who, under the<br /><br />
supervision of<br /><br />
170<br /><br />
<br /><br />
<PAGE><br /><br />
the Directorate shall be responsible for developing financial reporting<br /><br />
and control systems in order to allow the Partners to monitor<br /><br />
efficiently the financial status and results of the Company. The<br /><br />
Directorate shall be responsible for ensuring proper record-keeping and<br /><br />
payment with respect to taxes, customs, charges, levies or fees imposed<br /><br />
by the authorities and for keeping abreast of all changes in official<br /><br />
legislation or regulations relevant to the Company's finances,<br /><br />
accounting, reporting and payment obligations.<br /><br />
7.5<br /><br />
<br /><br />
The Directorate shall ensure that unaudited quarterly financial<br /><br />
statements are prepared and submitted to the Partners for approval<br /><br />
within the time frame set by the Partners. In addition, the Directorate<br /><br />
shall ensure that audited annual financial statements are prepared<br /><br />
according to GAAP or IAS, consisting of balance sheet, income<br /><br />
statement, and cash flow statement, and are submitted to the Partners<br /><br />
for approval no later than ten weeks after the end of the fiscal year<br /><br />
covered.<br /><br />
<br /><br />
7.6<br /><br />
<br /><br />
Every year, on a day to be determined by the Meeting of the Partners,<br /><br />
the Directorate shall submit to the Meeting of the Partners the<br /><br />
proposed capital and operating budgets for the subsequent year to be<br /><br />
approved by the Partners.<br /><br />
<br /><br />
7.7<br /><br />
<br /><br />
Without prior consent of the Partners, the Directorate shall not be<br /><br />
entitled to conduct separately the same activities as those of the<br /><br />
Company or to take part in the activities of companies of the same<br /><br />
type.<br /><br />
<br /><br />
7.8<br /><br />
<br /><br />
The members of the Directorate shall conduct the activities of the<br /><br />
Company in good faith and in accordance with the governing law and this<br /><br />
Charter, as well as in accordance with the decisions of the Meeting of<br /><br />
the Partners.<br /><br />
<br /><br />
7.9<br /><br />
<br /><br />
The members of the Directorate shall comply with the rules and<br /><br />
regulations of the Company and shall conduct all activities which<br /><br />
require the prior consent of the Meeting of the Partners only upon<br /><br />
their agreement.<br /><br />
<br /><br />
7.10<br /><br />
<br /><br />
The Directorate shall provide the Partners information on the<br /><br />
day-to-day operations of the Company as requested.<br /><br />
<br /><br />
7.11<br /><br />
<br /><br />
The following actions of the Directorate require prior approval of all<br /><br />
Partners. Such approval shall be obtained by a Meeting of the Partners<br /><br />
or by written decision:<br /><br />
171<br /><br />
<br /><br />
<PAGE><br /><br />
7.11.1<br /><br />
<br /><br />
acquisition (including construction), or lease of tangible or<br /><br />
intangible capital property;<br /><br />
<br /><br />
7.11.2<br /><br />
<br /><br />
alienation and encumbrance of real estate and any other<br /><br />
immovable or movable;<br /><br />
<br /><br />
7.11.3<br /><br />
<br /><br />
participation in any other ventures, as well as creation and<br /><br />
liquidation of branches;<br /><br />
<br /><br />
7.11.4<br /><br />
<br /><br />
execution of license, supply or operating agreement, and all<br /><br />
other agreements with other enterprises, concerning the<br /><br />
provision of oil and gas and their products<br /><br />
<br /><br />
7.11.5<br /><br />
<br /><br />
annual budget, strategic and business plans, the planned<br /><br />
balance, and the profit and loss balance-sheet, as well as the<br /><br />
investment plan;<br /><br />
<br /><br />
7.11.6<br /><br />
<br /><br />
the establishment of long-term (more than 6 months) binding<br /><br />
relations with third parties or the adoption of financial<br /><br />
commitments (i.e. purchase contracts) which exceed monetary<br /><br />
limits set above or by the Meeting of the Partners;<br /><br />
<br /><br />
7.11.7<br /><br />
<br /><br />
liabilities arising from long-term (more than 6 months)<br /><br />
obligations;<br /><br />
<br /><br />
7.11.8<br /><br />
<br /><br />
obtain loans and credits or assumption of indebtedness which<br /><br />
exceed the amount to be determined by the Meeting of the<br /><br />
Partners;<br /><br />
<br /><br />
7.11.9<br /><br />
<br /><br />
guarantee loans and credits;<br /><br />
<br /><br />
7.11.10 any new investment activity;<br /><br />
7.11.11 disclosure of annual budgets, quarterly and annual financial<br /><br />
statements, or any other report to third parties, except as<br /><br />
required by proper government authorities;<br /><br />
7.11.12 selection of banks for local and foreign accounts and for<br /><br />
effecting any transaction;<br /><br />
172<br /><br />
<PAGE><br /><br />
7.11.13 issuance and annulment of "powers-of-attorney", with the<br /><br />
exception of routine specific authorisations;<br /><br />
7.11.14 instalment of internal controls and procedures; and<br /><br />
7.11.15 any other actions which go beyond normal operational<br /><br />
activities and of equal importance to the above in this<br /><br />
article 7.11, shall be determined by the Meeting of the<br /><br />
Partners.<br /><br />
7.12<br /><br />
<br /><br />
The Meeting of the Partners may adopt further rules and regulations of<br /><br />
the Company with a view to fully determine the rights, obligations,<br /><br />
scope of competence and authority of the Directorate.<br /><br />
<br /><br />
7.13<br /><br />
<br /><br />
The Directorate shall have custody of the Corporate Seal of the Company<br /><br />
and shall affix and attest the same to all instruments requiring it and<br /><br />
shall act so within the scope of authority as determined by the Meeting<br /><br />
of the Partners.<br /><br />
<br /><br />
7.14<br /><br />
<br /><br />
In case of violation of duties, the members of the Directorate shall be<br /><br />
held personally liable before the Partners for the losses incurred.<br /><br />
Individual members of the Directorate may prove that there was no<br /><br />
violation of duties on their part and be relieved of such<br /><br />
responsibility.<br /><br />
173<br /><br />
<br /><br />
<PAGE><br /><br />
ARTICLE 8<br /><br />
ANNUAL AND QUARTERLY RESULTS AND DISTRIBUTION OF PROFITS<br /><br />
8.1<br /><br />
<br /><br />
The unaudited quarterly and audited annual financial statements and<br /><br />
reports shall be prepared under the supervision of the Directorate for<br /><br />
submission to the Partners. Quarterly reports shall be submitted within<br /><br />
<br /><br />
the time frame set by the Meeting of the Partners and annual reports<br /><br />
not more than 10 weeks after the end of the fiscal year covered. The<br /><br />
quarterly and annual reports shall be approved by the Meeting of the<br /><br />
Partners.<br /><br />
8.2<br /><br />
<br /><br />
The Directorate shall be responsible for producing and maintaining<br /><br />
proper books, accounts and reports in compliance with Georgian law and<br /><br />
International Accounting Standards (IAS) or Generally Accepted<br /><br />
Accounting Principles (GAAP).<br /><br />
<br /><br />
8.3<br /><br />
<br /><br />
The books of the Company shall be annually audited by independent<br /><br />
auditors appointed by the Meeting of the Partners. All charges for the<br /><br />
services and expenses related to the above auditing shall be paid by<br /><br />
the Company.<br /><br />
174<br /><br />
<br /><br />
<PAGE><br /><br />
ARTICLE 9<br /><br />
TERMINATION OF THE COMPANY<br /><br />
9.1<br /><br />
<br /><br />
The Partners may agree by majority vote to liquidate the Company.<br /><br />
<br /><br />
9.2<br /><br />
<br /><br />
The Partners may agree by majority vote to reorganise the Company<br /><br />
(merger, amalgamation, division, transformation).<br /><br />
<br /><br />
9.3<br /><br />
<br /><br />
Liquidation of the Company pursuant to this Article shall be<br /><br />
implemented by the Directorate. Upon the request of one of the<br /><br />
Partners, liquidators may be appointed by the court in whose<br /><br />
jurisdiction the Company is located. The court shall be entitled to<br /><br />
appoint a liquidator who is not the Director.<br /><br />
<br /><br />
9.4<br /><br />
<br /><br />
The property of the liquidated company, after the repayment of debts,<br /><br />
shall be distributed between the Partners in proportion to their share<br /><br />
in the Company. The distribution shall be made only upon the expiration<br /><br />
of a one year period. This period shall begin from the date when the<br /><br />
creditors were informed about the liquidation by way of publication and<br /><br />
notices no less than three times.<br /><br />
The distribution of property may be effected by the court prior to the<br /><br />
expiration of a one year period, if the prevailing situation creates no<br /><br />
risk to creditors.<br /><br />
<br /><br />
9.5<br /><br />
<br /><br />
If a dispute arises between the Partners during the distribution of<br /><br />
property, the liquidator shall stop the distribution until the dispute<br /><br />
is legally settled.<br /><br />
175<br /><br />
<br /><br />
<PAGE><br /><br />
ARTICLE 10<br /><br />
SETTLEMENT OF DISPUTES<br /><br />
10.1<br /><br />
<br /><br />
Dispute between the Partners, arising out of or in connection with this<br /><br />
Charter or the interpretation hereof, shall be settled amicably by the<br /><br />
Partners themselves. If the dispute cannot be resolved in this manner<br /><br />
within 30 calendar days after first conferring, or such further period<br /><br />
as the Partners shall agree in writing, then the dispute shall be<br /><br />
finally settled by arbitration.<br /><br />
Arbitration shall take place at the Arbitration Institute of the<br /><br />
Stockholm Chamber of Commerce in accordance with the UNCITRAL rules of<br /><br />
arbitration. Each party to the dispute may appoint one arbitrator, and<br /><br />
the arbitrators so appointed shall agree on an additional arbitrator to<br /><br />
serve as Chairman. All arbitrators shall be selected from the list<br /><br />
maintained by the Institute. The language of the proceedings shall be<br /><br />
the official language of the location where the arbitration shall be<br /><br />
held, except that the proceedings shall be in English if the<br /><br />
arbitration is held in Stockholm.<br /><br />
<br /><br />
10.2<br /><br />
<br /><br />
All decisions of the Court of Arbitration shall be final and binding on<br /><br />
<br /><br />
the Partners.<br /><br />
10.3<br /><br />
<br /><br />
Neither the existence of any dispute, controversy or claim, nor the<br /><br />
fact that arbitration is pending hereunder, shall relieve any of the<br /><br />
Partners of its obligation under this Charter.<br /><br />
<br /><br />
10.4<br /><br />
<br /><br />
Without prejudice to this Article 10, the Partners shall have the right<br /><br />
at their discretion to initiate legal actions against the Directorate<br /><br />
in the Georgian courts or any such jurisdiction as it deems necessary.<br /><br />
176<br /><br />
<br /><br />
<PAGE><br /><br />
ARTICLE 11<br /><br />
FINAL PROVISIONS<br /><br />
11.1<br /><br />
<br /><br />
No amendment to this Charter shall be effected unless notarised and<br /><br />
duly registered in the court where the Company is registered.<br /><br />
<br /><br />
11.2<br /><br />
<br /><br />
If any provisions of this Charter shall be invalid, the validity of the<br /><br />
Charter as a whole shall not in any way be affected.<br /><br />
<br /><br />
11.3<br /><br />
<br /><br />
Any notice required to be given by the Company to any person ("the<br /><br />
recipient") under these articles may be given by means of hand delivery<br /><br />
or international courier post to the address or number of the recipient<br /><br />
notified to the Company by the recipient for such purpose (or, if not<br /><br />
so notified, then to the address or number of the recipient last known<br /><br />
to the Company). Any notice so given shall be deemed, in the absence of<br /><br />
any agreement to the contrary between the Company and the recipient, to<br /><br />
have been served at the time of delivery (or, if delivery is refused,<br /><br />
then when tendered) and delivery shall be deemed to have occurred no<br /><br />
later than 10 days after dispatch in the case of international courier<br /><br />
post and at the expiration of 24 hours after dispatch in the case of<br /><br />
hand delivery.<br /><br />
Delivery may be made by facsimile only if the Partners agree in writing<br /><br />
that they may receive notice by that method.<br /><br />
<br /><br />
11.4<br /><br />
<br /><br />
The communications addresses of the Partners for any notice sent under<br /><br />
this agreement are as follows:<br /><br />

Georgia<br /><br />

This Charter is being executed in Georgian and English and the two<br /><br />

is official and determinative for all business before the Georgian<br /><br />
government, or any subdivision thereof, and in the event of arbitration<br /><br />
or litigation in a Georgian forum. The English version shall prevail,<br /><br />
however, in the event of any arbitration or litigation conducted<br /><br />
outside of Georgia.<br /><br />

COST REIMBURSEMENT AGREEMENT<br /><br />
BETWEEN<br /><br />
NATIONAL PETROLEUM LIMITED<br /><br />

TBILISI<br /><br />

<br /><br />
<PAGE><br /><br />
COST REIMBURSEMENT AGREEMENT<br /><br />
This Cost Reimbursement Agreement (this "Agreement"), dated as of ____________,<br /><br />
2001, is entered into by National Petroleum Limited, a company formed under the<br /><br />
laws of Bermuda ("Contractor") and Ioris Valley Oil and Gas Limited, a Limited<br /><br />
Liability Company formed under the laws of Georgia (the "Operating Company");<br /><br />
with the Contractor and the Operating Company collectively called the "Parties"<br /><br />
and each of them individually called a "Party").<br /><br />
RECITALS<br /><br />
A.<br /><br />
<br /><br />
The Operating Company, on behalf of the Contractor, may incur certain<br /><br />
Costs and Expenses (as defined below) in connection with the<br /><br />
development of the Project (as defined below). The Contractor and the<br /><br />
Operating Company now wish to set forth their understanding with<br /><br />
respect to the Operating Company's entitlement to reimbursement of<br /><br />
Costs and Expenses incurred as Costs and Expenses in Petroleum<br /><br />
Operations (as defined below) under the Production Sharing Contract (as<br /><br />
defined below).<br /><br />
<br /><br />
B.<br /><br />
<br /><br />
It is not the intention of the Parties that the Operating Company shall<br /><br />
make either a profit or a loss as a consequence of the discharge of its<br /><br />
obligations under this Agreement<br /><br />
<br /><br />
1<br /><br />
<br /><br />
DEFINITIONS<br /><br />
The following words and terms shall have the following meanings:<br /><br />
<br /><br />
1.1<br /><br />
<br /><br />
"Authorisation for Expenditure" or "AFE" shall mean a document<br /><br />
submitted by the Operating Company showing the detailed breakdown of<br /><br />
Project activity (or other Petroleum Operations required by<br /><br />
Contractor), costs, manpower and timing, and duly approved.<br /><br />
<br /><br />
1.2<br /><br />
<br /><br />
"Business Day" means any day other than a Saturday, a Sunday, or a day<br /><br />
on which banks in Tbilisi, Geneva or London are authorised or required<br /><br />
by law to be closed.<br /><br />

<br /><br />
1.4<br /><br />
<br /><br />
"day" means a calendar day.<br /><br />
<br /><br />
1.5<br /><br />
<br /><br />
"dollars" or "$" means U.S. dollars.<br /><br />
<br /><br />
1.6<br /><br />
<br /><br />
"Petroleum Operations" shall have the same meaning ascribed thereto in<br /><br />
Article 1.63 of the Production Sharing Contract.<br /><br />
<br /><br />
1.7<br /><br />
<br /><br />
"Production Sharing Contract" shall have the same meaning ascribed<br /><br />
thereto in Article 1.21 of the Production Sharing Contract.<br /><br />
<br /><br />
1.8<br /><br />
<br /><br />
"Project" means the exploration appraisal, and the subsequent<br /><br />
development of any discovery, financing, construction, ownership,<br /><br />
maintenance, and operation of such facilities by or on behalf of<br /><br />
Contractor (or carried out by the Operating Company on its behalf)<br /><br />
under the Production Sharing Contract.<br /><br />
<br /><br />
1.9<br /><br />
<br /><br />
"Project Contracts" means any agreements to which the Operating Company<br /><br />

including:<br /><br />
(i)<br /><br />
<br /><br />

<br /><br />
(ii)<br /><br />

<br /><br />

construction, operation, maintenance of the Project,<br /><br />
1.10<br /><br />
<br /><br />
"Project Manager" means the individual assigned to supervise the<br /><br />

costs.<br /><br />

<br /><br />
<PAGE><br /><br />
2<br /><br />
<br /><br />
RIGHTS AND COSTS<br /><br />
<br /><br />
2.1<br /><br />
<br /><br />
APPROVAL OF COSTS & EXPENSES. All Costs and Expenses to be incurred by<br /><br />
the Operating Company for Petroleum Operations under the Production<br /><br />
Sharing Contract shall be shall be submitted as AFEs by the Operating<br /><br />
Company for approval by the Contractor. The Operating Company agrees<br /><br />
not to negotiate, contract, or incur any liability other than Costs and<br /><br />
Expenses for Petroleum Operations approved through an AFE by<br /><br />
Contractor.<br /><br />
<br /><br />
2.2<br /><br />
<br /><br />
TRANSFER OF RIGHTS Project Contracts entered into by the Operating<br /><br />
Company shall be executed by the Operating Company, and all data,<br /><br />
engineering and other information relating to the Project will be<br /><br />
developed for the benefit of Contractor, subject to Oil & Gas Law of<br /><br />
Georgia..<br /><br />
<br /><br />
2.3<br /><br />
<br /><br />
The Operating Company shall have no claim against Contractor in respect<br /><br />
of any service or product provided hereunder<br /><br />
<br /><br />
3.<br /><br />
<br /><br />
REIMBURSEMENT OF COSTS AND EXPENSES<br /><br />
REIMBURSEMENT GENERALLY To the extent Contractor approves the AFEs in<br /><br />
Article 2.1, Operating Company shall be entitled to reimbursement or to<br /><br />
have Contractor discharge the payment under any Project Contract or<br /><br />
other Petroleum Operations required by Contractor. It is understood<br /><br />
that the Operating Company shall neither gain or lose from providing<br /><br />
services or entering into Project Contracts as required by Contractor.<br /><br />
Contractor shall not be liable to pay, and Operating Company<br /><br />
indemnifies Contractor against, any expense, liability or Costs and<br /><br />
Expenses the Operating Company becomes liable for, that have not been<br /><br />
approved by Contractor in accordance with Article 2. Operating Company<br /><br />
covenants with Contractor that it will only undertake activities and<br /><br />
perform Petroleum Operations that have been approved by the<br /><br />
Coordination Committee.<br /><br />
<br /><br />
3.2<br /><br />
<br /><br />
PAYMENT OF REIMBURSEMENT Prior to the commencement of each phase of a<br /><br />
Project<br /><br />
185<br /><br />
<br /><br />
<PAGE><br /><br />
(or other Petroleum Operations required by Contractor) and following<br /><br />
the approval of the AFE, Contractor shall advance sufficient funds to<br /><br />
the Operating Company, up to the amount specified in the AFE, for the<br /><br />
Operating Company to implement the Project under the supervision of the<br /><br />
Project Manager. The Contractor may elect to discharge some or all of<br /><br />
the payments itself.<br /><br />
Should it appear that the Project cost is likely to exceed the AFE and<br /><br />
the sum advanced, the Project Manager shall prepare and submit a<br /><br />
supplementary AFE explaining the reasons for the cost increase and<br /><br />
<br /><br />
detailing the additional costs and, if necessary, timing changes.<br /><br />
Subject to approval of the supplementary AFE, the Contractor will<br /><br />
advance sufficient funds to the Operating Company for it to continue<br /><br />
with the Project.<br /><br />
At the completion (or at such other time as Contractor may require) of<br /><br />
each phase of a Project or other Petroleum Operations required by<br /><br />
Contractor, the Operating Company shall submit details of expenditure<br /><br />
to Contractor for Costs and Expenses incurred through each phase of the<br /><br />
Project (or for other Petroleum Operations required by Contractor) as<br /><br />
applicable to the AFE.<br /><br />
In the event that the expenditure is less than the sum advanced by the<br /><br />
Contractor, the Operating Company shall reimburse the difference to the<br /><br />
Contractor within 30 days of making the expenditure, or at such other<br /><br />
time as Contractor may require. The Contractor may opt to carry forward<br /><br />
such reimbursements.<br /><br />
186<br /><br />
<PAGE><br /><br />
4.<br /><br />
<br /><br />
RESOLUTION OF DISPUTES<br /><br />
<br /><br />
4.1<br /><br />
<br /><br />
ARBITRATION If any dispute or claim between Contractor and the<br /><br />
Operating Company (in this Section 4.1, each a "disputing party")<br /><br />
arising out of this Agreement or the rights and duties of the<br /><br />
Contractor and the Operating Company arising out of this Agreement (in<br /><br />
this Section 4.1, a "claim") has not been resolved by mutual agreement<br /><br />
on or before the 30th day following the first notice of the subject<br /><br />
matter of the claim to or from the disputing parties, then any<br /><br />
disputing party may refer the claim to arbitration under the following<br /><br />
provisions:<br /><br />
(i)<br /><br />
<br /><br />
To refer a claim to arbitration, a disputing party must<br /><br />
provide notice to the other disputing parties stating (a) a<br /><br />
general description of the claim and (b) that the claim is<br /><br />
being referred to arbitration under this Section 4.1. (the<br /><br />
"Notice").<br /><br />
<br /><br />
(ii)<br /><br />
<br /><br />
The disputing parties shall endeavour to agree promptly on a<br /><br />
panel of three arbitrators. If no agreement is reached within<br /><br />
30 days of receipt of the Notice either party may request the<br /><br />
panel of three arbitrators be appointed in accordance with the<br /><br />
rules of the International Chamber of Commerce.<br /><br />
<br /><br />
(iii)<br /><br />
<br /><br />
The arbitration shall be conducted in London or such other<br /><br />
place as the disputing parties may agree. The arbitrators<br /><br />
shall set the date, the time, and the place of the hearing,<br /><br />
which must commence on or before the 30th day following the<br /><br />
designation of the third arbitrator. The hearing may be<br /><br />
adjourned to later times and dates as the arbitrators<br /><br />
determine. The arbitration shall be conducted under the rules<br /><br />
of the International Chamber of Commerce not inconsistent with<br /><br />
the provisions of this Agreement. The arbitrators shall<br /><br />
endeavour to notify any disputing parties not present of any<br /><br />
adjournment to other dates or places; however, the proceedings<br /><br />
may continue in the absence of any disputing party that has<br /><br />
received notice of the date, the time, and the place of the<br /><br />
initial session of the hearing. All hearings shall be<br /><br />
conducted in English.<br /><br />
<br /><br />
(iv)<br /><br />
<br /><br />
The arbitrators shall endeavour to render their decision on or<br /><br />
before the 30th day following the last session of the hearing.<br /><br />
If the position of one or more disputing parties prevails,<br /><br />
then the other disputing party or parties shall pay all fees<br /><br />
and expenses of the arbitrators and the prevailing disputing<br /><br />
party in the arbitration. Each disputing party against which<br /><br />
the decision assesses a<br /><br />
187<br /><br />
<br /><br />
<PAGE><br /><br />
monetary obligation shall pay that obligation on or before the<br /><br />
<br /><br />
30th day following the decision or such other date as the<br /><br />
decision may provide.<br /><br />
<br /><br />
4.2<br /><br />
<br /><br />
(v)<br /><br />
<br /><br />
The decisions of the arbitrators are final and binding on all<br /><br />
disputing parties and are not subject to appeal. Without<br /><br />
limiting the provisions of Section 4.2, the decisions of the<br /><br />
arbitrators may be enforced in any court of competent<br /><br />
jurisdiction, and the disputing parties authorise any such<br /><br />
court to enter judgement on the arbitrators' decisions.<br /><br />
<br /><br />
(vi)<br /><br />
<br /><br />
Each Party agrees that arbitration under this Section 4.1 is<br /><br />
the exclusive method for resolving any claim and that it will<br /><br />
not commence any action or proceeding based on a claim, except<br /><br />
to reinforce arbitrators' decisions as provided in section<br /><br />
4.1(v) or to compel the other Party to participate in<br /><br />
arbitration under this section 4.1.<br /><br />
<br /><br />
JURISDICTION<br /><br />
(i)<br /><br />
<br /><br />
This Section 4.2 does not affect the limitations set forth in<br /><br />
Section 4.1 on commencing judicial proceedings, but may be<br /><br />
used to enforce arbitrators' decisions, to compel Parties to<br /><br />
participate in arbitration, or to compel Parties that have<br /><br />
brought judicial proceedings other than in compliance with<br /><br />
this Article 4 to dismiss those proceedings.<br /><br />
<br /><br />
(ii)<br /><br />
<br /><br />
Any action arising out of this Agreement or the rights and<br /><br />
duties of the Parties arising out of this Agreement may be<br /><br />
brought, if at all, only in the courts of England and not in<br /><br />
any other jurisdiction, court or tribunal.<br /><br />
<br /><br />
(iii)<br /><br />
<br /><br />
Each Party submits itself and its property to the personal<br /><br />
jurisdiction of the English courts in any such action. In this<br /><br />
connection, each Party waives any objection that now or in the<br /><br />
future it may have to the venue of any such action<br /><br />
188<br /><br />
<br /><br />
<PAGE><br /><br />
and any right to assert that the court is inconvenient, and<br /><br />
agrees not to raise any such objection or assertion. A copy of<br /><br />
this Agreement may serve as evidence of this waiver.<br /><br />

affected.<br /><br />
<br /><br />
5.7<br /><br />
<br /><br />
WAIVERS Any waiver, express or implied, by any of the Parties of any<br /><br />
right under this Agreement or of any breach by another Party shall not<br /><br />
constitute or be deemed as a waiver of any other right or any other<br /><br />
breach, whether of a similar or dissimilar nature to the right or<br /><br />
breach being waived. A waiver of a Party's rights under this Agreement<br /><br />
shall be effective only if that Party agrees.<br /><br />
<br /><br />

<br /><br />
LANGUAGE This Agreement has been drafted in English and Georgian; the<br /><br />
English version shall prevail over any translations.<br /><br />

NO THIRD PARTY BENEFICIARIES This Agreement is solely for the benefit<br /><br />

and this Agreement shall not otherwise be deemed to confer upon or give<br /><br />
to any other third party any remedy, claim, liability, reimbursement,<br /><br />

5.10<br /><br />
<br /><br />

invalid or unenforceable under the applicable law of any jurisdiction,<br /><br />
the remaining provisions shall not be affected in that jurisdiction,<br /><br />
and any such invalidity or unenforceability shall not invalidate or<br /><br />
render unenforceable that provision in any other jurisdiction. In that<br /><br />
event, the Parties agree that the provisions of this Agreement shall be<br /><br />
modified and reformed so as to effect the original intent of the<br /><br />
Parties as closely as possible with respect to those provisions that<br /><br />
were held to be invalid or unenforceable.<br /><br />

5.11<br /><br />

COUNTERPARTS This Agreement may be executed in two or more<br /><br />
